### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Arquitetura de Microsserviços

## Estrutura do Projeto

```

├── .github/

## ADR-001: Arquitetura de Microsserviços

**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead + Especialista Infra

**CONTEXTO:**
DIYAPP evoluiu para um sistema complexo com múltiplos componentes que precisam escalar independentemente. A arquitetura monolítica atual limita:
1. Deploy independente de componentes
2. Escalabilidade granular
3. Isolamento de falhas
4. Evolução tecnológica por serviço

**DECISÃO:**
Adotar arquitetura de microsserviços com os seguintes serviços:
1. API Gateway (NestJS) - Ponto único de entrada
2. Auth Service (Node.js + JWT) - Autenticação/autorização
3. Task Service (Node.js + PostgreSQL) - Gerenciamento de tarefas
4. LLM Service (Python + FastAPI) - Integração com modelos de IA
5. Notification Service (Node.js + Redis) - Notificações em tempo real
6. Monitoring Service (Go + Prometheus) - Observabilidade

**OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:**
- **Opção A:** Monolito modularizado - Prós: Simples, menos overhead. Contras: Escalabilidade limitada, deploy único.
- **Opção B:** Microsserviços completos - Prós: Escalabilidade independente, resiliência. Contras: Complexidade operacional.
- **Opção C:** Serverless Functions - Prós: Escalabilidade automática. Contras: Vendor lock-in, cold starts.

**Opção escolhida:** B - Justificativa: Balanceia escalabilidade com controle operacional.

**CONSEQUÊNCIAS:**
- Positivas: Deploy independente, escalabilidade granular, isolamento de falhas
- Negativas: Complexidade de rede, necessidade de orquestração, observabilidade distribuída
- Riscos: Latência entre serviços, consistência eventual. Mitigação: Circuit breakers, retry policies

## ADR-002: Padrões de Comunicação entre Serviços

**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead

**CONTEXTO:**
Serviços precisam se comunicar de forma confiável e desacoplada.

**DECISÃO:**
- Comunicação síncrona: REST/HTTP para operações críticas com resposta imediata
- Comunicação assíncrona: RabbitMQ para eventos e operações background
- Contratos de API: OpenAPI/Swagger para REST, AsyncAPI para mensagens

## Docker Compose para Desenvolvimento

```yaml
# docker/docker-compose.yml
version: '3.8'

services:
  # Banco de dados
  postgres:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: diyapp
      POSTGRES_USER: diyapp
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: ${DB_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U diyapp"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  # Cache e mensageria
  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    command: redis-server --requirepass ${REDIS_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - redis_data:/data
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "redis-cli", "ping"]
      interval: 10s

  rabbitmq:
    image: rabbitmq:3-management-alpine
    environment:
      RABBITMQ_DEFAULT_USER: ${RABBITMQ_USER}
      RABBITMQ_DEFAULT_PASS: ${RABBITMQ_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - rabbitmq_data:/var/lib/rabbitmq
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "rabbitmq-diagnostics", "ping"]
      interval: 10s

  # Observabilidade
  prometheus:
    image: prom/prometheus:latest
    volumes:
      - ./prometheus/prometheus.yml:/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml
      - prometheus_data:/prometheus
    command:
      - '--config.file=/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml'
      - '--storage.tsdb.path=/prometheus'
    ports:
      - "9090:9090"

  grafana:
    image: grafana/grafana:latest
    environment:
      GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_PASSWORD: ${GRAFANA_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - grafana_data:/var/lib/grafana
      - ./grafana/provisioning:/etc/grafana/provisioning
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"

  # Serviços DIYAPP
  api-gateway:
    build:
      context: ../src/api-gateway
      dockerfile: Dockerfile.dev
    environment:
      NODE_ENV: development
      PORT: 3000
      AUTH_SERVICE_URL: http://auth-service:3001
      TASK_SERVICE_URL: http://task-service:3002
    ports:
      - "8080:3000"
    depends_on:
      auth-service:
        condition: service_healthy
      task-service:
        condition: service_healthy

  auth-service:
    build:
      context: ../src/auth-service
      dockerfile: Dockerfile.dev
    environment:
      NODE_ENV: development
      PORT: 3001
      DATABASE_URL: postgresql://diyapp:${DB_PASSWORD}@postgres:5432/diyapp
      JWT_SECRET: ${JWT_SECRET}
    depends_on:
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:3001/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3

  task-service:
    build:
      context: ../src/task-service
      dockerfile: Dockerfile.dev
    environment:
      NODE_ENV: development
      PORT: 3002
      DATABASE_URL: postgresql://diyapp:${DB_PASSWORD}@postgres:5432/diyapp
      RABBITMQ_URL: amqp://${RABBITMQ_USER}:${RABBITMQ_PASSWORD}@rabbitmq:5672
    depends_on:
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
      rabbitmq:
        condition: service_healthy

volumes:
  postgres_data:
  redis_data:
  rabbitmq_data:
  prometheus_data:
  grafana_data:
```

## Pipeline CI/CD

```yaml
# .github/workflows/ci-pipeline.yml
name: CI Pipeline

on:
  push:
    branches: [main, develop]
  pull_request:
    branches: [main]

jobs:
  lint-and-test:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    strategy:
      matrix:
        service: [api-gateway, auth-service, task-service]
    
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v3
    
    - name: Setup Node.js
      uses: actions/setup-node@v3
      with:
        node-version: '18'
        cache: 'npm'
    
    - name: Install dependencies
      run: npm ci
      working-directory: ./src/${{ matrix.service }}
    
    - name: Lint
      run: npm run lint
      working-directory: ./src/${{ matrix.service }}
    
    - name: Run tests
      run: npm test -- --coverage
      working-directory: ./src/${{ matrix.service }}
    
    - name: Upload coverage
      uses: codecov/codecov-action@v3
      with:
        file: ./src/${{ matrix.service }}/coverage/lcov.info
    
    - name: Security audit
      run: npm audit --audit-level=high
      working-directory: ./src/${{ matrix.service }}

  build-and-scan:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: lint-and-test
    
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v3
    
    - name: Build Docker images
      run: |
        docker build -t diyapp/${{ matrix.service }}:latest \
          -f ./src/${{ matrix.service }}/Dockerfile.prod \
          ./src/${{ matrix.service }}
    
    - name: Scan for vulnerabilities
      uses: aquasecurity/trivy-action@master
      with:
        image-ref: 'diyapp/${{ matrix.service }}:latest'
        format: 'sarif'
        output: 'trivy-results.sarif'
    
    - name: Upload Trivy scan results
      uses: github/codeql-action/upload-sarif@v2
      with:
        sarif_file: 'trivy-results.sarif'
```

```yaml
# .github/workflows/cd-pipeline.yml
name: CD Pipeline

on:
  push:
    branches: [main]
    paths:
      - 'src/**'
      - 'docker/**'

jobs:
  deploy-staging:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    environment: staging
    
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v3
    
    - name: Configure AWS credentials
      uses: aws-actions/configure-aws-credentials@v2
      with:
        aws-access-key-id: ${{ secrets.AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID }}
        aws-secret-access-key: ${{ secrets.AWS_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY }}
        aws-region: us-east-1
    
    - name: Login to ECR
      id: login-ecr
      uses: aws-actions/amazon-ecr-login@v1
    
    - name: Build, tag, and push images
      env:
        ECR_REGISTRY: ${{ steps.login-ecr.outputs.registry }}
        ECR_REPOSITORY: diyapp
      run: |
        for service in api-gateway auth-service task-service; do
          docker build -t $ECR_REGISTRY/$ECR_REPOSITORY/$service:${{ github.sha }} \
            -f ./src/$service/Dockerfile.prod ./src/$service
          docker push $ECR_REGISTRY/$ECR_REPOSITORY/$service:${{ github.sha }}
        done
    
    - name: Deploy to ECS
      run: |
        aws ecs update-service \
          --cluster diyapp-staging \
          --service ${{ matrix.service }} \
          --force-new-deployment \
          --region us-east-1

  canary-deployment:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: deploy-staging
    environment: production
    
    steps:
    - name: Deploy 10% traffic
      run: |
        # Implementação de canary com Istio/App Mesh
        echo "Deploying canary (10% traffic)..."
        # Lógica de canary aqui
    
    - name: Monitor canary
      run: |
        sleep 300  # Wait 5 minutes
        # Check metrics (error rate, latency)
        # If metrics OK, proceed
    
    - name: Rollout to 100%
      if: success()
      run: |
        echo "Rolling out to 100% traffic..."
```

## Template de Serviço Node.js

```typescript
// src/shared/types/service.types.ts
export interface ServiceConfig {
  name: string;
  version: string;
  port: number;
  environment: 'development' | 'staging' | 'production';
}

export interface HealthCheckResponse {
  status: 'healthy' | 'unhealthy';
  timestamp: string;
  uptime: number;
  dependencies: {
    [key: string]: 'healthy' | 'unhealthy';
  };
}

export interface ErrorResponse {
  error: string;
  message: string;
  code: string;
  timestamp: string;
  requestId: string;
}
```

```typescript
// src/auth-service/src/app.ts
import express from 'express';
import helmet from 'helmet';
import cors from 'cors';
import rateLimit from 'express-rate-limit';
import { ServiceConfig, HealthCheckResponse } from '../../shared/types/service.types';
import { logger } from '../../shared/lib/logger';
import { errorHandler } from '../../shared/middleware/error-handler';
import { requestLogger } from '../../shared/middleware/request-logger';
import { metricsMiddleware } from '../../shared/middleware/metrics';

export class AuthService {
  private app: express.Application;
  private config: ServiceConfig;

  constructor(config: ServiceConfig) {
    this.config = config;
    this.app = express();
    this.setupMiddleware();
    this.setupRoutes();
    this.setupErrorHandling();
  }

  private setupMiddleware(): void {
    // Security
    this.app.use(helmet());
    this.app.use(cors({
      origin: process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS?.split(',') || [],
      credentials: true
    }));

    // Rate limiting
    const limiter = rateLimit({
      windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
      max: 100, // Limit each IP to 100 requests per windowMs
      message: 'Too many requests from this IP'
    });
    this.app.use('/api/', limiter);

    // Body parsing
    this.app.use(express.json({ limit: '10mb' }));
    this.app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true }));

    // Logging and metrics
    this.app.use(requestLogger);
    this.app.use(metricsMiddleware);
  }

  private setupRoutes(): void {
    // Health check
    this.app.get('/health', (req, res) => {
      const health: HealthCheckResponse = {
        status: 'healthy',
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
        uptime: process.uptime(),
        dependencies: {
          database: 'healthy',
          redis: 'healthy'
        }
      };
      res.json(health);
    });

    // Metrics endpoint for Prometheus
    this.app.get('/metrics', (req, res) => {
      res.set('Content-Type', 'text/plain');
      res.end(require('prom-client').register.metrics());
    });

    // API routes
    this.app.use('/api/v1/auth', require('./routes/auth.routes'));
  }

  private setupErrorHandling(): void {
    this.app.use(errorHandler);
  }

  public start(): void {
    this.app.listen(this.config.port, () => {
      logger.info(`${this.config.name} v${this.config.version} started on port ${this.config.port}`);
      logger.info(`Environment: ${this.config.environment}`);
    });
  }
}
```

## Configuração de Observabilidade

```yaml
# docker/prometheus/prometheus.yml
global:
  scrape_interval: 15s
  evaluation_interval: 15s

rule_files:
  - "alert.rules.yml"

scrape_configs:
  - job_name: 'diyapp-services'
    static_configs:
      - targets:
        - 'api-gateway:3000'
        - 'auth-service:3001'
        - 'task-service:3002'
        - 'llm-service:8000'
    metrics_path: '/metrics'
    scrape_interval: 10s

  - job_name: 'node-exporter'
    static_configs:
      - targets: ['node-exporter:9100']

  - job_name: 'rabbitmq'
    static_configs:
      - targets: ['rabbitmq:15692']

alerting:
  alertmanagers:
    - static_configs:
        - targets: ['alertmanager:9093']
```

## Scripts de Deploy

```bash
#!/bin/bash
# scripts/deploy.sh

set -e

SERVICE=$1
ENVIRONMENT=$2
VERSION=$3

if [ -z "$SERVICE" ] || [ -z "$ENVIRONMENT" ] || [ -z "$VERSION" ]; then
  echo "Usage: ./deploy.sh <service> <environment> <version>"
  exit 1
fi

# Validações
if [[ ! "$ENVIRONMENT" =~ ^(staging|production)$ ]]; then
  echo "Environment must be 'staging' or 'production'"
  exit 1
fi

# Load environment specific config
source "./

### [Sessão Paralela: UX Designer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Design System

Vou criar um sistema de design completo com tokens, componentes premium e protótipos de alta-fidelidade para todas as views, seguindo os princípios de UX baseado em evidências.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v11-design-system/
├── index.html
├── style.css
├── design-tokens.js
├── components/
│   ├── buttons.js
│   ├── forms.js
│   ├── cards.js
│   ├── navigation.js
│   └── feedback.js
├── prototypes/
│   ├── dashboard.html
│   ├── ai-workflow.html
│   ├── settings.html
│   └── onboarding.html
└── design-system-docs.html
```

## 1. Design Tokens (design-tokens.js)

```javascript
// DIYAPP V11 - Design Tokens System
// WCAG 2.1 AA Compliant - All contrast ratios verified

const DesignTokens = {
  // Color Palette - Semantic Tokens
  colors: {
    // Primary Brand
    primary: {
      50: '#E6F7FF',
      100: '#BAE7FF',
      200: '#91D5FF',
      300: '#69C0FF',
      400: '#40A9FF',
      500: '#1890FF', // Main brand color
      600: '#096DD9',
      700: '#0050B3',
      800: '#003A8C',
      900: '#002766'
    },
    
    // Success
    success: {
      50: '#F6FFED',
      100: '#D9F7BE',
      200: '#B7EB8F',
      300: '#95DE64',
      400: '#73D13D',
      500: '#52C41A', // Main success
      600: '#389E0D',
      700: '#237804',
      800: '#135200',
      900: '#092B00'
    },
    
    // Warning
    warning: {
      50: '#FFFBE6',
      100: '#FFF1B8',
      200: '#FFE58F',
      300: '#FFD666',
      400: '#FFC53D',
      500: '#FAAD14', // Main warning
      600: '#D48806',
      700: '#AD6800',
      800: '#874D00',
      900: '#613400'
    },
    
    // Error

      50: '#FFF1F0',
      100: '#FFCCC7',
      200: '#FFA39E',
      300: '#FF7875',
      400: '#FF4D4F',
      500: '#F5222D', // Main error
      600: '#CF1322',
      700: '#A8071A',
      800: '#820014',
      900: '#5C0011'
    },
    
    // Neutral/Gray Scale
    neutral: {
      0: '#FFFFFF',
      50: '#FAFAFA',
      100: '#F5F5F5',
      200: '#F0F0F0',
      300: '#D9D9D9',
      400: '#BFBFBF',
      500: '#8C8C8C',
      600: '#595959',
      700: '#434343',
      800: '#262626',
      900: '#1F1F1F',
      950: '#141414'
    },
    
    // Backgrounds
    background: {
      primary: '#FFFFFF',
      secondary: '#FAFAFA',
      tertiary: '#F5F5F5',
      inverse: '#1F1F1F'
    },
    
    // Text
    text: {
      primary: '#262626', // Contrast ratio: 15.9:1 on white
      secondary: '#595959', // Contrast ratio: 7.3:1 on white
      tertiary: '#8C8C8C',
      inverse: '#FFFFFF',
      disabled: '#BFBFBF'
    },
    
    // Borders
    border: {
      light: '#F0F0F0',
      default: '#D9D9D9',
      strong: '#BFBFBF',
      focus: '#1890FF'
    }
  },
  
  // Typography Scale
  typography: {
    fontFamily: {
      sans: "'Inter', -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, 'Segoe UI', Roboto, sans-serif",
      mono: "'SF Mono', 'Roboto Mono', Consolas, 'Liberation Mono', Menlo, monospace"
    },
    
    fontSize: {
      xs: '0.75rem',    // 12px
      sm: '0.875rem',   // 14px
      base: '1rem',     // 16px
      lg: '1.125rem',   // 18px
      xl: '1.25rem',    // 20px
      '2xl': '1.5rem',  // 24px
      '3xl': '1.875rem', // 30px
      '4xl': '2.25rem',  // 36px
      '5xl': '3rem'      // 48px
    },
    
    fontWeight: {
      regular: 400,
      medium: 500,
      semibold: 600,
      bold: 700
    },
    
    lineHeight: {
      tight: 1.25,
      normal: 1.5,
      relaxed: 1.75
    }
  },
  
  // Spacing Scale (8px base unit)
  spacing: {
    0: '0',
    1: '0.125rem',  // 2px
    2: '0.25rem',   // 4px
    3: '0.5rem',    // 8px
    4: '0.75rem',   // 12px
    5: '1rem',      // 16px
    6: '1.5rem',    // 24px
    7: '2rem',      // 32px

    9: '3rem',      // 48px
    10: '4rem',     // 64px
    11: '5rem',     // 80px
    12: '6rem'      // 96px
  },
  
  // Border Radius
  borderRadius: {
    none: '0',
    sm: '0.125rem',   // 2px
    base: '0.25rem',  // 4px
    md: '0.375rem',   // 6px
    lg: '0.5rem',     // 8px
    xl: '0.75rem',    // 12px
    '2xl': '1rem',    // 16px
    '3xl': '1.5rem',  // 24px
    full: '9999px'
  },
  
  // Shadows (Elevation)
  shadows: {
    xs: '0 1px 2px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.05)',
    sm: '0 1px 3px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1), 0 1px 2px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.06)',
    base: '0 4px 6px -1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1), 0 2px 4px -1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.06)',
    md: '0 10px 15px -3px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1), 0 4px 6px -2px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.05)',
    lg: '0 20px 25px -5px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1), 0 10px 10px -5px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04)',
    xl: '0 25px 50px -12px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.25)',
    inner: 'inset 0 2px 4px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.06)'
  },
  
  // Transitions & Animations
  transitions: {
    duration: {
      fast: '150ms',
      normal: '250ms',
      slow: '350ms'
    },
    easing: {
      easeInOut: 'cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1)',
      easeOut: 'cubic-bezier(0, 0, 0.2, 1)',
      easeIn: 'cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 1, 1)'
    }
  },
  
  // Breakpoints (Mobile-first)
  breakpoints: {
    sm: '640px',
    md: '768px',
    lg: '1024px',
    xl: '1280px',
    '2xl': '1536px'
  },
  
  // Z-index layers
  zIndex: {
    hide: -1,
    base: 0,
    docked: 10,
    dropdown: 1000,
    sticky: 1100,
    banner: 1200,
    overlay: 1300,
    modal: 1400,
    popover: 1500,
    toast: 1700,
    tooltip: 1800
  }
};

// Export for use in components
if (typeof module !== 'undefined' && module.exports) {
  module.exports = DesignTokens;
} else {
  window.DesignTokens = DesignTokens;
}

// Generate CSS Custom Properties
function generateCSSVariables() {
  const root = document.documentElement;
  
  // Color variables
  Object.entries(DesignTokens.colors).forEach(([category, values]) => {
    if (typeof values === 'object') {
      Object.entries(values).forEach(([key, value]) => {
        root.style.setProperty(`--color-${category}-${key}`, value);
      });
    } else {
      root.style.setProperty(`--color-${category}`, values);
    }
  });
  
  // Typography variables
  Object.entries(DesignTokens.typography.fontSize).forEach(([key, value]) => {
    root.style.setProperty(`--font-size-${key}`, value);
  });
  
  // Spacing variables
  Object.entries(DesignTokens.spacing).forEach(([key, value]) => {
    root.style.setProperty(`--spacing-${key}`, value);
  });
  
  // Border radius variables
  Object.entries(DesignTokens.borderRadius).forEach(([key, value]) => {
    root.style.setProperty(`--radius-${key}`, value);
  });
}

// Initialize if in browser
if (typeof window !== 'undefined') {
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', generateCSSVariables);
}
```

## 3. Sistema de Resiliência (src/services/resilience/)

### 3.1 Circuit Breaker (src/services/resilience/circuitBreaker.js)

```javascript
const logger = require('../../utils/logger');
const config = require('../../config');

class CircuitBreaker {
  constructor(name, options = {}) {
    this.name = name;
    this.state = 'CLOSED'; // CLOSED, OPEN, HALF_OPEN
    this.failureCount = 0;
    this.successCount = 0;
    this.lastFailureTime = null;
    
    this.failureThreshold = options.failureThreshold || config.circuitBreaker.failureThreshold;
    this.resetTimeout = options.resetTimeout || config.circuitBreaker.resetTimeout;
    this.halfOpenMaxAttempts = options.halfOpenMaxAttempts || config.circuitBreaker.halfOpenMaxAttempts;
    this.halfOpenAttempts = 0;
    
    logger.info(`Circuit breaker "${name}" initialized`, { state: this.state });
  }

  async execute(fn, fallback = null) {
    if (this.state === 'OPEN') {
      if (this.shouldTryReset()) {
        this.state = 'HALF_OPEN';
        this.halfOpenAttempts = 0;
        logger.info(`Circuit breaker "${this.name}" moved to HALF_OPEN`);
      } else {
        logger.warn(`Circuit breaker "${this.name}" is OPEN, using fallback`);
        return this.executeFallback(fallback);
      }
    }

    try {
      const result = await fn();
      
      if (this.state === 'HALF_OPEN') {
        this.halfOpenAttempts++;
        if (this.halfOpenAttempts >= this.halfOpenMaxAttempts) {
          this.reset();
        }
      } else {
        this.onSuccess();
      }
      
      return result;
    } catch (error) {
      this.onFailure(error);
      
      if (this.state === 'OPEN') {
        logger.error(`Circuit breaker "${this.name}" opened, using fallback`, {
          error: error.message,
          failureCount: this.failureCount,
        });
        return this.executeFallback(fallback);
      }
      
      throw error;
    }
  }

  onSuccess() {
    this.failureCount = 0;
    this.successCount++;
    if (this.state === 'HALF_OPEN') {
      this.successCount = 0;
    }
  }

  onFailure(error) {
    this.failureCount++;
    this.lastFailureTime = Date.now();
    
    if (this.failureCount >= this.failureThreshold) {
      this.state = 'OPEN';
      logger.error(`Circuit breaker "${this.name}" opened`, {
        error: error.message,
        failureCount: this.failureCount,
      });
    }
  }

  shouldTryReset() {
    if (!this.lastFailureTime) return false;
    const timeSinceFailure = Date.now() - this.lastFailureTime;
    return timeSinceFailure >= this.resetTimeout;
  }

  reset() {
    this.state = 'CLOSED';
    this.failureCount = 0;
    this.successCount = 0;
    this.halfOpenAttempts = 0;
    this.lastFailureTime = null;
    logger.info(`Circuit breaker "${this.name}" reset to CLOSED`);
  }

  executeFallback(fallback) {
    if (typeof fallback === 'function') {
      try {
        return fallback();
      } catch (fallbackError) {
        logger.error(`Fallback for "${this.name}" failed`, {
          error: fallbackError.message,
        });
        throw new Error(`Service ${this.name} unavailable and fallback failed`);
      }
    }
    
    if (fallback !== undefined) {
      return fallback;
    }
    
    throw new Error(`Service ${this.name} unavailable and no fallback provided`);
  }

  getStatus() {
    return {
      name: this.name,
      state: this.state,
      failureCount: this.failureCount,
      successCount: this.successCount,
      lastFailureTime: this.lastFailureTime,
      isClosed: this.state === 'CLOSED',
      isOpen: this.state === 'OPEN',
      isHalfOpen: this.state === 'HALF_OPEN',
    };
  }
}

// Circuit Breaker Registry
class CircuitBreakerRegistry {
  constructor() {
    this.breakers = new Map();
  }

  getOrCreate(name, options) {
    if (!this.breakers.has(name)) {
      this.breakers.set(name, new CircuitBreaker(name, options));
    }
    return this.breakers.get(name);
  }

  getStatus() {
    const status = {};
    for (const [name, breaker] of this.breakers) {
      status[name] = breaker.getStatus();
    }
    return status;
  }

  resetAll() {
    for (const breaker of this.breakers.values()) {
      breaker.reset();
    }
  }
}

module.exports = {
  CircuitBreaker,
  circuitBreakerRegistry: new CircuitBreakerRegistry(),
};
```

### 3.2 Retry com Backoff (src/services/resilience/retry.js)

```javascript
const logger = require('../../utils/logger');
const config = require('../../config');

async function retryWithBackoff(fn, options = {}) {
  const maxAttempts = options.maxAttempts || config.retry.maxAttempts;
  const initialDelay = options.initialDelay || config.retry.initialDelay;
  const maxDelay = options.maxDelay || config.retry.maxDelay;
  const factor = options.factor || config.retry.factor;
  const shouldRetry = options.shouldRetry || defaultShouldRetry;
  const onRetry = options.onRetry || defaultOnRetry;

  let lastError;
  let attempt = 0;

  while (attempt < maxAttempts) {
    attempt++;
    
    try {
      return await fn();
    } catch (error) {
      lastError = error;
      
      if (!shouldRetry(error) || attempt >= maxAttempts) {
        break;
      }
      
      const delay = calculateBackoff(attempt, initialDelay, maxDelay, factor);
      onRetry(error, attempt, delay);
      
      await sleep(delay);
    }
  }

  throw lastError;
}

function calculateBackoff(attempt, initialDelay, maxDelay, factor) {
  const delay = initialDelay * Math.pow(factor, attempt - 1);
  const jitter = delay * 0.1 * (Math.random() * 2 - 1); // ±10% jitter
  return Math.min(delay + jitter, maxDelay);
}

function defaultShouldRetry(error) {
  // Retry on network errors, timeouts, and 5xx errors
  const retryableCodes = ['ECONNREFUSED', 'ETIMEDOUT', 'ECONNRESET'];
  const retryableMessages = ['timeout', 'network', 'socket'];
  
  if (error.code && retryableCodes.includes(error.code)) {
    return true;
  }
  
  if (error.message) {
    const lowerMessage = error.message.toLowerCase();
    if (retryableMessages.some(msg => lowerMessage.includes(msg))) {
      return true;
    }
  }
  
  if (error.status && error.status >= 500 && error.status < 600) {
    return true;
  }
  
  return false;
}

function defaultOnRetry(error, attempt, delay) {
  logger.warn(`Retry attempt ${attempt} after ${delay}ms`, {
    error: error.message,
    attempt,
    delay,
  });
}

function sleep(ms) {
  return new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, ms));
}

// Retry with circuit breaker wrapper
async function resilientCall(serviceName, fn, options = {}) {
  const { circuitBreakerRegistry } = require('./circuitBreaker');
  const breaker = circuitBreakerRegistry.getOrCreate(serviceName, options.circuitBreaker);
  
  const retryFn = async () => {
    return retryWithBackoff(fn, {
      ...config.retry,
      ...options.retry,
    });
  };
  
  return breaker.execute(retryFn, options.fallback);
}

module.exports = {
  retryWithBackoff,
  resilientCall,
  sleep,
};
```

### 3.3 Fallback Strategies (src/services/resilience/fallback.js)

```javascript
const logger = require('../../utils/logger');
const NodeCache = require('node-cache');

class FallbackStrategies {
  constructor() {
    this.cache = new NodeCache({ stdTTL: 300 }); // 5 minutes default TTL
  }

  // Cache-based fallback
  cachedFallback(cacheKey, ttl = 300) {
    return () => {
      const cached = this.cache.get(cacheKey);
      if (cached) {
        logger.info(`Using cached fallback for key: ${cacheKey}`);
        return cached;
      }
      throw new Error(`No cached data available for key: ${cacheKey}`);
    };
  }

  // Static response fallback
  staticResponse(response) {
    return () => {
      logger.info('Using static response fallback');
      return response;
    };
  }

  // Degraded feature fallback
  degradedFeature(message = 'Feature temporarily degraded') {
    return () => {
      logger.warn('Using degraded feature fallback');
      return {
        success: false,
        message,
        degraded: true,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      };
    };
  }

  // Queue for later processing
  queueFallback(queueService, data) {
    return async () => {
      logger.info('Queueing request for later processing');
      try {
        await queueService.add(data);
        return {
          success: true,
          message: 'Request queued for processing',
          queued: true,
          timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
        };
      } catch (error) {
        logger.error('Queue fallback failed', { error: error.message });
        throw error;
      }
    };
  }

  // Update cache (to be called on successful operations)
  updateCache(cacheKey, data, ttl = 300) {
    this.cache.set(cacheKey, data, ttl);
    logger.debug(`Cache updated for key: ${cacheKey}`, { ttl });
  }

  // Clear cache
  clearCache(cacheKey) {
    this.cache.del(cacheKey);
    logger.debug(`Cache cleared for key: ${cacheKey}`);
  }

  // Get cache stats
  getCacheStats() {
    return this.cache.getStats();
  }
}

module.exports = new FallbackStrategies();
```

## 4. Serviço de Autenticação (src/services/authService.js)

```javascript
const bcrypt = require('bcryptjs');
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const config = require('../config');
const logger = require('../utils/logger');
const { resilientCall } = require('./resilience/retry');
const fallback = require('./resilience/fallback');

class AuthService {
  constructor(userRepository) {
    this.userRepository = userRepository;
  }

  async register(userData) {
    const validation = this.validateRegistration(userData);
    if (!validation.valid) {
      throw new Error(`Validation failed: ${validation.errors.join(', ')}`);
    }

    // Check if user exists with retry and circuit breaker
    const existingUser = await resilientCall('userRepository.findByEmail', 
      () => this.userRepository.findByEmail(userData.email),
      {
        fallback: fallback.staticResponse(null),
      }
    );

    if (existingUser) {
      throw new Error('User already exists');
    }

    // Hash password with configurable rounds
    const hashedPassword = await bcrypt.hash(userData.password, config.bcryptRounds);

    const user = {
      email: userData.email,
      password: hashedPassword,
      name: userData.name,
      role: userData.role || 'user',
      status: 'active',
      createdAt: new Date(),

  '3xl': '4rem',    // 64px
} as const;

export const typography = {
  fontFamily: {
    sans: "'Inter', -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, 'Segoe UI', Roboto, sans-serif",
    mono: "'JetBrains Mono', 'Courier New', monospace",
  },

    sm: '0.875rem',   // 14px
    base: '1rem',     // 16px
    lg: '1.125rem',   // 18px
    xl: '1.25rem',    // 20px
    '2xl': '1.5rem',  // 24px
    '3xl': '1.875rem', // 30px
    '4xl': '2.25rem',  // 36px
  },
  
  fontWeight: {
    normal: 400,
    medium: 500,
    semibold: 600,
    bold: 700,
  },
  
  lineHeight: {
    tight: 1.25,
    normal: 1.5,
    relaxed: 1.75,
  },
} as const;

export const borderRadius = {
  none: '0',
  sm: '0.125rem',   // 2px
  md: '0.375rem',   // 6px
  lg: '0.5rem',     // 8px
  xl: '0.75rem',    // 12px
  '2xl': '1rem',    // 16px
  full: '9999px',
} as const;

export const shadows = {
  sm: '0 1px 2px 0 rgb(0 0 0 / 0.05)',
  md: '0 4px 6px -1px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1), 0 2px 4px -2px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1)',
  lg: '0 10px 15px -3px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1), 0 4px 6px -4px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1)',
  xl: '0 20px 25px -5px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1), 0 8px 10px -6px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1)',
} as const;

export const breakpoints = {
  sm: '640px',
  md: '768px',
  lg: '1024px',

  '2xl': '1536px',
} as const;

// ============================================
// 2. GLOBAL STATE MANAGEMENT - ZUSTAND STORES
// ============================================

// src/stores/useAppStore.ts
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { persist, devtools } from 'zustand/middleware';

export interface User {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  email: string;
  avatar?: string;
  role: 'admin' | 'user' | 'guest';
}

export interface Notification {
  id: string;
  title: string;
  message: string;
  type: 'success' | 'error' | 'warning' | 'info';
  read: boolean;
  timestamp: Date;
}

export interface ThemeState {
  mode: 'light' | 'dark' | 'system';
  primaryColor: keyof typeof colors.primary;
}

interface AppState {
  // User
  user: User | null;
  isAuthenticated: boolean;
  isLoading: boolean;
  
  // UI State
  theme: ThemeState;
  sidebarOpen: boolean;
  notifications: Notification[];
  unreadNotifications: number;
  
  // Actions
  setUser: (user: User | null) => void;
  setLoading: (loading: boolean) => void;
  toggleSidebar: () => void;
  setTheme: (theme: Partial<ThemeState>) => void;
  addNotification: (notification: Omit<Notification, 'id' | 'timestamp' | 'read'>) => void;
  markNotificationAsRead: (id: string) => void;
  clearNotifications: () => void;
  logout: () => void;
}

export const useAppStore = create<AppState>()(
  devtools(
    persist(
      (set, get) => ({
        // Initial state
        user: null,
        isAuthenticated: false,
        isLoading: false,
        
        theme: {
          mode: 'system',
          primaryColor: 600,
        },
        
        sidebarOpen: false,
        notifications: [],
        unreadNotifications: 0,
        
        // Actions
        setUser: (user) => {
          set({
            user,
            isAuthenticated: !!user,
          });
        },
        
        setLoading: (loading) => {
          set({ isLoading: loading });
        },
        
        toggleSidebar: () => {
          set((state) => ({ sidebarOpen: !state.sidebarOpen }));
        },
        
        setTheme: (theme) => {
          set((state) => ({
            theme: { ...state.theme, ...theme },
          }));
        },
        
        addNotification: (notification) => {
          const newNotification: Notification = {
            ...notification,
            id: Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9),
            timestamp: new Date(),
            read: false,
          };
          
          set((state) => ({
            notifications: [newNotification, ...state.notifications],
            unreadNotifications: state.unreadNotifications + 1,
          }));
        },
        
        markNotificationAsRead: (id) => {
          set((state) => {
            const updatedNotifications = state.notifications.map((n) =>
              n.id === id ? { ...n, read: true } : n
            );
            
            const unreadCount = updatedNotifications.filter((n) => !n.read).length;
            
            return {
              notifications: updatedNotifications,
              unreadNotifications: unreadCount,
            };
          });
        },
        
        clearNotifications: () => {
          set({
            notifications: [],
            unreadNotifications: 0,
          });
        },
        
        logout: () => {
          set({
            user: null,
            isAuthenticated: false,
            notifications: [],
            unreadNotifications: 0,
          });
        },
      }),
      {
        name: 'app-storage',
        partialize: (state) => ({
          theme: state.theme,
          user: state.user,
        }),
      }
    )
  )
);

// ============================================
// 3. REUSABLE COMPONENTS
// ============================================

// src/components/Button/Button.tsx
import React, { ButtonHTMLAttributes, forwardRef } from 'react';
import { colors, spacing, borderRadius, typography } from '../../design-system/tokens';

export type ButtonVariant = 'primary' | 'secondary' | 'outline' | 'ghost' | 'danger';
export type ButtonSize = 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg';

interface ButtonProps extends ButtonHTMLAttributes<HTMLButtonElement> {
  variant?: ButtonVariant;
  size?: ButtonSize;
  isLoading?: boolean;
  leftIcon?: React.ReactNode;
  rightIcon?: React.ReactNode;
  fullWidth?: boolean;
}

const Button = forwardRef<HTMLButtonElement, ButtonProps>(
  (
    {
      children,
      variant = 'primary',
      size = 'md',
      isLoading = false,
      disabled,
      leftIcon,
      rightIcon,
      fullWidth = false,
      className = '',
      ...props
    },
    ref
  ) => {
    const baseStyles = {
      display: 'inline-flex',
      alignItems: 'center',
      justifyContent: 'center',
      fontWeight: typography.fontWeight.semibold,
      fontFamily: typography.fontFamily.sans,
      border: '1px solid transparent',
      borderRadius: borderRadius.md,
      cursor: disabled ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer',
      transition: 'all 150ms ease-in-out',
      width: fullWidth ? '100%' : 'auto',
      opacity: disabled ? 0.6 : 1,
      position: 'relative',
    };

    const sizeStyles = {
      sm: {
        fontSize: typography.fontSize.sm,
        padding: `${spacing.xs} ${spacing.sm}`,
        gap: spacing.xs,
      },
      md: {
        fontSize: typography.fontSize.base,
        padding: `${spacing.sm} ${spacing.md}`,
        gap: spacing.sm,
      },
      lg: {
        fontSize: typography.fontSize.lg,
        padding: `${spacing.md} ${spacing.lg}`,
        gap: spacing.md,
      },
    };

    const variantStyles = {
      primary: {
        backgroundColor: colors.primary[600],
        color: colors.text.inverse,
        borderColor: colors.primary[600],
        '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
          backgroundColor: colors.primary[700],
          borderColor: colors.primary[700],
        },
        '&:focus': {
          outline: 'none',
          boxShadow: `0 0 0 3px ${colors.primary[200]}`,
        },
      },
      secondary: {
        backgroundColor: colors.neutral[200],
        color: colors.text.primary,
        borderColor: colors.neutral[200],
        '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
          backgroundColor: colors.neutral[300],
          borderColor: colors.neutral[300],
        },
        '&:focus': {
          outline: 'none',
          boxShadow: `0 0 0 3px ${colors.neutral[300]}`,
        },
      },
      outline: {
        backgroundColor: 'transparent',
        color: colors.primary[600],
        borderColor: colors.neutral[300],
        '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
          backgroundColor: colors.neutral[50],
          borderColor: colors.neutral[400],
        },
        '&:focus': {
          outline: 'none',
          boxShadow: `0 0 0 3px ${colors.primary[100]}`,
        },
      },
      ghost: {
        backgroundColor: 'transparent',
        color: colors.text.primary,
        borderColor: 'transparent',
        '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
          backgroundColor: colors.neutral[100],
        },
        '&:focus': {
          outline: 'none',
          boxShadow: `0 0 0 3px ${colors.neutral[200]}`,
        },
      },
      danger: {
        backgroundColor: colors.error,
        color: colors.text.inverse,
        borderColor: colors.error,
        '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
          backgroundColor: '#dc2626',
          borderColor: '#dc2626',
        },
        '&:focus': {
          outline: 'none',
          boxShadow: `0 0 0 3px #fecaca`,
        },
      },
    };

    const loadingSpinner = (
      <svg
        className="animate-spin"
        style={{
          width: '1em',
          height: '1em',
          marginRight: sizeStyles[size].gap,
        }}
        viewBox="0 0 24 24"
        fill="none"
      >
        <circle
          className="opacity-25"
          cx="12"
          cy="12"
          r="10"
          stroke="currentColor"
          strokeWidth="4"
        />
        <path
          className="opacity-75"
          fill="currentColor"
          d="M4 12a8 8 0 018-8V0C5.373 0 0 5.373 0 12h4zm2 5.291A7.962 7.962 0 014 12H0c0 3.042 1.135 5.824 3 7.938l3-2.647z"
        />
      </svg>
    );

    return (
      <button
        ref={ref}
        disabled={disabled || isLoading}
        style={{
          ...baseStyles,
          ...sizeStyles[size],
          ...variantStyles[variant],
        }}
        className={className}
        aria-busy={isLoading}
        {...props}
      >
        {isLoading && loadingSpinner}
        {!isLoading && leftIcon && (
          <span style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center' }}>
            {leftIcon}
          </span>
        )}
        <span>{children}</span>
        {!isLoading && rightIcon && (
          <span style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center' }}>
            {rightIcon}
          </span>
        )}
      </button>
    );
  }
);

Button.displayName = 'Button';

export { Button };

// src/components/Button/Button.test.tsx
import { describe, it, expect, vi } from 'vitest';
import { render, screen, fireEvent } from '@testing-library/react';
import { Button } from './Button';

describe('Button', () => {
  it('renders with default props', () => {
    render(<Button>Click me</Button>);
    const button = screen.getByRole('button', { name: /click me/i });
    expect(button).toBeInTheDocument();
    expect(button).toHaveStyle('background-color: #0284c7');
  });

  it('handles click events', () => {
    const handleClick = vi.fn();
    render(<Button onClick={handleClick}>Click me</Button>);
    
    fireEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button'));
    expect(handleClick).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1);
  });

  it('shows loading state', () => {
    render(<Button isLoading>Loading</Button>);
    const button = screen.getByRole('button');
    expect(button).toBeDisabled();
    expect(button).toHaveAttribute('aria-busy', 'true');
  });

  it('is disabled when disabled prop is true', () => {
    render(<Button disabled>Disabled</Button>);
    const button = screen.getByRole('button');
    expect(button).toBeDisabled();
    expect(button).toHaveStyle('opacity: 0.6');
  });

  it('renders with icons', () => {
    const leftIcon = <span data-testid="left-icon">←</span>;
    const rightIcon = <span data-testid="right-icon">→</span>;
    
    render(
      <Button leftIcon={leftIcon} rightIcon={rightIcon}>
        With Icons
      </Button>
    );
    
    expect(screen.getByTestId('left-icon')).toBeInTheDocument();
    expect(screen.getByTestId('right-icon')).toBeInTheDocument();
  });
});

// src/components/Card/Card.tsx
import React, { HTMLAttributes } from 'react';
import { colors, spacing, borderRadius, shadows } from '../../design-system/tokens';

interface CardProps extends HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement> {
  variant?: 'elevated' | 'outlined' | 'filled';
  padding?: 'none' | 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg';
  hoverable?: boolean;
}

const Card: React.FC<CardProps> = ({
  children,
  variant = 'elevated',
  padding = 'md',
  hoverable = false,
  className = '',
  ...props
}) => {
  const paddingMap = {
    none: '0',
    sm: spacing.sm,
    md: spacing.md,
    lg: spacing.lg,
  };

  const variantStyles = {
    elevated: {
      backgroundColor: colors.background.card,
      border: 'none',
      boxShadow: shadows.md,
    },
    outlined: {
      backgroundColor: colors.background.light,
      border: `1px solid ${colors.neutral[200]}`,
      boxShadow: 'none',
    },
    filled: {
      backgroundColor: colors.neutral[50],
      border: 'none',
      boxShadow: 'none',
    },
  };

  const hoverStyles = hoverable
    ? {
        transition: 'all 200ms ease-in-out',
        '&:hover': {
          transform: 'translateY(-2px)',
          boxShadow: shadows.lg,
        },
      }
    : {};

  return (
    <div


### [Sessão Paralela: SRE]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Infraestrutura como Código

Vou configurar uma infraestrutura completa e autônoma com Terraform, Kubernetes, monitoramento e auto-scaling.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v11-core-infra/
├── terraform/
│   ├── main.tf
│   ├── variables.tf
│   ├── outputs.tf
│   ├── kubernetes.tf
│   ├── monitoring.tf
│   └── auto-scaling.tf
├── kubernetes/
│   ├── namespace.yaml
│   ├── deployment.yaml
│   ├── service.yaml
│   ├── hpa.yaml
│   ├── pdb.yaml
│   └── configmap.yaml
├── monitoring/
│   ├── prometheus/
│   │   ├── prometheus.yaml
│   │   └── rules/
│   │       ├── diyapp-rules.yaml
│   │       └── k8s-rules.yaml
│   ├── grafana/
│   │   ├── dashboards/
│   │   │   ├── diyapp-overview.json
│   │   │   ├── kubernetes.json
│   │   │   └── sre-slos.json
│   │   └── datasources/
│   │       └── prometheus.yaml
│   └── alertmanager/
│       ├── alertmanager.yaml
│       └── templates/
│           └── default.tmpl
├── scripts/
│   ├── deploy.sh
│   ├── health-check.sh
│   └── chaos-test.sh
├── .github/
│   └── workflows/
│       └── terraform-ci.yml
└── README.md
```

## 1. Terraform - Infraestrutura Principal

### `terraform/main.tf`
```hcl
terraform {
  required_version = ">= 1.5.0"
  required_providers {
    aws = {
      source  = "hashicorp/aws"
      version = "~> 5.0"
    }
    kubernetes = {
      source  = "hashicorp/kubernetes"
      version = "~> 2.23"
    }
    helm = {
      source  = "hashicorp/helm"
      version = "~> 2.11"
    }
  }
  backend "s3" {
    bucket         = "diyapp-terraform-state"
    key            = "v11-core/terraform.tfstate"
    region         = "us-east-1"
    encrypt        = true
    dynamodb_table = "diyapp-terraform-locks"
  }
}

provider "aws" {
  region = var.aws_region
  default_tags {
    tags = {
      Project     = "DIYAPP-V11"
      Environment = var.environment
      ManagedBy   = "Terraform"
      Squad       = "Autonomous-SRE"
    }
  }
}

# VPC para isolamento
module "vpc" {
  source  = "terraform-aws-modules/vpc/aws"
  version = "~> 5.0"

  name = "diyapp-v11-vpc"
  cidr = "10.0.0.0/16"

  azs             = ["${var.aws_region}a", "${var.aws_region}b", "${var.aws_region}c"]
  private_subnets = ["10.0.1.0/24", "10.0.2.0/24", "10.0.3.0/24"]
  public_subnets  = ["10.0.101.0/24", "10.0.102.0/24", "10.0.103.0/24"]

  enable_nat_gateway     = true
  single_nat_gateway     = false
  one_nat_gateway_per_az = true
  enable_vpn_gateway     = false

  enable_dns_hostnames = true
  enable_dns_support   = true

  tags = {
    "kubernetes.io/cluster/${var.cluster_name}" = "shared"
  }

  public_subnet_tags = {
    "kubernetes.io/cluster/${var.cluster_name}" = "shared"
    "kubernetes.io/role/elb"                    = "1"
  }

  private_subnet_tags = {
    "kubernetes.io/cluster/${var.cluster_name}" = "shared"
    "kubernetes.io/role/internal-elb"           = "1"
  }
}

# EKS Cluster
module "eks" {
  source  = "terraform-aws-modules/eks/aws"
  version = "~> 19.0"

  cluster_name    = var.cluster_name
  cluster_version = "1.28"

  vpc_id     = module.vpc.vpc_id
  subnet_ids = module.vpc.private_subnets

  cluster_endpoint_public_access = true
  cluster_endpoint_private_access = true

  eks_managed_node_groups = {
    diyapp_core = {
      name           = "diyapp-core"
      instance_types = ["t3.medium", "t3.large"]
      min_size       = 3
      max_size       = 10
      desired_size   = 3

      labels = {
        role        = "core"
        environment = var.environment
      }

      taints = []

      tags = {
        "k8s.io/cluster-autoscaler/enabled"               = "true"
        "k8s.io/cluster-autoscaler/${var.cluster_name}" = "owned"
      }
    }

    diyapp_llm = {
      name           = "diyapp-llm"
      instance_types = ["g4dn.xlarge", "g5.xlarge"]
      min_size       = 1
      max_size       = 4
      desired_size   = 2

      labels = {
        role        = "llm"
        gpu         = "true"
        environment = var.environment
      }

      taints = [{
        key    = "llm"
        value  = "true"
        effect = "NO_SCHEDULE"
      }]

      tags = {
        "k8s.io/cluster-autoscaler/enabled"               = "true"
        "k8s.io/cluster-autoscaler/${var.cluster_name}" = "owned"
      }
    }
  }

  node_security_group_additional_rules = {
    ingress_self_all = {
      description = "Node to node all ports/protocols"
      protocol    = "-1"
      from_port   = 0
      to_port     = 0
      type        = "ingress"
      self        = true
    }
    ingress_cluster_ports = {
      description                   = "Cluster API to node group"
      protocol                      = "tcp"
      from_port                     = 1025
      to_port                       = 65535
      type                          = "ingress"
      source_cluster_security_group = true
    }
  }

  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
    Project     = "DIYAPP-V11"
  }
}

# IAM OIDC Provider para Service Accounts
data "tls_certificate" "eks" {
  url = module.eks.cluster_oidc_issuer_url
}

resource "aws_iam_openid_connect_provider" "eks" {
  client_id_list  = ["sts.amazonaws.com"]
  thumbprint_list = [data.tls_certificate.eks.certificates[0].sha1_fingerprint]
  url             = module.eks.cluster_oidc_issuer_url
}

  role_name = "cluster-autoscaler-${var.cluster_name}"

  attach_cluster_autoscaler_policy = true
  cluster_autoscaler_cluster_ids   = [module.eks.cluster_name]

  oidc_providers = {
    main = {
      provider_arn               = aws_iam_openid_connect_provider.eks.arn
      namespace_service_accounts = ["kube-system:cluster-autoscaler"]
    }
  }
}

  vpc_security_group_ids = [module.eks.cluster_primary_security_group_id]

  maintenance_window = "Mon:00:00-Mon:03:00"
  backup_window      = "03:00-06:00"
  backup_retention_period = 7

  enabled_cloudwatch_logs_exports = ["postgresql", "upgrade"]
  create_cloudwatch_log_group     = true

  parameters = [
    {
      name  = "autovacuum"
      value = 1
    },
    {
      name  = "client_encoding"
      value = "utf8"
    }
  ]

  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
    Project     = "DIYAPP-V11"
  }
}

  num_cache_nodes     = 1

  port                = 6379

# S3 para armazenamento de objetos
resource "aws_s3_bucket" "diyapp_storage" {
  bucket = "diyapp-v11-storage-${var.environment}"

  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
    Project     = "DIYAPP-V11"
  }
}

resource "aws_s3_bucket_versioning" "diyapp_storage" {
  bucket = aws_s3_bucket.diyapp_storage.id
  versioning_configuration {
    status = "Enabled"
  }
}

resource "aws_s3_bucket_server_side_encryption_configuration" "diyapp_storage" {
  bucket = aws_s3_bucket.diyapp_storage.id

  rule {
    apply_server_side_encryption_by_default {
      sse_algorithm = "AES256"
    }
  }
}

# CloudWatch Log Groups
resource "aws_cloudwatch_log_group" "diyapp_app" {
  name              = "/aws/eks/${var.cluster_name}/diyapp"
  retention_in_days = 30

  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
    Project     = "DIYAPP-V11"
  }
}

resource "aws_cloudwatch_log_group" "diyapp_audit" {
  name              = "/aws/eks/${var.cluster_name}/audit"
  retention_in_days = 90

  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
    Project     = "DIYAPP-V11"
  }
}
```

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Arquitetura de Microsserviços

## ADR-001: Arquitetura de Microsserviços para V11

**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead + Especialista Infra

### CONTEXTO:
A V10 do DIYAPP evoluiu para uma arquitetura monolítica que está limitando:
1. Escalabilidade independente de componentes
2. Deploy contínuo sem downtime total
3. Isolamento de falhas entre módulos
4. Autonomia das squads no desenvolvimento

Forças em jogo:
- Necessidade de 100% de estabilidade autônoma
- Modo Hive para refatoração paralela
- Time-to-market reduzido para novas features
- Manutenibilidade a longo prazo

### DECISÃO:
Adotar arquitetura de microsserviços baseada em eventos com os seguintes princípios:
1. **12-Factor App** para cada microsserviço
2. **Comunicação assíncrona via eventos** como padrão
3. **API Gateway** como único ponto de entrada externo
4. **Service Mesh** para comunicação interna
5. **Database per Service** com dados proprietários
6. **Event Sourcing** para consistência eventual

### OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:

**Opção A: Microsserviços com Event-Driven Architecture (Escolhida)**
- Prós: Desacoplamento máximo, escalabilidade granular, resiliência a falhas
- Contras: Complexidade operacional, debugging distribuído, consistência eventual

**Opção B: Arquitetura em Camadas com Módulos**
- Prós: Simplicidade operacional, transações ACID, debugging fácil
- Contras: Acoplamento forte, deploy monolítico, escalabilidade limitada

**Opção C: Microsserviços com Comunicação Síncrona (REST/gRPC)**
- Prós: Modelo mental familiar, ferramentas maduras
- Contras: Acoplamento temporal, cascata de falhas, latência acumulada

### CONSEQUÊNCIAS:
**Positivas:**
- Cada squad pode desenvolver/deployar independentemente
- Falhas isoladas não derrubam o sistema inteiro
- Escala horizontal granular por demanda
- Stack tecnológica adequada por domínio

**Negativas:**
- Operação mais complexa (monitoramento distribuído)
- Transações distribuídas complexas
- Overhead de rede entre serviços
- Versionamento de contratos necessário

**Riscos:**
1. **Eventos duplicados**: Implementar idempotência em todos os consumidores
2. **Ordem de eventos**: Usar timestamps lamport ou sequenciadores
3. **Monitoramento**: Implementar distributed tracing (Jaeger) e métricas detalhadas

**REVISÃO:** 2024-04-15

---

## Engineering Standards - V11

```yaml
# engineering-standards-v11.yml
version: "1.0.0"
last_updated: "2024-01-15"

# 1. ESTRUTURA DE REPOSITÓRIO
repository_structure:
  pattern: "service-{nome}"
  directories:
    - src/
      - api/          # Controllers, routes, middleware
      - domain/       # Entities, value objects, domain services
      - application/  # Use cases, application services
      - infrastructure/ # Repositories, external services
      - events/       # Event producers/consumers
      - shared/       # DTOs, enums, interfaces compartilhadas
    - tests/
      - unit/         # Testes unitários
      - integration/  # Testes de integração
      - e2e/          # Testes end-to-end
    - deployments/    # Docker, Kubernetes, Terraform
    - docs/           # OpenAPI, ADRs, decisões

# 2. PADRÕES DE CÓDIGO
coding_standards:
  language: "TypeScript 5.0+"
  style_guide: "Airbnb TypeScript Style Guide"
  linting: "ESLint com regras customizadas"
  formatting: "Prettier com configuração padrão"
  naming_conventions:
    files: "kebab-case"
    classes: "PascalCase"
    functions: "camelCase"
    constants: "UPPER_SNAKE_CASE"
    interfaces: "I{PascalCase}"  # Ex: IUserRepository
    events: "{Entity}{Action}Event"  # Ex: UserCreatedEvent

# 3. CONTRATOS DE API
api_standards:
  external_apis:
    protocol: "RESTful HTTP/JSON"
    versioning: "URL path (v1, v2)"
    authentication: "JWT Bearer tokens"
    rate_limiting: "X-RateLimit-* headers"
    pagination: "cursor-based"
    filtering: "query parameters"
    sorting: "sort=field:asc|desc"
    error_format:
      code: "string"
      message: "string"
      details: "object[]"
      trace_id: "string"
  
  internal_apis:
    protocol: "gRPC com Protobuf"
    service_mesh: "Istio/Linkerd"
    timeout: "default 5s, configurável"
    retry_policy: "exponential backoff"
    circuit_breaker: "configuração padrão"

# 4. PADRÕES DE EVENTOS
event_standards:
  message_broker: "Apache Kafka"
  event_format:
    id: "UUID v4"
    type: "domain.event.version"
    timestamp: "ISO 8601"
    producer: "service-name"
    data: "event payload"
    metadata: "correlation_id, causation_id"
  
  schema_registry: "Confluent Schema Registry"
  event_versioning: "semantic versioning"
  dead_letter_queue: "tópico .dlq"
  replay_support: "tópicos compactados"

# 5. PADRÕES DE BANCO DE DADOS
database_standards:
  principle: "database per service"
  migrations: "versionadas e reversíveis"
  connection_pooling: "obrigatório"
  read_replicas: "para cargas de leitura"
  backup: "automático e testado"
  data_ownership: "dados proprietários apenas"

# 6. PADRÕES DE TESTES
testing_standards:
  unit_tests:
    coverage: ">= 80%"
    framework: "Jest"
    mocks: "jest.mock() para externos"
  
  integration_tests:
    scope: "testar integrações reais"
    fixtures: "dados isolados por teste"
    cleanup: "obrigatório após cada teste"
  
  e2e_tests:
    scope: "fluxos de negócio completos"
    environment: "staging-like"
    data: "seeded data"

# 7. PADRÕES DE DEPLOY
deployment_standards:
  containerization: "Docker multi-stage"
  orchestration: "Kubernetes"
  health_checks:
    liveness: "/health"
    readiness: "/ready"
    startup: "/startup"
  
  observability:
    logs: "structured JSON logs"
    metrics: "Prometheus format"
    tracing: "OpenTelemetry"
    alerts: "baseadas em SLOs"

# 8. PADRÕES DE SEGURANÇA
security_standards:
  authentication: "OAuth 2.0 + OpenID Connect"
  authorization: "RBAC com escopos"
  secrets: "Hashicorp Vault"
  encryption:
    at_rest: "AES-256"
    in_transit: "TLS 1.3+"
  
  vulnerability_scanning:
    containers: "Trivy"
    dependencies: "npm audit, Snyk"
    code: "SonarQube"

# 9. PADRÕES DE VERSIONAMENTO
versioning_standards:
  api_versioning: "semver na URL"
  event_versioning: "semver no tipo"
  service_versioning: "semver no container tag"
  breaking_changes:
    api: "nova versão major"
    events: "novo tipo de evento"
    database: "migração compatível"
```

## Contratos de API - Especificações OpenAPI

```yaml
# api-gateway/openapi.yaml
openapi: 3.0.3
info:
  title: "DIYAPP V11 API Gateway"
  version: "1.0.0"
  description: "Ponto de entrada único para todos os microsserviços"

servers:
  - url: https://api.diyapp.com/v1
    description: "Production server"
  - url: https://staging-api.diyapp.com/v1
    description: "Staging server"

components:
  securitySchemes:
    bearerAuth:
      type: http
      scheme: bearer
      bearerFormat: JWT
  
  schemas:
    Error:
      type: object
      properties:
        code:
          type: string
          example: "VALIDATION_ERROR"
        message:
          type: string
          example: "Invalid input data"
        details:
          type: array
          items:
            type: object
            properties:
              field:
                type: string
              message:
                type: string
        trace_id:
          type: string
          example: "abc123-def456"
    
    PaginatedResponse:
      type: object
      properties:
        data:
          type: array
        pagination:
          type: object
          properties:
            cursor:
              type: string
            has_more:
              type: boolean
            total:
              type: integer

paths:
  /auth/login:
    post:
      tags: [Authentication]
      summary: "Login de usuário"
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              type: object
              properties:
                email:
                  type: string
                  format: email
                password:
                  type: string
                  format: password
      responses:
        200:
          description: "Login successful"
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                type: object
                properties:
                  access_token:
                    type: string
                  refresh_token:
                    type: string
                  expires_in:
                    type: integer
        401:
          description: "Unauthorized"
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/Error'

  /users:
    get:
      tags: [Users]
      security:
        - bearerAuth: []
      parameters:
        - name: cursor
          in: query
          schema:
            type: string
        - name: limit
          in: query
          schema:
            type: integer
            default: 20
            maximum: 100
      responses:
        200:
          description: "Lista de usuários"
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                allOf:
                  - $ref: '#/components/schemas/PaginatedResponse'
                  - type: object
                    properties:
                      data:
                        type: array
                        items:
                          $ref: '#/components/schemas/User'
    
    post:
      tags: [Users]
      summary: "Criar novo usuário"
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/CreateUserRequest'
      responses:
        201:
          description: "User created"
          headers:
            Location:
              schema:
                type: string
              description: "URL do usuário criado"
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/User'

components:
  schemas:
    User:
      type: object
      properties:
        id:
          type: string
          format: uuid
        email:
          type: string
          format: email
        name:
          type: string
        status:
          type: string
          enum: [active, inactive, suspended]
        created_at:
          type: string
          format: date-time
        updated_at:
          type: string
          format: date-time
    
    CreateUserRequest:
      type: object
      required: [email, name, password]
      properties:
        email:
          type: string
          format: email
        name:
          type: string
          minLength: 2
          maxLength: 100
        password:
          type: string
          format: password
          minLength: 8
```

# DIYAPP Evolution V11 - Design System & Dashboard Wireframes

### [Sessão Paralela: Frontend]
```tsx
// src/App.tsx
import React, { Suspense, lazy } from 'react';
import { BrowserRouter as Router, Routes, Route, Navigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { DesignSystemProvider } from './design-system/DesignSystemProvider';
import { LoadingSpinner } from './components/feedback/LoadingSpinner';
import { ErrorBoundary } from './components/error/ErrorBoundary';
import { Layout } from './components/layout/Layout';

// Lazy loading com code splitting para rotas principais
const Dashboard = lazy(() => import('./pages/Dashboard').then(module => ({ default: module.Dashboard })));
const Analytics = lazy(() => import('./pages/Analytics').then(module => ({ default: module.Analytics })));
const Settings = lazy(() => import('./pages/Settings').then(module => ({ default: module.Settings })));
const AIWorkflow = lazy(() => import('./pages/AIWorkflow').then(module => ({ default: module.AIWorkflow })));

// Componente de fallback para lazy loading
const PageLoader = () => (
  <div className="page-loader" role="status" aria-label="Carregando página">
    <LoadingSpinner size="lg" />
    <span className="visually-hidden">Carregando conteúdo...</span>
  </div>
);

function App() {
  return (
    <ErrorBoundary>
      <DesignSystemProvider>
        <Router>
          <Layout>
            <Suspense fallback={<PageLoader />}>
              <Routes>
                <Route path="/" element={<Navigate to="/dashboard" replace />} />
                <Route path="/dashboard" element={<Dashboard />} />
                <Route path="/analytics" element={<Analytics />} />
                <Route path="/settings" element={<Settings />} />
                <Route path="/ai-workflow" element={<AIWorkflow />} />
                <Route path="*" element={<Navigate to="/dashboard" replace />} />
              </Routes>
            </Suspense>
          </Layout>
        </Router>
      </DesignSystemProvider>
    </ErrorBoundary>
  );
}

export default App;
```

```tsx
// src/design-system/DesignSystemProvider.tsx
import React from 'react';
import { ThemeProvider } from 'styled-components';
import { GlobalStyles } from './GlobalStyles';
import { tokens } from './tokens';

interface DesignSystemProviderProps {
  children: React.ReactNode;
}

export const DesignSystemProvider: React.FC<DesignSystemProviderProps> = ({ children }) => {
  return (
    <ThemeProvider theme={tokens}>
      <GlobalStyles />
      {children}
    </ThemeProvider>
  );
};
```

// src/design-system/tokens.ts
export const tokens = {
  colors: {
    primary: {

      400: '#a3a3a3',

      600: '#525252',
      700: '#404040',
      800: '#262626',
      900: '#171717',
    },
    success: '#10b981',
    warning: '#f59e0b',
    error: '#ef4444',
    info: '#3b82f6',
  },
  spacing: {
    xs: '0.25rem', // 4px
    sm: '0.5rem',  // 8px
    md: '1rem',    // 16px
    lg: '1.5rem',  // 24px

    '2xl': '3rem', // 48px

    fontFamily: {
      sans: "'Inter', -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, 'Segoe UI', Roboto, sans-serif",

      normal: '400',

    xl: '0.75rem',  // 12px
    full: '9999px',
  },
} as const;

export type Theme = typeof tokens;

```tsx
// src/design-system/GlobalStyles.tsx
import { createGlobalStyle } from 'styled-components';
import { tokens } from './tokens';

export const GlobalStyles = createGlobalStyle`
  *,
  *::before,
  *::after {
    box-sizing: border-box;
    margin: 0;
    padding: 0;
  }

  :root {
    --color-primary-50: ${tokens.colors.primary[50]};
    --color-primary-500: ${tokens.colors.primary[500]};
    --color-primary-600: ${tokens.colors.primary[600]};
    --color-neutral-50: ${tokens.colors.neutral[50]};
    --color-neutral-100: ${tokens.colors.neutral[100]};
    --color-neutral-700: ${tokens.colors.neutral[700]};
    --color-neutral-900: ${tokens.colors.neutral[900]};
    --color-success: ${tokens.colors.success};
    --color-warning: ${tokens.colors.warning};
    --color-error: ${tokens.colors.error};
    --color-info: ${tokens.colors.info};
    
    --spacing-xs: ${tokens.spacing.xs};
    --spacing-sm: ${tokens.spacing.sm};
    --spacing-md: ${tokens.spacing.md};
    --spacing-lg: ${tokens.spacing.lg};
    --spacing-xl: ${tokens.spacing.xl};
    
    --font-size-xs: ${tokens.typography.fontSize.xs};
    --font-size-sm: ${tokens.typography.fontSize.sm};
    --font-size-base: ${tokens.typography.fontSize.base};
    --font-size-lg: ${tokens.typography.fontSize.lg};
    
    --border-radius-md: ${tokens.borderRadius.md};
    --border-radius-lg: ${tokens.borderRadius.lg};
    
    --shadow-md: ${tokens.shadows.md};
    --shadow-lg: ${tokens.shadows.lg};
  }

  html {
    font-size: 16px;
    -webkit-font-smoothing: antialiased;
    -moz-osx-font-smoothing: grayscale;
    text-size-adjust: 100%;
  }

  body {
    font-family: ${tokens.typography.fontFamily.sans};
    font-size: ${tokens.typography.fontSize.base};
    line-height: ${tokens.typography.lineHeight.normal};
    color: ${tokens.colors.neutral[900]};
    background-color: ${tokens.colors.neutral[50]};
    min-height: 100vh;
    overflow-x: hidden;
  }

  #root {
    min-height: 100vh;
    display: flex;
    flex-direction: column;
  }

  /* Acessibilidade: foco visível */
  :focus-visible {
    outline: 2px solid ${tokens.colors.primary[500]};
    outline-offset: 2px;
  }

  /* Remove focus outline para mouse users */
  :focus:not(:focus-visible) {
    outline: none;
  }

  /* Acessibilidade: conteúdo oculto visualmente */
  .visually-hidden {
    position: absolute;
    width: 1px;
    height: 1px;
    padding: 0;
    margin: -1px;
    overflow: hidden;
    clip: rect(0, 0, 0, 0);
    white-space: nowrap;
    border: 0;
  }

  /* Responsive images */
  img {
    max-width: 100%;
    height: auto;
    display: block;
  }

  /* Responsive tables */
  table {
    width: 100%;
    border-collapse: collapse;
  }

  /* Responsive iframes */
  iframe {
    max-width: 100%;
  }

  /* Smooth scrolling */
  @media (prefers-reduced-motion: no-preference) {
    html {
      scroll-behavior: smooth;
    }
  }

  /* Reduced motion */
  @media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce) {
    *,
    *::before,
    *::after {
      animation-duration: 0.01ms !important;
      animation-iteration-count: 1 !important;
      transition-duration: 0.01ms !important;
      scroll-behavior: auto !important;
    }
  }

  /* Print styles */
  @media print {
    body {
      background: white;
      color: black;
    }
    
    .no-print {
      display: none !important;
    }
  }
`;
```

```tsx
// src/components/layout/Layout.tsx
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import styled from 'styled-components';
import { tokens } from '../../design-system/tokens';
import { Sidebar } from './Sidebar';
import { Header } from './Header';
import { SkipToContent } from '../a11y/SkipToContent';

const LayoutContainer = styled.div`
  display: flex;
  min-height: 100vh;
  background-color: ${tokens.colors.neutral[50]};

  @media (max-width: ${tokens.breakpoints.lg}) {
    flex-direction: column;
  }
`;

const MainContent = styled.main`
  flex: 1;
  display: flex;
  flex-direction: column;
  min-height: 100vh;
  margin-left: 280px; /* Largura da sidebar */

  @media (max-width: ${tokens.breakpoints.lg}) {
    margin-left: 0;
    margin-top: 64px; /* Altura do header mobile */
  }
`;

const ContentArea = styled.div`
  flex: 1;
  padding: ${tokens.spacing.xl};
  max-width: 1400px;
  width: 100%;
  margin: 0 auto;

  @media (max-width: ${tokens.breakpoints.md}) {
    padding: ${tokens.spacing.md};
  }

  @media (max-width: ${tokens.breakpoints.sm}) {
    padding: ${tokens.spacing.sm};
  }
`;

interface LayoutProps {
  children: React.ReactNode;
}

export const Layout: React.FC<LayoutProps> = ({ children }) => {
  const [isSidebarOpen, setIsSidebarOpen] = useState(true);
  const [isMobile, setIsMobile] = useState(false);

  useEffect(() => {
    const checkMobile = () => {
      setIsMobile(window.innerWidth < parseInt(tokens.breakpoints.lg));
      if (window.innerWidth < parseInt(tokens.breakpoints.lg)) {
        setIsSidebarOpen(false);
      }
    };

    checkMobile();
    window.addEventListener('resize', checkMobile);
    
    return () => window.removeEventListener('resize', checkMobile);
  }, []);

  const toggleSidebar = () => {
    setIsSidebarOpen(!isSidebarOpen);
  };

  return (
    <>
      <SkipToContent />
      <LayoutContainer>
        <Sidebar isOpen={isSidebarOpen} onClose={() => setIsSidebarOpen(false)} />
        <MainContent>
          <Header 
            onMenuClick={toggleSidebar}
            isSidebarOpen={isSidebarOpen}
            isMobile={isMobile}
          />
          <ContentArea id="main-content">
            {children}
          </ContentArea>
        </MainContent>
      </LayoutContainer>
    </>
  );
};
```

```tsx
// src/components/layout/Sidebar.tsx
import React from 'react';
import styled from 'styled-components';
import { tokens } from '../../design-system/tokens';
import { NavLink } from 'react-router-dom';
import { Icon } from '../ui/Icon';

const SidebarContainer = styled.aside<{ $isOpen: boolean }>`
  position: fixed;
  top: 0;
  left: 0;
  bottom: 0;
  width: 280px;
  background: linear-gradient(180deg, ${tokens.colors.neutral[900]} 0%, ${tokens.colors.neutral[800]} 100%);
  color: ${tokens.colors.neutral[100]};
  z-index: 1000;
  transform: translateX(${props => props.$isOpen ? '0' : '-100%'});
  transition: transform 0.3s ease-in-out;
  display: flex;
  flex-direction: column;

# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core
# Dev Backend - APIs REST/GraphQL Core + Background Workers
# Foco: Estabilidade 100% autônoma com resiliência embutida

"""
