# ==================== CONFIGURAÇÃO PRINCIPAL ====================
# config.py
import os
from typing import Dict, Any
from pydantic import BaseSettings, Field
from datetime import timedelta


class Settings(BaseSettings):
    """Configurações da aplicação com validação de tipos"""
    
    # API
    API_V1_PREFIX: str = "/api/v1"
    API_V2_PREFIX: str = "/api/v2"
    GRAPHQL_PATH: str = "/graphql"
    
    # Database
    DATABASE_URL: str = Field(
        default=os.getenv("DATABASE_URL", "postgresql://user:pass@localhost:5432/diyapp"),
        description="URL de conexão com o banco de dados"
    )
    DATABASE_POOL_SIZE: int = 20
    DATABASE_MAX_OVERFLOW: int = 10
    
    # Redis para cache e workers
    REDIS_URL: str = Field(
        default=os.getenv("REDIS_URL", "redis://localhost:6379/0"),
        description="URL do Redis para cache e filas"
    )
    
    # Autenticação
    SECRET_KEY: str = Field(
        default=os.getenv("SECRET_KEY", "your-secret-key-change-in-production"),
        min_length=32
    )
    ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES: int = 30
    ALGORITHM: str = "HS256"
    
    # LLM Integration
    LLM_API_KEY: str = Field(default=os.getenv("LLM_API_KEY", ""))
    LLM_BASE_URL: str = Field(default=os.getenv("LLM_BASE_URL", "https://api.openai.com/v1"))
    LLM_TIMEOUT: int = 30  # segundos
    LLM_MAX_RETRIES: int = 3
    
    # Rate Limiting
    RATE_LIMIT_REQUESTS: int = 100
    RATE_LIMIT_PERIOD: int = 60  # segundos
    
    # Circuit Breaker
    CIRCUIT_BREAKER_FAILURE_THRESHOLD: int = 5
    CIRCUIT_BREAKER_RECOVERY_TIMEOUT: int = 30
    
    # Observability
    LOG_LEVEL: str = "INFO"
    METRICS_PORT: int = 9090
    JAEGER_ENDPOINT: str = Field(default=os.getenv("JAEGER_ENDPOINT", "http://localhost:14268/api/traces"))
    
    class Config:
        env_file = ".env"
        case_sensitive = False


settings = Settings()

# ==================== MODELOS DE DADOS ====================
# src/core/models/automation.py
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Optional, Dict, Any, List
from enum import Enum
from pydantic import BaseModel, Field, validator


class AutomationStatus(str, Enum):
    """Status dos workflows de automação"""
    DRAFT = "draft"
    ACTIVE = "active"
    PAUSED = "paused"
    ERROR = "error"
    COMPLETED = "completed"


class TriggerType(str, Enum):
    """Tipos de trigger para automação"""
    SCHEDULED = "scheduled"
    WEBHOOK = "webhook"
    MANUAL = "manual"
    EVENT = "event"


class Automation(BaseModel):
    """Modelo principal de automação"""
    id: str = Field(description="ID único da automação")
    name: str = Field(..., min_length=1, max_length=100, description="Nome da automação")
    description: Optional[str] = Field(None, max_length=500)
    status: AutomationStatus = Field(default=AutomationStatus.DRAFT)
    trigger_type: TriggerType
    trigger_config: Dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict)
    workflow_steps: List[Dict[str, Any]] = Field(default_factory=list)
    created_at: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.utcnow)
    updated_at: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.utcnow)
    created_by: str = Field(..., description="ID do usuário criador")
    last_execution: Optional[datetime] = None
    execution_count: int = Field(default=0, ge=0)
    error_count: int = Field(default=0, ge=0)
    
    @validator('workflow_steps')
    def validate_workflow_steps(cls, v):
        """Valida que há pelo menos um passo no workflow"""
        if not v:
            raise ValueError("Workflow deve ter pelo menos um passo")
        return v
    
    class Config:
        schema_extra = {
            "example": {
                "id": "auto_123",
                "name": "Processar pedidos diários",
                "description": "Automação para processar pedidos pendentes",
                "status": "active",
                "trigger_type": "scheduled",
                "trigger_config": {"cron": "0 9 * * *"},
                "workflow_steps": [
                    {"type": "fetch_data", "config": {"source": "orders"}},
                    {"type": "transform", "config": {"rules": ["validate_amount"]}},
                    {"type": "notify", "config": {"channel": "email"}}
                ]
            }
        }


# src/core/models/analysis.py
class AnalysisType(str, Enum):
    """Tipos de análise disponíveis"""
    TREND = "trend"
    PREDICTION = "prediction"
    CLUSTERING = "clustering"
    ANOMALY = "anomaly"


class Analysis(BaseModel):
    """Modelo de análise de dados"""
    id: str = Field(description="ID único da análise")
    name: str = Field(..., min_length=1, max_length=100)
    type: AnalysisType
    dataset_id: str = Field(..., description="ID do dataset analisado")
    parameters: Dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict)
    results: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None
    status: str = Field(default="pending")  # pending, running, completed, failed
    created_at: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.utcnow)
    completed_at: Optional[datetime] = None
    created_by: str
    execution_time_ms: Optional[int] = None
    error_message: Optional[str] = None
    
    class Config:
        schema_extra = {
            "example": {
                "id": "analysis_456",
                "name": "Previsão de vendas Q4",
                "type": "prediction",
                "dataset_id": "ds_789",
                "parameters": {"model": "prophet", "horizon": 30},
                "status": "completed",
                "results": {"mse": 0.05, "predictions": [...]}
            }
        }

# ==================== SCHEMAS DE API ====================
# src/api/v1/schemas/automation.py
from typing import Optional, List
from pydantic import BaseModel, validator


class AutomationCreate(BaseModel):
    """Schema para criação de automação"""
    name: str = Field(..., min_length=1, max_length=100)
    description: Optional[str] = None
    trigger_type: TriggerType
    trigger_config: Dict[str, Any]
    workflow_steps: List[Dict[str, Any]]
    
    @validator('trigger_config')
    def validate_trigger_config(cls, v, values):
        """Valida configuração do trigger baseado no tipo"""
        trigger_type = values.get('trigger_type')
        
        if trigger_type == TriggerType.SCHEDULED:
            if 'cron' not in v:
                raise ValueError("Trigger scheduled requer campo 'cron'")
            # Validação básica de cron expression
            cron_parts = v['cron'].split()
            if len(cron_parts) != 5:
                raise ValueError("Cron expression deve ter 5 partes")
        
        elif trigger_type == TriggerType.WEBHOOK:
            if 'secret' not in v:
                raise ValueError("Trigger webhook requer campo 'secret'")
        
        return v


class AutomationUpdate(BaseModel):
    """Schema para atualização de automação"""
    name: Optional[str] = Field(None, min_length=1, max_length=100)
    description: Optional[str] = None
    status: Optional[AutomationStatus] = None
    trigger_config: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None
    workflow_steps: Optional[List[Dict[str, Any]]] = None


class AutomationResponse(BaseModel):
    """Schema de resposta para automação"""
    id: str
    name: str
    description: Optional[str]
    status: AutomationStatus
    trigger_type: TriggerType
    trigger_config: Dict[str, Any]
    workflow_steps: List[Dict[str, Any]]
    created_at: datetime
    updated_at: datetime
    last_execution: Optional[datetime]
    execution_count: int
    error_count: int


class AutomationListResponse(BaseModel):
    """Schema para listagem de automações"""
    items: List[AutomationResponse]
    total: int
    page: int
    page_size: int
    has_more: bool


# src/api/v1/schemas/analysis.py
class AnalysisCreate(BaseModel):
    """Schema para criação de análise"""
    name: str = Field(..., min_length=1, max_length=100)
    type: AnalysisType
    dataset_id: str
    parameters: Dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict)


class AnalysisResponse(BaseModel):
    """Schema de resposta para análise"""
    id: str
    name: str
    type: AnalysisType
    dataset_id: str
    parameters: Dict[str, Any]
    results: Optional[Dict[str, Any]]
    status: str
    created_at: datetime
    completed_at: Optional[datetime]
    execution_time_ms: Optional[int]
    error_message: Optional[str]


# ==================== LÓGICA DE NEGÓCIO ====================
# src/core/business_logic/automation_service.py
import asyncio
from typing import List, Optional, Dict, Any
from datetime import datetime
import uuid
import json
from functools import lru_cache

from ..models.automation import Automation, AutomationStatus, TriggerType
from ...database.repository import AutomationRepository
from ...external.llm_client import LLMClient
from ...external.circuit_breaker import CircuitBreaker
from ...utils.observability import metrics, logger


class AutomationService:
    """Serviço de lógica de negócio para automações"""
    
    def __init__(self, repository: AutomationRepository, llm_client: Optional[LLMClient] = None):
        self.repository = repository
        self.llm_client = llm_client or LLMClient()
        self.circuit_breaker = CircuitBreaker(
            name="llm_service",
            failure_threshold=5,
            recovery_timeout=30
        )
    
    async def create_automation(self, automation_data: Dict[str, Any], user_id: str) -> Automation:
        """Cria uma nova automação com validação"""
        # Validação de negócio: usuário não pode ter mais de 50 automações ativas
        active_count = await self.repository.count_user_automations(user_id, status=AutomationStatus.ACTIVE)
        if active_count >= 50:
            raise ValueError("Limite de 50 automações ativas atingido")
        
        # Gera ID único
        automation_id = f"auto_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:12]}"
        
        # Cria objeto de automação
        automation = Automation(
            id=automation_id,
            created_by=user_id,
            **automation_data
        )
        
        # Salva no repositório
        await self.repository.create(automation)
        
        # Log e métrica
        logger.info(
            "Automation created",
            automation_id=automation_id,
            user_id=user_id,
            trigger_type=automation.trigger_type.value
        )
        metrics.increment_counter("automation_created", tags={"trigger_type": automation.trigger_type.value})
        
        return automation
    
    async def execute_automation(self, automation_id: str, trigger_data: Optional[Dict] = None) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Executa uma automação com resiliência"""
        # Busca automação
        automation = await self.repository.get_by_id(automation_id)
        if not automation:
            raise ValueError(f"Automação {automation_id} não encontrada")
        
        if automation.status != AutomationStatus.ACTIVE:
            raise ValueError(f"Automação {automation_id} não está ativa")
        
        start_time = datetime.utcnow()
        
        try:
            # Executa cada passo do workflow
            results = []
            for step_index, step in enumerate(automation.workflow_steps):
                step_result = await self._execute_workflow_step(
                    step=step,
                    step_index=step_index,
                    automation_id=automation_id,
                    trigger_data=trigger_data
                )
                results.append(step_result)
                
                # Se passo falhar, interrompe execução
                if step_result.get("status") == "error":
                    break
            
            # Atualiza estatísticas
            await self.repository.update_execution_stats(
                automation_id,
                success=True,
                execution_time=datetime.utcnow() - start_time
            )
            
            return {
                "automation_id": automation_id,
                "status": "completed",
                "steps_executed": len(results),
                "results": results,
                "execution_time_ms": int((datetime.utcnow() - start_time).total_seconds() * 1000)
            }
            
        except Exception as e:
            # Atualiza estatísticas de erro
            await self.repository.update_execution_stats(
                automation_id,
                success=False,
                error_message=str(e)
            )
            
            logger.error(
                "Automation execution failed",
                automation_id=automation_id,
                error=str(e),
                execution_time_ms=int((datetime.utcnow() - start_time).total_seconds() * 1000)
            )
            metrics.increment_counter("automation_execution_failed")
            
            raise
    
    async def _execute_workflow_step(self, step: Dict[str, Any], step_index: int, 
                                    automation_id: str, trigger_data: Optional[Dict]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Executa um passo individual do workflow com circuit breaker"""
        step_type = step.get("type")
        step_config = step.get("config", {})
        
        step_start = datetime.utcnow()
        
        try:
            if step_type == "llm_processing":
                # Usa circuit breaker para chamadas LLM
                result = await self.circuit_breaker.execute(
                    self._call_llm_service,
                    step_config,
                    automation_id,
                    step_index
                )
            elif step_type == "data_transformation":
                result = await self._transform_data(step_config, trigger_data)
            elif step_type == "webhook_call":
                result = await self._call_webhook(step_config, trigger_data)
            elif step_type == "database_operation":
                result = await self._execute_db_operation(step_config)
            else:
                result = {"status": "skipped", "reason": f"Tipo de passo desconhecido: {step_type}"}
            
            execution_time = int((datetime.utcnow() - step_start).total_seconds() * 1000)
            
            logger.info(
                "Workflow step executed",
                automation_id=automation_id,
                step_index=step_index,
                step_type=step_type,
                execution_time_ms=execution_time,
                status=result.get("status", "unknown")
            )
            
            return {
                "step_index": step_index,
                "step_type": step_type,
                "status": "completed",
                "result": result,
                "execution_time_ms": execution_time
            }
            
        except Exception as e:
            execution_time = int((datetime.utcnow() - step_start).total_seconds() * 1000)
            
            logger.error(
                "Workflow step failed",
                automation_id=automation_id,

## 1. Configuração do dbt (dbt_project.yml)

```yaml
# dbt/dbt_project.yml
name: 'diyapp_v11_analytics'
version: '1.0.0'
config-version: 2

profile: 'diyapp_v11'

model-paths: ["models"]
analysis-paths: ["analyses"]
test-paths: ["tests"]
seed-paths: ["seeds"]
macro-paths: ["macros"]
snapshot-paths: ["snapshots"]

target-path: "target"
clean-targets:
  - "target"
  - "dbt_packages"

models:
  diyapp_v11_analytics:
    materialized: table
    raw:
      materialized: incremental
      unique_key: ['id', 'loaded_at']
      post-hook:
        - "{{ create_index(this, ['loaded_at', 'source_table']) }}"
    staging:
      materialized: view
      post-hook:
        - "{{ create_index(this, ['event_timestamp']) }}"
    marts:
      materialized: table
      post-hook:
        - "{{ grant_select_on_table(this) }}"

seeds:
  diyapp_v11_analytics:
    enabled: true
    quote_columns: false
```

## 2. Camada RAW (Bronze) - Dados Brutos

```sql
-- dbt/models/raw/raw_executions.sql
{{ config(
    materialized='incremental',
    unique_key=['execution_id', 'loaded_at'],
    partition_by={
      "field": "loaded_at",
      "data_type": "timestamp",
      "granularity": "day"
    },
    cluster_by = ["project_id", "status"]
) }}

SELECT
  CAST(execution_id AS STRING) as execution_id,
  CAST(project_id AS STRING) as project_id,
  CAST(user_id AS STRING) as user_id,
  CAST(session_id AS STRING) as session_id,
  CAST(execution_type AS STRING) as execution_type,
  CAST(status AS STRING) as status,
  CAST(error_code AS STRING) as error_code,
  CAST(error_message AS STRING) as error_message,
  CAST(llm_model_used AS STRING) as llm_model_used,
  CAST(llm_provider AS STRING) as llm_provider,
  CAST(input_tokens AS INTEGER) as input_tokens,
  CAST(output_tokens AS INTEGER) as output_tokens,
  CAST(total_tokens AS INTEGER) as total_tokens,
  CAST(execution_time_ms AS INTEGER) as execution_time_ms,
  CAST(memory_used_mb AS INTEGER) as memory_used_mb,
  CAST(cpu_usage_percent AS FLOAT64) as cpu_usage_percent,
  CAST(request_timestamp AS TIMESTAMP) as request_timestamp,
  CAST(response_timestamp AS TIMESTAMP) as response_timestamp,
  CAST(created_at AS TIMESTAMP) as created_at,
  CAST(updated_at AS TIMESTAMP) as updated_at,
  CAST(_source_file AS STRING) as _source_file,
  CAST(_source_line AS INTEGER) as _source_line,
  CURRENT_TIMESTAMP() as loaded_at,
  'executions_api' as source_table
  
FROM {{ source('v11_api', 'executions') }}

{% if is_incremental() %}
WHERE loaded_at > (SELECT MAX(loaded_at) FROM {{ this }})
{% endif %}
```

```sql

FROM {{ source('llm_gateway', 'calls') }}

WHERE loaded_at > (SELECT MAX(loaded_at) FROM {{ this }})

## 3. Camada STAGING (Silver) - Limpeza e Padronização

```sql
-- dbt/models/staging/stg_executions.sql
{{ config(
    materialized='view',
    tags=['staging', 'executions']
) }}

WITH raw_executions AS (
    SELECT 
        *,
        ROW_NUMBER() OVER (
            PARTITION BY execution_id 
            ORDER BY loaded_at DESC
        ) as rn
    FROM {{ ref('raw_executions') }}
    WHERE execution_id IS NOT NULL
      AND project_id IS NOT NULL
      AND user_id IS NOT NULL
      AND request_timestamp IS NOT NULL
)

SELECT
    -- Identificadores
    execution_id,
    project_id,
    user_id,
    session_id,
    
    -- Dados de execução
    execution_type,
    status,
    error_code,
    error_message,
    
    -- Dados LLM
    llm_model_used,
    llm_provider,
    input_tokens,
    output_tokens,
    total_tokens,
    
    -- Métricas de performance
    execution_time_ms,
    memory_used_mb,
    cpu_usage_percent,
    
    -- Timestamps
    request_timestamp as event_timestamp,
    response_timestamp,
    created_at,
    updated_at,
    
    -- Campos calculados
    TIMESTAMP_DIFF(response_timestamp, request_timestamp, MILLISECOND) as total_latency_ms,
    CASE 
        WHEN status = 'success' THEN 1
        ELSE 0 
    END as is_success,
    
    -- Metadados
    loaded_at,
    source_table
    
FROM raw_executions
WHERE rn = 1
  AND request_timestamp >= TIMESTAMP_SUB(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(), INTERVAL 90 DAY)
```

```sql
-- dbt/models/staging/stg_llm_calls.sql
{{ config(
    materialized='view',
    tags=['staging', 'llm']
) }}

WITH raw_llm_calls AS (
    SELECT 
        *,
        ROW_NUMBER() OVER (
            PARTITION BY call_id 
            ORDER BY loaded_at DESC
        ) as rn
    FROM {{ ref('raw_llm_calls') }}
    WHERE call_id IS NOT NULL
      AND execution_id IS NOT NULL
      AND start_time IS NOT NULL
)

SELECT
    -- Identificadores
    call_id,
    execution_id,
    
    -- Dados do modelo
    provider,
    model,
    operation_type,
    
    -- Tokens e custo
    input_tokens,
    output_tokens,
    total_tokens,
    cost_usd,
    
    -- Performance
    latency_ms,
    status_code,
    error_message,
    
    -- Hashes para deduplicação
    request_body_hash,
    response_body_hash,
    
    -- Timestamps
    start_time as event_timestamp,
    end_time,
    created_at,
    
    -- Campos calculados
    CASE 
        WHEN status_code BETWEEN 200 AND 299 THEN 1
        ELSE 0 
    END as is_successful,
    cost_usd / NULLIF(total_tokens, 0) * 1000 as cost_per_1k_tokens,
    
    -- Metadados
    loaded_at,
    source_table
    
FROM raw_llm_calls
WHERE rn = 1
  AND start_time >= TIMESTAMP_SUB(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(), INTERVAL 90 DAY)
```

## 4. Camada MARTS (Gold) - Dados Prontos para Consumo

### 4.1 Mart de Produto (PM)

```sql
-- dbt/models/marts/mart_product/daily_active_users.sql
{{ config(
    materialized='table',
    partition_by={
      "field": "date",
      "data_type": "date",
      "granularity": "day"
    },
    cluster_by = ["user_segment"]
) }}

WITH user_sessions AS (
    SELECT
        user_id,
        DATE(event_timestamp) as date,
        COUNT(DISTINCT session_id) as session_count,
        COUNT(DISTINCT execution_id) as execution_count,
        SUM(CASE WHEN is_success = 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as successful_executions,
        AVG(total_latency_ms) as avg_latency_ms,
        MAX(event_timestamp) as last_activity
    FROM {{ ref('stg_executions') }}
    WHERE event_timestamp >= TIMESTAMP_SUB(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(), INTERVAL 30 DAY)
    GROUP BY 1, 2
),

user_segments AS (
    SELECT
        user_id,
        CASE
            WHEN COUNT(DISTINCT date) >= 20 THEN 'power_user'
            WHEN COUNT(DISTINCT date) >= 10 THEN 'active_user'
            WHEN COUNT(DISTINCT date) >= 5 THEN 'regular_user'
            ELSE 'casual_user'
        END as user_segment
    FROM user_sessions
    GROUP BY 1
)

SELECT
    us.date,
    us.user_id,
    us.session_count,
    us.execution_count,
    us.successful_executions,
    us.avg_latency_ms,
    us.last_activity,
    seg.user_segment,
    CASE 
        WHEN DATE_DIFF(CURRENT_DATE(), DATE(us.last_activity), DAY) <= 7 THEN 'active'
        WHEN DATE_DIFF(CURRENT_DATE(), DATE(us.last_activity), DAY) <= 30 THEN 'dormant'
        ELSE 'churned'
    END as activity_status,
    CURRENT_TIMESTAMP() as calculated_at
    
FROM user_sessions us
LEFT JOIN user_segments seg ON us.user_id = seg.user_id
```

```sql
-- dbt/models/marts/mart_product/execution_funnel.sql
{{ config(
    materialized='table',
    partition_by={
      "field": "funnel_date",
      "data_type": "date",
      "granularity": "day"
    }
) }}

WITH execution_steps AS (
    SELECT
        execution_id,
        user_id,
        DATE(request_timestamp) as funnel_date,
        execution_type,
        status,
        CASE 
            WHEN execution_type = 'code_generation' THEN 1
            WHEN execution_type = 'code_execution' THEN 2
            WHEN execution_type = 'test_execution' THEN 3
            WHEN execution_type = 'deployment' THEN 4
            ELSE 0
        END as step_number,
        CASE 
            WHEN status = 'success' THEN 1
            ELSE 0
        END as is_step_completed
    FROM {{ ref('stg_executions') }}
    WHERE request_timestamp >= TIMESTAMP_SUB(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(), INTERVAL 30 DAY)
),

funnel_aggregation AS (
    SELECT
        funnel_date,
        step_number,
        execution_type as step_name,
        COUNT(DISTINCT execution_id) as total_attempts,
        COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) as unique_users,
        SUM(is_step_completed) as successful_completions,
        LAG(COUNT(DISTINCT execution_id)) OVER (PARTITION BY funnel_date ORDER BY step_number) as previous_step_attempts
    FROM execution_steps
    GROUP BY 1, 2, 3
)

SELECT
    funnel_date,
    step_number,
    step_name,
    total_attempts,
    unique_users,
    successful_completions,
    previous_step_attempts,
    CASE 
        WHEN previous_step_attempts > 0 
        THEN ROUND(CAST(total_attempts AS FLOAT64) / previous_step_attempts * 100, 2)
        ELSE 100.00
    END as conversion_rate_from_previous,
    ROUND(CAST(successful_completions AS FLOAT64) / total_attempts * 100, 2) as success_rate,
    CURRENT_TIMESTAMP() as calculated_at
    
FROM funnel_aggregation
ORDER BY funnel_date DESC, step_number
```

### 4.2 Mart de IA (AI Ops + Especialista LLM)

```sql
-- dbt/models/marts/mart_ai/llm_cost_by_feature.sql
{{ config(
    materialized='table',
    partition_by={
      "field": "cost_date",
      "data_type": "date",
      "granularity": "day"
    },
    cluster_by = ["provider", "model", "feature_name"]
) }}

WITH execution_features AS (
    SELECT
        e.execution_id,
        e.execution_type as feature_name,
        e.user_id,
        e.project_id,
        e.event_timestamp,
        DATE(e.event_timestamp) as cost_date,
        e.llm_provider,
        e.llm_model_used as model,
        e.total_tokens as execution_tokens
    FROM {{ ref('stg_executions') }} e
    WHERE e.event_timestamp >= TIMESTAMP_SUB(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(), INTERVAL 30 DAY)
      AND e.llm_provider IS NOT NULL
),

llm_costs AS (
    SELECT
        l.execution_id,
        l.provider,
        l.model,
        l.operation_type,
        l.total_tokens,
        l.cost_usd

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Arquitetura de Microsserviços e Observabilidade

## 2. ADRs (Architecture Decision Records)

### ADR-001: Arquitetura de Microsserviços

```markdown
# ADR-001: Arquitetura Baseada em Microsserviços com Comunicação por Eventos

**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead + Arquitetura Squad

## CONTEXTO:
O DIYAPP V10 atingiu limites de escalabilidade com arquitetura monolítica. 
Necessidade de:
1. Deploy independente por funcionalidade
2. Escala horizontal seletiva
3. Isolamento de falhas
4. Evolução tecnológica independente

## DECISÃO:
Adotar arquitetura de microsserviços com os seguintes princípios:
- Cada serviço gerencia seu próprio banco de dados
- Comunicação assíncrona via eventos (Kafka)
- API Gateway para roteamento de requisições HTTP
- Service Discovery via Consul
- Circuit Breaker em todas as chamadas síncronas

## OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:
- **Opção A:** Monólito modularizado - Prós: Simples, baixa latência. Contras: Acoplamento, deploy único
- **Opção B:** Microsserviços com REST - Prós: Desacoplamento. Contras: Latência, complexidade de versionamento
- **Opção C:** Microsserviços com eventos - Prós: Desacoplamento total, resiliência. Contras: Complexidade eventual consistency

**Opção escolhida:** C - Justificativa: Alinhamento com requisitos de autonomia e escalabilidade

## CONSEQUÊNCIAS:
**Positivas:**
- Deploy independente por squad
- Escala seletiva de serviços críticos
- Falhas isoladas por serviço
- Evolução tecnológica independente

**Negativas:**
- Complexidade de debugging distribuído
- Eventual consistency em alguns cenários
- Overhead de infraestrutura

**Riscos:**
1. Latência em cadeias de eventos longas
   - Mitigação: Timeouts configuráveis e dead letter queues
2. Perda de eventos
   - Mitigação: Persistência em Kafka com replicação

## REVISÃO:** 2024-04-15
```

### ADR-002: Padrão Event-Driven

```markdown
# ADR-002: Padrão Event-Driven com Kafka

**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead + Especialista Infra

## CONTEXTO:
Necessidade de comunicação desacoplada entre serviços com garantia de entrega e ordenação.

## DECISÃO:
Usar Apache Kafka como message broker com:
- Tópicos por domínio (ex: user.events, task.events)
- Schema Registry para validação de contratos
- Retry policies com exponential backoff
- Dead Letter Queues para eventos não processáveis

## CONSEQUÊNCIAS:
**Positivas:** Desacoplamento total, resiliência a falhas, replay de eventos
**Negativas:** Complexidade operacional, learning curve
```

## 3. Engineering Standards

```markdown
# Engineering Standards - DIYAPP V11

## 1. Padrões de Código

### 1.1 Estrutura de Serviço
```
service-name/
├── src/
│   ├── controllers/
│   ├── services/
│   ├── repositories/
│   ├── models/
│   ├── events/
│   │   ├── producers/
│   │   └── consumers/
│   ├── middleware/
│   └── config/
├── tests/
│   ├── unit/
│   ├── integration/
│   └── e2e/
├── Dockerfile
├── package.json
└── .env.example
```

### 1.2 Convenções de Nomenclatura
- Arquivos: kebab-case (user-service.js)
- Classes: PascalCase (UserService)
- Funções/métodos: camelCase (getUserById)
- Constantes: UPPER_SNAKE_CASE (MAX_RETRY_COUNT)
- Variáveis: camelCase (userProfile)

### 1.3 Padrões de API REST
```
GET    /resources          # Listar
GET    /resources/:id      # Obter por ID
POST   /resources          # Criar
PUT    /resources/:id      # Substituir
PATCH  /resources/:id      # Atualizar parcial
DELETE /resources/:id      # Remover
```

### 1.4 Versionamento de API
- URL versioning: `/api/v1/resources`
- Header versioning: `Accept: application/vnd.diyapp.v1+json`

## 2. Padrões de Commits
- feat: Nova funcionalidade
- fix: Correção de bug
- docs: Documentação
- style: Formatação
- refactor: Refatoração
- test: Testes
- chore: Tarefas de build

Exemplo: `feat(auth): implement JWT authentication`

## 3. Estratégia de Branching
- `main`: Produção
- `staging`: Pré-produção
- `develop`: Desenvolvimento
- `feature/*`: Funcionalidades
- `hotfix/*`: Correções urgentes

## 4. Testes
- Cobertura mínima: 80%
- Testes unitários: Jest
- Testes de integração: Supertest
- E2E: Cypress para front, Newman para APIs

## 5. Segurança
- Secrets em HashiCorp Vault
- Scan de dependências: Snyk/Dependabot
- SAST: SonarQube
- Rate limiting por IP/serviço
```

## 4. Shared Libraries

### 4.1 Logger Library (`shared/libs/logger/index.js`)

```javascript
const winston = require('winston');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');

class Logger {
  constructor(serviceName) {
    this.serviceName = serviceName;
    this.correlationId = uuidv4();
    
    this.logger = winston.createLogger({
      level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
      format: winston.format.combine(
        winston.format.timestamp(),
        winston.format.json()
      ),
      defaultMeta: {
        service: serviceName,
        correlationId: this.correlationId,
        environment: process.env.NODE_ENV
      },
      transports: [
        new winston.transports.Console(),
        new winston.transports.File({ 
          filename: `logs/${serviceName}-error.log`, 
          level: 'error' 
        }),
        new winston.transports.File({ 
          filename: `logs/${serviceName}-combined.log` 
        })
      ]
    });
  }

  setCorrelationId(id) {
    this.correlationId = id;
  }

  info(message, meta = {}) {
    this.logger.info(message, meta);
  }

  error(message, error = null, meta = {}) {
    const logData = {
      ...meta,
      error: error ? {
        message: error.message,
        stack: error.stack,
        code: error.code
      } : null
    };
    this.logger.error(message, logData);
  }

  warn(message, meta = {}) {
    this.logger.warn(message, meta);
  }

  debug(message, meta = {}) {
    this.logger.debug(message, meta);
  }

  // Método para logs estruturados de negócio
  businessLog(eventType, userId, data = {}) {
    this.info(`Business event: ${eventType}`, {
      eventType,
      userId,
      ...data,
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    });
  }
}

module.exports = Logger;
```

### 4.2 Metrics Library (`shared/libs/metrics/index.js`)

```javascript
const client = require('prom-client');

class Metrics {
  constructor() {
    this.register = new client.Registry();
    
    // Métricas padrão do Node.js
    client.collectDefaultMetrics({ register: this.register });
    
    // Métricas customizadas
    this.httpRequestDuration = new client.Histogram({
      name: 'http_request_duration_seconds',
      help: 'Duration of HTTP requests in seconds',
      labelNames: ['method', 'route', 'status_code', 'service'],
      buckets: [0.1, 0.5, 1, 2, 5]
    });

    this.eventProcessingDuration = new client.Histogram({
      name: 'event_processing_duration_seconds',
      help: 'Duration of event processing in seconds',
      labelNames: ['event_type', 'consumer', 'status'],
      buckets: [0.1, 0.5, 1, 2, 5]
    });

    this.databaseQueryDuration = new client.Histogram({
      name: 'database_query_duration_seconds',
      help: 'Duration of database queries in seconds',
      labelNames: ['operation', 'table', 'success'],
      buckets: [0.01, 0.05, 0.1, 0.5, 1]
    });

    this.activeConnections = new client.Gauge({
      name: 'active_connections',
      help: 'Number of active connections',
      labelNames: ['type']
    });

    this.register.registerMetric(this.httpRequestDuration);
    this.register.registerMetric(this.eventProcessingDuration);
    this.register.registerMetric(this.databaseQueryDuration);
    this.register.registerMetric(this.activeConnections);
  }

  startHttpTimer(method, route) {
    return this.httpRequestDuration.startTimer({
      method,
      route,
      service: process.env.SERVICE_NAME
    });
  }

  startEventTimer(eventType, consumer) {
    return this.eventProcessingDuration.startTimer({
      eventType,
      consumer
    });
  }

  startDbTimer(operation, table) {
    return this.databaseQueryDuration.startTimer({
      operation,
      table
    });
  }

  incrementCounter(name, labels = {}, value = 1) {
    let counter = this.register.getSingleMetric(name);
    if (!counter) {
      counter = new client.Counter({
        name,
        help: `Counter for ${name}`,
        labelNames: Object.keys(labels)
      });
      this.register.registerMetric(counter);
    }
    counter.inc(labels, value);
  }

  setGauge(name, value, labels = {}) {
    let gauge = this.register.getSingleMetric(name);
    if (!gauge) {
      gauge = new client.Gauge({
        name,
        help: `Gauge for ${name}`,
        labelNames: Object.keys(labels)
      });
      this.register.registerMetric(gauge);
    }
    gauge.set(labels, value);
  }

  async getMetrics() {
    return this.register.metrics();
  }
}

module.exports = new Metrics();
```

### 4.3 Tracing Library (`shared/libs/tracing/index.js`)

```javascript
const { NodeTracerProvider } = require('@opentelemetry/sdk-trace-node');
const { SimpleSpanProcessor } = require('@opentelemetry/sdk-trace-base');
const { JaegerExporter } = require('@opentelemetry/exporter-jaeger');
const { Resource } = require('@opentelemetry/resources');
const { SemanticResourceAttributes } = require('@opentelemetry/semantic-conventions');
const { trace } = require('@opentelemetry/api');

class Tracing {
  constructor(serviceName) {
    this.serviceName = serviceName;
    this.provider = null;
    this.tracer = null;
  }

  initialize() {
    const provider = new NodeTracerProvider({
      resource: new Resource({
        [SemanticResourceAttributes.SERVICE_NAME]: this.serviceName,
        'deployment.environment': process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development'
      })
    });

    // Exportador Jaeger
    const jaegerExporter = new JaegerExporter({
      endpoint: process.env.JAEGER_ENDPOINT || 'http://localhost:14268/api/traces'
    });

    provider.addSpanProcessor(new SimpleSpanProcessor(jaegerExporter));
    provider.register();

    this.provider = provider;
    this.tracer = trace.getTracer(this.serviceName);
    
    console.log(`Tracing initialized for ${this.serviceName}`);
  }

  startSpan(name, options = {}) {
    if (!this.tracer) {
      this.initialize();
    }
    
    return this.tracer.startSpan(name, {
      attributes: {
        'service.name': this.serviceName,
        'timestamp': new Date().toISOString(),
        ...options.attributes
      },
      ...options
    });
  }

  async withSpan(name, fn, options = {}) {
    const span = this.startSpan(name, options);
    
    try {
      const result = await trace.getSpanContext(span.spanContext()).bind(fn)();
      span.setStatus({ code: 1 }); // OK
      span.end();
      return result;
    } catch (error) {
      span.setStatus({ 
        code: 2, // ERROR
        message: error.message 
      });
      span.recordException(error);
      span.end();
      throw error;
    }
  }

  addEventToSpan(span, name, attributes = {}) {
    span.addEvent(name, attributes);
  }

  getCurrentSpan() {
    return trace.getSpan(trace.contextActive());
  }

  injectContext(carrier, setter) {
    const span = this.getCurrentSpan();
    if (span) {
      const context = trace.setSpan(trace.contextActive(), span);
      const propagator = new W3CTraceContextPropagator();
      propagator.inject(context, carrier, setter);
    }
  }
}

module.exports = Tracing;
```

### 4.4 Events Library (`shared/libs/events/index.js`)

```javascript
const { Kafka, logLevel } = require('kafkajs');
const avro = require('avsc');

class EventBus {
  constructor(serviceName) {
    this.serviceName = serviceName;
    this.kafka = null;
    this.producer = null;
    this.consumers = new Map();
    this.schemas = new Map();
    
    this.initialize();
  }

  initialize() {
    this.kafka = new Kafka({
      clientId: this.serviceName,
      brokers: process.env.KAFKA_BROKERS.split(','),
      logLevel: logLevel.ERROR,
      retry: {
        initialRetryTime: 100,
        retries: 8,
        maxRetryTime: 30000
      }
    });

    this.producer = this.kafka.producer();
  }

  async connect() {
    await this.producer.connect();
    console.log(`Kafka producer connected for ${this.serviceName}`);
  }

  async disconnect() {
    await this.producer.disconnect();
    for (const consumer of this.consumers.values()) {
      await consumer.disconnect();
    }
    console.log(`Kafka disconnected for ${this.serviceName}`);
  }

  // Registrar schema Avro
  registerSchema(eventType, schemaDefinition) {
    const schema = avro.Type.forSchema(schemaDefinition);
    this.schemas.set(eventType, schema);
    return schema;
  }

  // Publicar evento
  async publish(eventType, data, metadata = {}) {
    const eventId = require('crypto').randomUUID();
    const timestamp = new Date().toISOString();
    
    const event = {
      id: eventId,
      type: eventType,
      version: '1.0.0',
      timestamp,
      source: this.serviceName,
      data,
      metadata: {
        correlationId: metadata.correlationId || require('crypto').randomUUID(),
        userId: metadata.userId,
        ...metadata
      }
    };

    // Validar schema se existir
    const schema = this.schemas.get(eventType);
    if (schema) {
      schema.isValid(event);
    }

    const message = {
      value: JSON.stringify(event),
      headers: {
        'event-type': eventType,
        'event-version': '1.0.0',
        'correlation-id': event.metadata.correlationId,
        'timestamp': timestamp
      }
    };

    try {
      await this.producer.send({
        topic: `${eventType}.events`,
        messages: [message]
      });

      console.log(`Event published: ${eventType}`, { eventId });
      return eventId;
    } catch (error) {
      console.error(`Failed to publish event ${eventType}:`, error);
      throw error;
    }
  }

  // Consumir eventos
  async subscribe(eventType, groupId, handler) {
    const consumer = this.kafka.consumer({ 
      groupId: `${groupId}-${this.serviceName}`,
      sessionTimeout: 30000,
      heartbeatInterval: 3000,
      maxBytesPerPartition: 1048576 // 1MB

### [Sessão Paralela: SRE]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Infraestrutura como Código e Monitoramento

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
terraform/
├── environments/
│   ├── staging/
│   │   ├── main.tf
│   │   ├── variables.tf
│   │   ├── outputs.tf
│   │   └── terraform.tfvars.example
│   └── production/
│       ├── main.tf
│       ├── variables.tf
│       ├── outputs.tf
│       └── terraform.tfvars.example
├── modules/
│   ├── vpc/
│   ├── ecs/
│   ├── rds/
│   ├── monitoring/
│   └── s3/
├── scripts/
│   ├── deploy.sh
│   ├── destroy.sh
│   └── validate.sh
└── monitoring/
    ├── prometheus/
    ├── grafana/
    ├── alerts/
    └── dashboards/
```

## 1. Configuração Principal do Terraform

**terraform/environments/staging/main.tf:**
```hcl
terraform {
  required_version = ">= 1.5.0"
  
  required_providers {
    aws = {
      source  = "hashicorp/aws"
      version = "~> 5.0"
    }
    random = {
      source  = "hashicorp/random"
      version = "~> 3.5"
    }
  }
  
  backend "s3" {
    bucket         = "diyapp-terraform-state-staging"
    key            = "terraform.tfstate"
    region         = "us-east-1"
    encrypt        = true
    dynamodb_table = "diyapp-terraform-locks-staging"
  }
}

provider "aws" {
  region = var.aws_region
  
  default_tags {
    tags = {
      Environment = "staging"
      Project     = "DIYAPP"
      ManagedBy   = "Terraform"
      Squad       = "Autonomous-SRE"
    }
  }
}

# Módulo VPC
module "vpc" {
  source = "../../modules/vpc"
  
  environment    = "staging"
  vpc_cidr       = var.vpc_cidr
  azs            = var.availability_zones
  public_subnets = var.public_subnet_cidrs
}

# Módulo ECS (Fargate)
module "ecs" {
  source = "../../modules/ecs"
  
  environment      = "staging"
  vpc_id          = module.vpc.vpc_id
  private_subnets = module.vpc.private_subnet_ids
  public_subnets  = module.vpc.public_subnet_ids
  
  # Configurações específicas do DIYAPP
  api_service_name     = "diyapp-api"
  api_container_image  = var.api_container_image
  api_container_port   = 3000
  api_desired_count    = 2
  api_cpu             = 1024
  api_memory          = 2048
  
  llm_gateway_service_name = "diyapp-llm-gateway"
  llm_gateway_image       = var.llm_gateway_image
  llm_gateway_port        = 8080
  llm_gateway_desired_count = 2
  llm_gateway_cpu         = 2048
  llm_gateway_memory      = 4096
}

# Módulo RDS (PostgreSQL)
module "database" {
  source = "../../modules/rds"
  
  environment    = "staging"
  vpc_id        = module.vpc.vpc_id
  subnet_ids    = module.vpc.private_subnet_ids
  
  db_name       = "diyapp"
  db_username   = var.db_username
  db_instance_class = "db.t3.medium"
  allocated_storage = 20
}

# Módulo de Monitoramento
module "monitoring" {
  source = "../../modules/monitoring"
  
  environment = "staging"
  vpc_id     = module.vpc.vpc_id
  subnet_ids = module.vpc.private_subnet_ids
  
  # Endpoints para health checks
  api_endpoint         = "https://api.staging.diyapp.com/health"
  llm_gateway_endpoint = "https://llm.staging.diyapp.com/health"
  
  # Configurações de SLO
  availability_slo    = 99.9
  latency_slo_p95    = 300
  error_rate_slo     = 0.1
  llm_latency_slo_p95 = 8000
}

# Módulo S3 para assets e logs
module "storage" {
  source = "../../modules/s3"
  
  environment = "staging"
  
  buckets = {
    "diyapp-assets-staging" = {
      versioning = true
      encryption = true
    }
    "diyapp-logs-staging" = {
      versioning = false
      encryption = true
      lifecycle_rules = [
        {
          id      = "log-expiration"
          enabled = true
          expiration_days = 90
        }
      ]
    }
  }
}
```

## 2. Módulo de Monitoramento

**terraform/modules/monitoring/main.tf:**
```hcl
# Prometheus Server
resource "aws_ecs_task_definition" "prometheus" {
  family                   = "prometheus-${var.environment}"
  network_mode            = "awsvpc"
  requires_compatibilities = ["FARGATE"]
  cpu                     = 1024
  memory                  = 2048
  execution_role_arn     = aws_iam_role.ecs_execution_role.arn
  task_role_arn          = aws_iam_role.ecs_task_role.arn
  
  container_definitions = jsonencode([
    {
      name      = "prometheus"
      image     = "prom/prometheus:v2.45.0"
      cpu       = 512
      memory    = 1024
      essential = true
      
      portMappings = [
        {
          containerPort = 9090
          hostPort      = 9090
          protocol      = "tcp"
        }
      ]
      
      environment = [
        {
          name  = "PROMETHEUS_CONFIG_FILE"
          value = "/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml"
        }
      ]
      
      mountPoints = [
        {
          sourceVolume  = "prometheus-config"
          containerPath = "/etc/prometheus"
          readOnly      = true
        },
        {
          sourceVolume  = "prometheus-data"
          containerPath = "/prometheus"
        }
      ]
      
      logConfiguration = {
        logDriver = "awslogs"
        options = {
          "awslogs-group"         = "/ecs/prometheus-${var.environment}"
          "awslogs-region"        = data.aws_region.current.name
          "awslogs-stream-prefix" = "ecs"
        }
      }
    }
  ])
  
  volume {
    name = "prometheus-config"
    
    efs_volume_configuration {
      file_system_id = aws_efs_file_system.prometheus_config.id
      root_directory = "/"
    }
  }
  
  volume {
    name = "prometheus-data"
    
    efs_volume_configuration {
      file_system_id = aws_efs_file_system.prometheus_data.id
      root_directory = "/"
    }
  }
}

          "awslogs-region"        = data.aws_region.current.name
          "awslogs-stream-prefix" = "ecs"
        }
      }
    }
  ])

    name = "grafana-data"

  - "alerts.yml"

        - ${var.api_endpoint}

# Configuração de Alertas do Prometheus
resource "local_file" "prometheus_alerts" {
  filename = "${path.module}/config/alerts.yml"
  
  content = <<-EOT
groups:
  - name: diyapp-slo-alerts
    rules:
      # SLO: Disponibilidade 99.9%
      - alert: APIAvailabilityBelowSLO
        expr: |
          (
            avg_over_time(probe_success{job="blackbox-exporter", instance=~".*api.*"}[5m]) * 100
          ) < ${var.availability_slo}
        for: 5m
        labels:
          severity: critical
          service: api
          slo: availability
        annotations:
          summary: "API availability below SLO (${var.availability_slo}%)"
          description: "API availability is at {{ $value }}% for 5 minutes"
          runbook: "https://runbooks.diyapp.com/api-availability"
      
      # SLO: Latência P95 < 300ms
      - alert: APILatencyAboveSLO
        expr: |
          histogram_quantile(0.95, 
            rate(http_request_duration_seconds_bucket{service="api", method="POST", path!~"/health.*"}[5m])
          ) * 1000 > ${var.latency_slo_p95}
        for: 5m
        labels:
          severity: warning
          service: api
          slo: latency
        annotations:
          summary: "API latency P95 above SLO (${var.latency_slo_p95}ms)"
          description: "API latency P95 is {{ $value }}ms for 5 minutes"
          runbook: "https://runbooks.diyapp.com/api-latency"
      
      # SLO: Error rate < 0.1%
      - alert: APIErrorRateAboveSLO
        expr: |
          (
            rate(http_requests_total{service="api", status=~"5.."}[5m]) 
            / 
            rate(http_requests_total{service="api"}[5m])
          ) * 100 > ${var.error_rate_slo}
        for: 2m
        labels:
          severity: critical
          service: api
          slo: error-rate
        annotations:
          summary: "API error rate above SLO (${var.error_rate_slo}%)"
          description: "API error rate is {{ $value }}% for 2 minutes"
          runbook: "https://runbooks.diyapp.com/api-errors"
      
      # SLO: LLM Latency P95 < 8s
      - alert: LLMLatencyAboveSLO
        expr: |
          histogram_quantile(0.95, 
            rate(llm_request_duration_seconds_bucket{service="llm-gateway"}[5m])
          ) * 1000 > ${var.llm_latency_slo_p95}
        for: 5m
        labels:
          severity: warning
          service: llm-gateway
          slo: llm-latency
        annotations:
          summary: "LLM latency P95 above SLO (${var.llm_latency_slo_p95}ms)"
          description: "LLM latency P95 is {{ $value }}ms for 5 minutes"
          runbook: "https://runbooks.diyapp.com/llm-latency"
      
      # Error Budget Burn Rate Alerts
      - alert: ErrorBudgetBurnRateHigh
        expr: |
          (
            rate(http_requests_total{service="api", status=~"5.."}[1h])
            /
            rate(http_requests_total{service="api"}[1h])
          ) * 100 * 24 > 5  # Burning >5% of monthly budget per hour
        for: 5m
        labels:
          severity: critical
          service: api
          slo: error-budget
        annotations:
          summary: "High error budget burn rate detected"
          description: "Error budget burning at {{ $value }}% per hour"
          runbook: "https://runbooks.diyapp.com/error-budget"
      
      # LLM Provider Availability
      - alert: LLMProviderDegraded
        expr: |
          avg_over_time(llm_provider_availability{provider=~".*"}[5m]) < 95
        for: 5m
        labels:
          severity: warning
          service: llm-gateway
        annotations:
          summary: "LLM Provider availability degraded"
          description: "Provider {{ $labels.provider }} availability at {{ $value }}%"
          runbook: "https://runbooks.diyapp.com/llm-provider-fallback"
      
      # Database Connections
      - alert: DatabaseConnectionHigh
        expr: |
          pg_stat_database_numbackends{datname="diyapp"} > 50
        for: 5m
        labels:
          severity: warning
          service: database
        annotations:
          summary: "High database connections"
          description: "Database connections at {{ $value }}"
          runbook: "https://runbooks.diyapp.com/database-connections"
  
  - name: infrastructure-alerts
    rules:
      - alert: ContainerMemoryHigh
        expr: |
          container_memory_working_set_bytes{container!="", image!=""} / container_spec_memory_limit_bytes > 0.8
        for: 5m
        labels:
          severity: warning
        annotations:
          summary: "Container memory usage high"
          description: "Container {{ $labels.container }} memory usage at {{ $value }}%"
      
      - alert: ContainerCPUHigh
        expr: |
          rate(container_cpu_usage_seconds_total{container!=""}[5m]) > 0.8
        for: 5m
        labels:
          severity: warning
        annotations:
          summary: "Container CPU usage high"
          description: "Container {{ $labels.container }} CPU usage at {{ $value }}%"
      
      - alert: NodeDiskSpaceLow
        expr: |
          node_filesystem_avail_bytes{mountpoint="/"} / node_filesystem_size_bytes{mountpoint="/"} < 0.2
        for: 5m
        labels:
          severity: critical
        annotations:
          summary: "Node disk space low"
          description: "Disk space on {{ $labels.instance }} at {{ $value }}%"
EOT
}

    "dashboard" = {
      "title" = "DIYAPP SLO Dashboard - ${var.en

# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Serviços Backend

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v11-core/
├── api-gateway/
├── auth-service/
├── project-service/

## 1. API Gateway (Node.js + Express)

### `api-gateway/src/index.js`

```javascript
const express = require('express');
const cors = require('cors');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const { createProxyMiddleware } = require('http-proxy-middleware');
const morgan = require('morgan');
const winston = require('winston');
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');

// Configuração de logging estruturado
const logger = winston.createLogger({
  level: 'info',
  format: winston.format.combine(
    winston.format.timestamp(),
    winston.format.json()
  ),
  transports: [
    new winston.transports.Console(),
    new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'logs/api-gateway-error.log', level: 'error' }),
    new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'logs/api-gateway-combined.log' })
  ]
});

const app = express();
const PORT = process.env.API_GATEWAY_PORT || 3000;

// Middlewares de segurança
app.use(helmet());
app.use(cors({
  origin: process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS ? process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS.split(',') : ['http://localhost:8080'],
  credentials: true
}));

// Rate limiting
const limiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutos
  max: 100, // limite por IP
  message: { error: 'Too many requests, please try again later.' },
  standardHeaders: true,
  legacyHeaders: false
});
app.use('/api', limiter);

// Logging estruturado
app.use(morgan((tokens, req, res) => {
  return JSON.stringify({
    correlation_id: req.headers['x-correlation-id'] || 'none',
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    method: tokens.method(req, res),
    url: tokens.url(req, res),
    status: tokens.status(req, res),
    duration_ms: tokens['response-time'](req, res),
    user_agent: req.headers['user-agent'],
    ip: req.ip
  });
}, {
  stream: {
    write: (message) => logger.info('HTTP Request', JSON.parse(message))
  }
}));

// Middleware para adicionar correlation ID
app.use((req, res, next) => {
  req.correlationId = req.headers['x-correlation-id'] || `corr-${Date.now()}-${Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9)}`;
  res.setHeader('X-Correlation-ID', req.correlationId);
  next();
});

// Middleware de autenticação
const authenticateToken = (req, res, next) => {
  const authHeader = req.headers['authorization'];
  const token = authHeader && authHeader.split(' ')[1];

  if (!token) {
    return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Authentication token required' });
  }

  try {
    const decoded = jwt.verify(token, process.env.JWT_SECRET);
    req.user = decoded;
    next();
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error('Token verification failed', {
      correlation_id: req.correlationId,
      error: error.message
    });
    return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Invalid or expired token' });
  }
};

// Health check endpoint
app.get('/health', (req, res) => {
  res.json({
    status: 'healthy',
    service: 'api-gateway',
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    uptime: process.uptime()
  });
});

// Rotas públicas (não requerem autenticação)
app.use('/api/auth', createProxyMiddleware({
  target: `http://${process.env.AUTH_SERVICE_HOST || 'localhost'}:${process.env.AUTH_SERVICE_PORT || 3001}`,
  changeOrigin: true,
  pathRewrite: { '^/api/auth': '' },
  onError: (err, req, res) => {
    logger.error('Auth service proxy error', {
      correlation_id: req.correlationId,
      error: err.message
    });
    res.status(503).json({ error: 'Authentication service temporarily unavailable' });
  },
  timeout: 5000
}));

// Rotas protegidas
const protectedRoutes = ['/api/projects', '/api/users'];

protectedRoutes.forEach(route => {
  app.use(route, authenticateToken, createProxyMiddleware({
    target: `http://${process.env.PROJECT_SERVICE_HOST || 'localhost'}:${process.env.PROJECT_SERVICE_PORT || 3002}`,
    changeOrigin: true,
    pathRewrite: { '^/api': '' },
    onError: (err, req, res) => {
      logger.error('Project service proxy error', {
        correlation_id: req.correlationId,
        route: req.path,
        error: err.message
      });
      res.status(503).json({ error: 'Service temporarily unavailable' });
    },
    timeout: 10000
  }));
});

// Middleware de tratamento de erros
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
  logger.error('Unhandled error', {
    correlation_id: req.correlationId,
    error: err.message,
    stack: err.stack
  });

  res.status(err.status || 500).json({
    error: 'Internal server error',
    correlation_id: req.correlationId
  });
});

// Rota 404
app.use('*', (req, res) => {
  res.status(404).json({
    error: 'Route not found',
    path: req.originalUrl
  });
});

app.listen(PORT, () => {
  logger.info(`API Gateway running on port ${PORT}`);
});

module.exports = app;
```

### `api-gateway/package.json`

```json
{
  "name": "api-gateway",
  "version": "1.0.0",
  "description": "API Gateway for DIYAPP V11",
  "main": "src/index.js",
  "scripts": {
    "start": "node src/index.js",
    "dev": "nodemon src/index.js",
    "test": "jest --coverage",
    "lint": "eslint src/"
  },
  "dependencies": {
    "express": "^4.18.2",
    "cors": "^2.8.5",
    "helmet": "^7.0.0",
    "express-rate-limit": "^6.10.0",
    "http-proxy-middleware": "^2.0.6",
    "morgan": "^1.10.0",
    "winston": "^3.10.0",
    "jsonwebtoken": "^9.0.0",
    "dotenv": "^16.3.1"
  },
  "devDependencies": {
    "nodemon": "^3.0.1",
    "jest": "^29.6.2",
    "supertest": "^6.3.3",
    "eslint": "^8.47.0"
  }
}
```

## 2. Serviço de Autenticação (Node.js + Express + PostgreSQL)

### `auth-service/src/index.js`

```javascript
const express = require('express');
const bcrypt = require('bcryptjs');
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const { Pool } = require('pg');
const crypto = require('crypto');
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const winston = require('winston');
const { body, validationResult } = require('express-validator');

// Configuração de logging
const logger = winston.createLogger({
  level: 'info',
  format: winston.format.combine(
    winston.format.timestamp(),
    winston.format.json()
  ),
  transports: [
    new winston.transports.Console(),
    new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'logs/auth-service-error.log', level: 'error' }),
    new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'logs/auth-service-combined.log' })
  ]
});

// Configuração do banco de dados
const pool = new Pool({
  host: process.env.DB_HOST || 'localhost',
  port: process.env.DB_PORT || 5432,
  database: process.env.DB_NAME || 'diyapp_auth',
  user: process.env.DB_USER || 'postgres',
  password: process.env.DB_PASSWORD || 'postgres',
  max: 20,
  idleTimeoutMillis: 30000,
  connectionTimeoutMillis: 2000
});

// Circuit breaker para o banco de dados
class CircuitBreaker {
  constructor(failureThreshold = 5, resetTimeout = 60000) {
    this.failureThreshold = failureThreshold;
    this.resetTimeout = resetTimeout;
    this.failureCount = 0;
    this.lastFailureTime = null;
    this.state = 'CLOSED';
  }

  async execute(fn) {
    if (this.state === 'OPEN') {
      if (Date.now() - this.lastFailureTime > this.resetTimeout) {
        this.state = 'HALF_OPEN';
      } else {
        throw new Error('Service unavailable (circuit breaker open)');
      }
    }

    try {
      const result = await fn();
      this.success();
      return result;
    } catch (error) {
      this.failure();
      throw error;
    }
  }

  success() {
    this.failureCount = 0;
    this.state = 'CLOSED';
  }

  failure() {
    this.failureCount++;
    this.lastFailureTime = Date.now();
    
    if (this.failureCount >= this.failureThreshold) {
      this.state = 'OPEN';
      logger.error('Circuit breaker opened for database', {
        failureCount: this.failureCount
      });
    }
  }
}

const dbCircuitBreaker = new CircuitBreaker();

const app = express();
const PORT = process.env.AUTH_SERVICE_PORT || 3001;

// Middlewares
app.use(helmet());
app.use(express.json());

// Rate limiting específico para autenticação
const authLimiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000,
  max: 10, // limite baixo para prevenir brute force
  message: { error: 'Too many authentication attempts' },
  skipSuccessfulRequests: true
});

// Health check
app.get('/health', async (req, res) => {
  try {
    await dbCircuitBreaker.execute(() => pool.query('SELECT 1'));
    res.json({
      status: 'healthy',
      service: 'auth-service',
      database: 'connected',
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    });
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(503).json({
      status: 'unhealthy',
      service: 'auth-service',
      database: 'disconnected',
      error: error.message
    });
  }
});

// Registro de usuário
app.post('/register', [
  body('email').isEmail().normalizeEmail(),
  body('password').isLength({ min: 8 }),
  body('name').trim().notEmpty()
], async (req, res) => {
  const errors = validationResult(req);
  if (!errors.isEmpty()) {
    return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
  }

  const { email, password, name } = req.body;
  const correlationId = req.headers['x-correlation-id'];

  try {
    // Verifica se usuário já existe
    const existingUser = await dbCircuitBreaker.execute(() =>
      pool.query('SELECT id FROM users WHERE email = $1', [email])
    );

    if (existingUser.rows.length > 0) {
      return res.status(409).json({ error: 'User already exists' });
    }

    // Hash da senha
    const salt = await bcrypt.genSalt(10);
    const passwordHash = await bcrypt.hash(password, salt);

    // Insere usuário
    const result = await dbCircuitBreaker.execute(() =>
      pool.query(
        'INSERT INTO users (email, password_hash, name, created_at) VALUES ($1, $2, $3, NOW()) RETURNING id, email, name',
        [email, passwordHash, name]
      )
    );

    const user = result.rows[0];
    
    // Gera token JWT
    const token = jwt.sign(
      { userId: user.id, email: user.email },
      process.env.JWT_SECRET,
      { expiresIn: '24h' }
    );

    // Log seguro (mascara dados sensíveis)
    logger.info('User registered successfully', {
      correlation_id: correlationId,
      user_id: user.id,
      email: email.replace(/(?<=.).(?=.*@)/g, '*') // mascara email
    });

    res.status(201).json({
      user: {
        id: user.id,
        email: user.email,
        name: user.name
      },
      token
    });
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error('Registration failed', {
      correlation_id: correlationId,
      error: error.message,
      email: email.replace(/(?<=.).(?=.*@)/g, '*')
    });
    
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Registration failed' });
  }
});

// Login
app.post('/login', authLimiter, [
  body('email').isEmail().normalizeEmail(),
  body('password').notEmpty()
], async (req, res) => {
  const errors = validationResult(req);
  if (!errors.isEmpty()) {
    return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
  }

  const { email, password } = req.body;
  const correlationId = req.headers['x-correlation-id'];

  try {
    // Busca usuário
    const result = await dbCircuitBreaker.execute(() =>
      pool.query(
        'SELECT id, email, password_hash, name FROM users WHERE email = $1',
        [email]
      )
    );

    if (result.rows.length === 0) {
      // Delay artificial para prevenir timing attacks
      await bcrypt.compare(password, '$2a$10$fakehashforsecurity');
      return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid credentials' });
    }

    const user = result.rows[0];

    // Verifica senha
    const isValidPassword = await bcrypt.compare(password, user.password_hash);
    if (!isValidPassword) {
      return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid credentials' });
    }

    // Gera token JWT
    const token = jwt.sign(
      { userId: user.id, email: user.email },
      process.env.JWT_SECRET,
      { expiresIn: '24h' }
    );

    // Atualiza último login
    await dbCircuitBreaker.execute(() =>
      pool.query('UPDATE users SET last_login = NOW() WHERE id = $1', [user.id])
    );

    logger.info('User logged in successfully', {
      correlation_id: correlationId,
      user_id: user.id,
      email: email.replace(/(?<=.).(?=.*@)/g, '*')
    });

    res.json({
      user: {
        id: user.id,
        email: user.email,
        name: user.name
      },
      token
    });
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error('Login failed', {
      correlation_id: correlationId,
      error: error.message,
      email: email.replace(/(?<=.).(?=.*@)/g, '*')
    });
    
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Login failed' });
  }
});

// Validação de token
app.post('/validate', async (req, res) => {
  const { token } = req.body;
  const correlationId = req.headers['x-correlation-id'];

  if (!token) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Token required' });
  }

  try {
    const decoded = jwt.verify(token, process.env.JWT_SECRET);
    
    // Verifica se usuário ainda existe
    const result = await dbCircuitBreaker.execute(() =>
      pool.query('SELECT id FROM users WHERE id = $1', [decoded.userId])
    );

    if (result.rows.length === 0) {
      return res.status(401).json({ valid: false, error: 'User not found' });
    }

    res.json({ valid: true, user: decoded });
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error('Token validation failed', {
      correlation_id: correlationId,
      error: error.message
    });
    
    res.json({ valid: false, error: error.message });
  }
});

// Refresh token
app.post('/refresh', async (req, res) => {
  const { refreshToken } = req.body;
  const correlationId = req.headers['x-correlation-id'];

  if (!refreshToken) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Refresh token required' });
  }

  try {
    // Verifica refresh token no banco
    const result = await dbCircuitBreaker.execute(() =>
      pool.query(
        `SELECT u.id, u.email 
         FROM refresh_tokens rt 
         JOIN users u ON rt.user_id = u.id 
         WHERE rt.token = $1 AND rt.expires_at > NOW()`,
        [refreshToken]
      )
    );

    if (result.rows.length === 0) {
      return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid refresh token' });
    }

    const user = result.rows[0];
    
    // Gera novo token
    const newToken = jwt.sign(
      { userId: user.id, email: user.email },
      process.env.JWT_SECRET,
      { expiresIn: '24h' }
    );

    // Gera novo refresh token
    const newRefreshToken = crypto.randomBytes(40).toString('hex');
    
    await dbCircuitBreaker.execute(() =>
      pool.query(
        `INSERT INTO refresh_tokens (user_id, token, expires_at) 
         VALUES ($1, $2, NOW() + INTERVAL '30 days')`,
        [user.id, newRefreshToken]
      )
    );

    res.json({
      token: newToken,
      refreshToken: newRefreshToken
    });
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error('Token refresh failed', {
      correlation_id: correlationId,
      error: error.message
    });
    
    res.status(500).json({ error: '

### [Sessão Paralela: Frontend]
Vou construir uma aplicação React robusta com TypeScript, implementando sistema de design, roteamento, estado global e consumo de APIs seguindo os padrões sênior estabelecidos.

```typescript
// src/main.tsx
import React from 'react'
import ReactDOM from 'react-dom/client'
import { BrowserRouter } from 'react-router-dom'
import { QueryClient, QueryClientProvider } from 'react-query'
import { ReactQueryDevtools } from 'react-query/devtools'
import App from './App'
import './index.css'

// Create a client for React Query with error handling
const queryClient = new QueryClient({
  defaultOptions: {
    queries: {
      retry: 2,
      retryDelay: (attemptIndex) => Math.min(1000 * 2 ** attemptIndex, 30000),
      staleTime: 5 * 60 * 1000, // 5 minutes
      refetchOnWindowFocus: false,
    },
  },
})

ReactDOM.createRoot(document.getElementById('root')!).render(
  <React.StrictMode>
    <BrowserRouter>
      <QueryClientProvider client={queryClient}>
        <App />
        {process.env.NODE_ENV === 'development' && (
          <ReactQueryDevtools initialIsOpen={false} />
        )}
      </QueryClientProvider>
    </BrowserRouter>
  </React.StrictMode>
)
```

```typescript
// src/App.tsx
import React from 'react'
import { Routes, Route, Navigate } from 'react-router-dom'
import { ErrorBoundary } from 'react-error-boundary'
import Layout from '@components/Layout/Layout'
import DashboardPage from '@pages/DashboardPage'
import ProjectsPage from '@pages/ProjectsPage'
import SettingsPage from '@pages/SettingsPage'
import NotFoundPage from '@pages/NotFoundPage'
import ErrorFallback from '@components/Error/ErrorFallback'
import { AppProvider } from '@contexts/AppContext'

const App: React.FC = () => {
  return (
    <ErrorBoundary
      FallbackComponent={ErrorFallback}
      onReset={() => window.location.reload()}
    >
      <AppProvider>
        <Routes>
          <Route path="/" element={<Layout />}>
            <Route index element={<Navigate to="/dashboard" replace />} />
            <Route path="dashboard" element={<DashboardPage />} />
            <Route path="projects" element={<ProjectsPage />} />
            <Route path="projects/:projectId" element={<ProjectsPage />} />
            <Route path="settings" element={<SettingsPage />} />
            <Route path="404" element={<NotFoundPage />} />
            <Route path="*" element={<Navigate to="/404" replace />} />
          </Route>
        </Routes>
      </AppProvider>
    </ErrorBoundary>
  )
}

export default App
```

```typescript
// src/components/Navigation/Navigation.tsx
import React, { useState } from 'react'
import { NavLink } from 'react-router-dom'
import { 
  HomeIcon, 
  FolderIcon, 
  Cog6ToothIcon,
  ChevronLeftIcon,
  ChevronRightIcon 
} from '@heroicons/react/24/outline'
import clsx from 'clsx'

const navigation = [
  { name: 'Dashboard', href: '/dashboard', icon: HomeIcon },
  { name: 'Projects', href: '/projects', icon: FolderIcon },
  { name: 'Settings', href: '/settings', icon: Cog6ToothIcon },
]

const Navigation: React.FC = () => {
  const [collapsed, setCollapsed] = useState(false)

  return (
    <div
      className={clsx(
        'fixed inset-y-0 z-50 flex flex-col bg-white border-r border-neutral-200 transition-all duration-300',
        collapsed ? 'w-20' : 'w-72'
      )}
    >
      {/* Logo */}
      <div className="flex items-center h-16 px-6 border-b border-neutral-200">
        <div className="flex items-center space-x-3">
          <div className="w-8 h-8 bg-primary-600 rounded-lg" />
          {!collapsed && (
            <span className="text-xl font-semibold text-neutral-900">
              DIYAPP V11
            </span>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Navigation Items */}
      <nav className="flex-1 px-4 py-6 space-y-1 overflow-y-auto">
        {navigation.map((item) => (
          <NavLink
            key={item.name}
            to={item.href}
            className={({ isActive }) =>
              clsx(
                'group flex items-center px-3 py-2 text-sm font-medium rounded-lg transition-colors',
                'hover:bg-neutral-100 hover:text-neutral-900',
                isActive
                  ? 'bg-primary-50 text-primary-700'
                  : 'text-neutral-700',
                collapsed ? 'justify-center' : ''
              )
            }
          >
            {({ isActive }) => (
              <>
                <item.icon
                  className={clsx(
                    'flex-shrink-0 w-5 h-5 transition-colors',
                    isActive ? 'text-primary-700' : 'text-neutral-500',
                    'group-hover:text-neutral-900',
                    collapsed ? 'mr-0' : 'mr-3'
                  )}
                  aria-hidden="true"
                />
                {!collapsed && <span>{item.name}</span>}
              </>
            )}
          </NavLink>
        ))}
      </nav>

      {/* Collapse Toggle */}
      <div className="p-4 border-t border-neutral-200">
        <button
          onClick={() => setCollapsed(!collapsed)}
          className="flex items-center justify-center w-full px-3 py-2 text-sm font-medium text-neutral-700 rounded-lg hover:bg-neutral-100 hover:text-neutral-900 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-primary-500 focus:ring-offset-2"
          aria-label={collapsed ? 'Expand navigation' : 'Collapse navigation'}
        >
          {collapsed ? (
            <ChevronRightIcon className="w-5 h-5" />
          ) : (
            <>
              <ChevronLeftIcon className="w-5 h-5 mr-2" />
              <span>Collapse</span>
            </>
          )}
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}

export default Navigation
```
