### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
```javascript
// ==============================================
// DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core Architecture
// Technical Leader: Arquitetura de Microsserviços
// ==============================================

// ADR-001: Arquitetura de Microsserviços V11
// Data: 2024-01-15
// Status: Aceita
// Autores: Tech Lead + Especialista Infra

/**
 * CONTEXTO:
 * A V10 do DIYAPP atingiu limites de escalabilidade com arquitetura monolítica.
 * Necessidade de:
 * 1. Deploy independente por funcionalidade
 * 2. Isolamento de falhas
 * 3. Escala granular por serviço
 * 4. Time-to-market reduzido para novas features
 * 
 * DECISÃO:
 * Adotar arquitetura de microsserviços com 6 serviços core + API Gateway.
 * Cada serviço é responsável por um domínio específico.
 * Comunicação via HTTP/REST para síncrono, RabbitMQ para assíncrono.
 * 
 * OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:
 * - Opção A: Monólito modularizado - Prós: Simples deploy, Contras: Escala limitada
 * - Opção B: Microsserviços completos - Prós: Escala ilimitada, Contras: Complexidade operacional
 * - Opção C: Arquitetura híbrida - Prós: Balanceado, Contras: Gerenciamento misto
 * 
 * Escolhida: Opção B com simplificações operacionais
 */

// ==============================================
// 1. ESTRUTURA DO REPOSITÓRIO
// ==============================================

/**
 * diyapp-v11/
 * ├── .github/
 * │   ├── workflows/
 * │   │   ├── ci-services.yml
 * │   │   ├── cd-canary.yml
 * │   │   └── security-scan.yml
 * │   └── PULL_REQUEST_TEMPLATE.md
 * ├── api-gateway/
 * │   ├── src/
 * │   ├── tests/
 * │   ├── Dockerfile
 * │   └── package.json
 * ├── services/
 * │   ├── auth-service/
 * │   ├── user-service/
 * │   ├── project-service/
 * │   ├── payment-service/
 * │   ├── notification-service/
 * │   └── analytics-service/
 * ├── shared/
 * │   ├── libs/
 * │   │   ├── logger/
 * │   │   ├── metrics/
 * │   │   └── database/
 * │   └── contracts/
 * │       ├── openapi/
 * │       └── protobuf/
 * ├── infrastructure/
 * │   ├── k8s/
 * │   ├── terraform/
 * │   └── monitoring/
 * ├── docs/
 * │   ├── adrs/
 * │   └── engineering-standards.md
 * └── docker-compose.yml
 */

// ==============================================
// 2. ENGINEERING STANDARDS (engineering-standards.md)
// ==============================================

const engineeringStandards = `
# DIYAPP V11 - Engineering Standards

## 1. Padrões de Código

### 1.1 Linguagens
- Backend: Node.js 18+ (TypeScript obrigatório)
- Frontend: React 18+ (TypeScript)
- Mobile: React Native 0.72+

### 1.2 Estrutura de Serviço
\`\`\`
service-name/
├── src/
│   ├── controllers/     # Handlers HTTP
│   ├── services/       # Lógica de negócio
│   ├── repositories/   # Acesso a dados
│   ├── models/         # Entidades/DTOs
│   ├── middleware/     # Auth, logging, validation
│   ├── config/         # Configurações
│   ├── utils/          # Funções utilitárias
│   └── index.ts        # Ponto de entrada
├── tests/
│   ├── unit/
│   ├── integration/
│   └── e2e/
├── Dockerfile
├── docker-compose.yml (dev)
├── package.json
└── tsconfig.json
\`\`\`

### 1.3 Convenções de Nomenclatura
- Classes: PascalCase (UserService)
- Funções/Métodos: camelCase (getUserById)
- Variáveis: camelCase (userData)
- Constantes: UPPER_SNAKE_CASE (MAX_RETRIES)
- Arquivos: kebab-case (user-controller.ts)
- Interfaces: Prefixo I (IUser)
- Types: Suffixo Type (UserType)

### 1.4 Commits (Conventional Commits)
\`\`\`
feat: add user registration endpoint
fix: resolve memory leak in image processing
docs: update API documentation
style: format code with prettier
refactor: simplify authentication logic
test: add unit tests for payment service
chore: update dependencies
perf: optimize database queries
\`\`\`

## 2. Padrões de API

### 2.1 REST Guidelines
- Versionamento: /api/v1/resource
- Métodos HTTP semânticos
- Plural para collections: /users não /user
- Nested resources: /users/{id}/projects
- Paginação: ?page=1&limit=20
- Filtros: ?status=active&created_after=2024-01-01
- Ordenação: ?sort=-created_at,name

### 2.2 Response Format
\`\`\`json
{
  "success": true,
  "data": {},
  "meta": {
    "timestamp": "2024-01-15T10:30:00Z",
    "version": "v1",
    "pagination": {
      "page": 1,
      "limit": 20,
      "total": 100
    }
  },
  "error": null
}
\`\`\`

### 2.3 Error Handling
- 400: Bad Request (validation errors)
- 401: Unauthorized (no auth token)
- 403: Forbidden (insufficient permissions)
- 404: Not Found
- 409: Conflict (duplicate resource)
- 422: Unprocessable Entity
- 429: Too Many Requests
- 500: Internal Server Error

## 3. Banco de Dados

### 3.1 Strategy
- PostgreSQL para dados relacionais
- MongoDB para dados não estruturados
- Redis para cache e session
- Cada serviço tem seu próprio banco

### 3.2 Migrations
- Usar TypeORM migrations
- Versionar migrations no Git
- Testar migrations em staging
- Rollback sempre possível

## 4. Segurança

### 4.1 Autenticação
- JWT com refresh tokens
- Tokens expiram em 15 minutos
- Refresh tokens expiram em 7 dias
- Rate limiting por IP/user

### 4.2 Validação
- Zod para schema validation
- Sanitize inputs contra XSS
- Validate file uploads
- Use parameterized queries

## 5. Performance

### 5.1 Targets
- P95 latency: < 200ms
- Availability: 99.95%
- Error rate: < 0.1%
- Throughput: 1000 req/s por serviço

### 5.2 Otimizações
- Connection pooling (PgBouncer)
- Query optimization (EXPLAIN ANALYZE)
- Caching estratégico (Redis)
- CDN para assets estáticos
`;

// ==============================================
// 3. CI/CD PIPELINE (.github/workflows/ci-services.yml)
// ==============================================

const ciCdPipeline = `
name: CI/CD Services

on:
  push:
    branches: [main, develop]
  pull_request:
    branches: [main]

jobs:
  test-and-build:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    strategy:
      matrix:
        service: [auth, user, project, payment, notification, analytics, gateway]
    
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v3
    
    - name: Setup Node.js
      uses: actions/setup-node@v3
      with:
        node-version: '18'
        cache: 'npm'
        cache-dependency-path: ./services/${{ matrix.service }}/package-lock.json
    
    - name: Install dependencies
      run: |
        cd ./services/${{ matrix.service }}
        npm ci --audit=false
    
    - name: Run linter
      run: |
        cd ./services/${{ matrix.service }}
        npm run lint
    
    - name: Run unit tests
      run: |
        cd ./services/${{ matrix.service }}
        npm test -- --coverage
        # Fail if coverage < 80%
        if [ $(node -p "require('./coverage/coverage-summary.json').total.lines.pct") -lt 80 ]; then exit 1; fi
    
    - name: Security scan
      uses: snyk/actions/node@master
      env:
        SNYK_TOKEN: \${{ secrets.SNYK_TOKEN }}
      with:
        args: --severity-threshold=high
    
    - name: Build Docker image
      run: |
        cd ./services/${{ matrix.service }}
        docker build -t diyapp/${{ matrix.service }}-service:\${{ github.sha }} .
    
    - name: Push to Registry
      if: github.event_name == 'push' && github.ref == 'refs/heads/main'
      run: |
        echo \${{ secrets.DOCKER_PASSWORD }} | docker login -u \${{ secrets.DOCKER_USERNAME }} --password-stdin
        docker push diyapp/${{ matrix.service }}-service:\${{ github.sha }}
        docker tag diyapp/${{ matrix.service }}-service:\${{ github.sha }} diyapp/${{ matrix.service }}-service:latest
        docker push diyapp/${{ matrix.service }}-service:latest

  deploy-canary:
    needs: test-and-build
    if: github.event_name == 'push' && github.ref == 'refs/heads/main'
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    
    steps:
    - name: Deploy canary (10%)
      run: |
        kubectl set image deployment/${{ matrix.service }}-deployment \
          ${{ matrix.service }}-container=diyapp/${{ matrix.service }}-service:\${{ github.sha }} \
          --namespace production \
          --patch='{"spec": {"replicas": 1}}'
    
    - name: Run smoke tests
      run: |
        ./scripts/smoke-test.sh
    
    - name: Monitor canary metrics
      run: |
        ./scripts/check-metrics.sh --service=${{ matrix.service }} --duration=5m
    
    - name: Full rollout
      if: success()
      run: |
        kubectl scale deployment/${{ matrix.service }}-deployment --replicas=10 --namespace production
`;

// ==============================================
// 4. API GATEWAY CONFIG (api-gateway/src/config/gateway.config.ts)
// ==============================================

const apiGatewayConfig = `
import { Express } from 'express';
import { createProxyMiddleware } from 'http-proxy-middleware';
import rateLimit from 'express-rate-limit';
import helmet from 'helmet';
import cors from 'cors';
import { logger } from '@diyapp/shared/logger';
import { metrics } from '@diyapp/shared/metrics';

export interface ServiceConfig {
  name: string;
  url: string;
  path: string;
  rateLimit?: number;
  timeout?: number;
}

const services: ServiceConfig[] = [
  {
    name: 'auth-service',
    url: process.env.AUTH_SERVICE_URL || 'http://auth-service:3001',
    path: '/api/v1/auth/**',
    rateLimit: 100, // requests per minute
    timeout: 5000
  },
  {
    name: 'user-service',
    url: process.env.USER_SERVICE_URL || 'http://user-service:3002',
    path: '/api/v1/users/**',
    rateLimit: 200,
    timeout: 3000
  },
  {
    name: 'project-service',
    url: process.env.PROJECT_SERVICE_URL || 'http://project-service:3003',
    path: '/api/v1/projects/**',
    rateLimit: 150,
    timeout: 10000
  },
  {
    name: 'payment-service',
    url: process.env.PAYMENT_SERVICE_URL || 'http://payment-service:3004',
    path: '/api/v1/payments/**',
    rateLimit: 50,
    timeout: 8000
  },
  {
    name: 'notification-service',
    url: process.env.NOTIFICATION_SERVICE_URL || 'http://notification-service:3005',
    path: '/api/v1/notifications/**',
    rateLimit: 300,
    timeout: 3000
  },
  {
    name: 'analytics-service',
    url: process.env.ANALYTICS_SERVICE_URL || 'http://analytics-service:3006',
    path: '/api/v1/analytics/**',
    rateLimit: 500,
    timeout: 2000
  }
];

export const configureGateway = (app: Express): void => {
  // Security middleware
  app.use(helmet());
  app.use(cors({
    origin: process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS?.split(',') || ['http://localhost:3000'],
    credentials: true
  }));
  
  // Global rate limiting
  app.use(rateLimit({
    windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
    max: 1000, // limit each IP to 1000 requests per windowMs
    message: 'Too many requests from this IP, please try again later.'
  }));
  
  // Health check endpoint
  app.get('/health', (req, res) => {
    res.json({
      status: 'healthy',
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      version: process.env.VERSION || 'v1.0.0',
      services: services.map(s => s.name)
    });
  });
  
  // Metrics endpoint (Prometheus format)
  app.get('/metrics', async (req, res) => {
    res.set('Content-Type', metrics.register.contentType);
    res.end(await metrics.register.metrics());
  });
  
  // Configure proxy for each service
  services.forEach(service => {
    const limiter = rateLimit({
      windowMs: 60 * 1000, // 1 minute
      max: service.rateLimit || 100,
      message: \`Too many requests to \${service.name}, please slow down.\`
    });
    
    app.use(
      service.path,
      limiter,
      createProxyMiddleware({
        target: service.url,
        changeOrigin: true,
        timeout: service.timeout || 5000,
        onProxyReq: (proxyReq, req, res) => {
          // Add request ID for tracing
          const requestId = req.headers['x-request-id'] || crypto.randomUUID();
          proxyReq.setHeader('X-Request-ID', requestId);
          proxyReq.setHeader('X-Forwarded-For', req.ip);
          
          // Log request
          logger.info('proxy_request', {
            service: service.name,
            method: req.method,
            path: req.path,
            requestId,
            ip: req.ip
          });
        },
        onProxyRes: (proxyRes, req, res) => {
          // Record metrics
          const duration = Date.now() - (req as any)._startTime;
          metrics.httpRequestDuration.observe(
            { service: service.name, method: req.method, status: proxyRes.statusCode },
            duration / 1000
          );
          
          metrics.httpRequestsTotal.inc({
            service: service.name,
            method: req.method,
            status: proxyRes.statusCode
          });
        },
        onError: (err, req, res) => {
          logger.error('proxy_error', {
            service: service.name,
            error: err.message,
            path: req.path,
            requestId: req.headers['x-request-id']
          });
          
          metrics.httpErrorsTotal.inc({ service: service.name });
          
          res.status(503).json({
            success: false,
            error: {
              code: 'SERVICE_UNAVAILABLE',
              message: \`\${service.name} is temporarily unavailable\`,
              requestId: req.headers['x-request-id']
            }
          });
        }
      })
    );
  });
  
  // 404 handler
  app.use('*', (req, res) => {
    res.status(404).json({
      success: false,
      error: {
        code: 'NOT_FOUND',
        message: \`Route \${req.originalUrl} not found\`
      }
    });
  });
};
`;

// ==============================================
// 5. SHARED LIBRARIES (shared/libs/logger/index.ts)
// ==============================================

const sharedLogger = `
import winston from 'winston';
import { v4 as uuidv4 } from 'uuid';

export interface LogContext {
  requestId?: string;
  userId?: string;
  service?: string;
  [key: string]: any;
}

class Logger {
  private logger: winston.Logger;
  private context: LogContext = {};

  constructor(serviceName: string) {
    this.logger = winston.createLogger({
      level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
      defaultMeta: { service: serviceName },
      format: winston.format.combine(
        winston.format.timestamp(),
        winston.format.errors({ stack: true }),
        winston.format.json()
      ),
      transports: [
        new winston.transports.Console({
          format: winston.format.combine(
            winston.format.colorize(),
            winston.format.printf(({ timestamp, level, message, ...meta }) => {
              return \`\${timestamp} [\${serviceName}] \${level}: \${message} \${JSON.stringify(meta)}\`;
            })
          )
        }),
        new winston.transports.File({ 
          filename: 'logs/error.log', 
          level: 'error',
          maxsize: 5242880, // 5MB
          maxFiles: 5
        }),
        new winston.transports.File({ 
          filename: 'logs/combined.log',
          maxsize: 

### [Sessão Paralela: UX Designer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Sistema de Design e Protótipo

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v11-design-system/
├── index.html              # Dashboard principal
├── design-tokens.css       # Sistema de tokens de design
├── design-system.html      # Documentação do Design System
├── prototype.js            # Lógica do protótipo interativo
├── styles.css             # Estilos principais
├── wireframes/
│   ├── dashboard.html     # Wireframe hi-fi do dashboard
│   ├── onboarding.html    # Fluxo de onboarding
│   ├── ai-workflow.html   # Fluxo de IA
│   └── settings.html      # Configurações
└── assets/
    └── icons/             # Ícones do sistema
```

/* ===== ESTADOS DE CARREGAMENTO ===== */
.skeleton {
  background: linear-gradient(
    90deg,
    var(--color-gray-100) 25%,
    var(--color-gray-200) 50%,
    var(--color-gray-100) 75%
  );
  background-size: 200% 100%;
  animation: loading 1.5s infinite;
  border-radius: var(--radius-base);
}

```typescript
// src/hooks/useLazyLoading.ts
import { useEffect, useRef, useState, useCallback } from 'react';

interface UseLazyLoadingOptions {
  rootMargin?: string;
  threshold?: number | number[];
  enabled?: boolean;
}

export function useLazyLoading<T extends HTMLElement = HTMLElement>(
  options: UseLazyLoadingOptions = {}
) {
  const { rootMargin = '50px', threshold = 0, enabled = true } = options;
  const [isVisible, setIsVisible] = useState(false);
  const elementRef = useRef<T>(null);

  const handleIntersection = useCallback(
    (entries: IntersectionObserverEntry[]) => {
      const [entry] = entries;
      if (entry.isIntersecting) {
        setIsVisible(true);
      }
    },
    []
  );

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!enabled || !elementRef.current) return;

    const observer = new IntersectionObserver(handleIntersection, {
      rootMargin,
      threshold
    });

    observer.observe(elementRef.current);

    return () => {
      if (elementRef.current) {
        observer.unobserve(elementRef.current);
      }
    };
  }, [enabled, rootMargin, threshold, handleIntersection]);

  return { elementRef, isVisible };
}
```

```typescript
// src/hooks/useVirtualList.ts
import { useEffect, useRef, useState, useCallback, useMemo } from 'react';

interface VirtualListOptions<T> {
  items: T[];
  itemHeight: number;
  overscan?: number;
  containerHeight: number;
}

interface VirtualItem<T> {
  index: number;
  data: T;
  offsetTop: number;
}

export function useVirtualList<T>({
  items,
  itemHeight,
  overscan = 3,
  containerHeight
}: VirtualListOptions<T>) {
  const containerRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
  const [scrollTop, setScrollTop] = useState(0);

  const handleScroll = useCallback(() => {
    if (containerRef.current) {
      setScrollTop(containerRef.current.scrollTop);
    }
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    const container = containerRef.current;
    if (!container) return;

    container.addEventListener('scroll', handleScroll, { passive: true });
    return () => container.removeEventListener('scroll', handleScroll);
  }, [handleScroll]);

  const virtualItems = useMemo(() => {
    const startIndex = Math.max(
      0,
      Math.floor(scrollTop / itemHeight) - overscan
    );
    const visibleItemCount = Math.ceil(containerHeight / itemHeight);
    const endIndex = Math.min(
      items.length - 1,
      startIndex + visibleItemCount + overscan * 2
    );

    const itemsToRender: VirtualItem<T>[] = [];
    for (let i = startIndex; i <= endIndex; i++) {
      itemsToRender.push({
        index: i,
        data: items[i],
        offsetTop: i * itemHeight
      });
    }

    return itemsToRender;
  }, [items, scrollTop, itemHeight, overscan, containerHeight]);

  const totalHeight = items.length * itemHeight;

  return {
    containerRef,
    virtualItems,
    totalHeight,
    startIndex: virtualItems[0]?.index || 0,
    endIndex: virtualItems[virtualItems.length - 1]?.index || 0
  };
}
```

```typescript
// src/components/Button/Button.tsx
import React, { forwardRef, ButtonHTMLAttributes } from 'react';
import { tokens } from '../../tokens';
import { useButtonA11y } from '../../hooks/useButtonA11y';

export type ButtonVariant = 'primary' | 'secondary' | 'ghost' | 'danger';
export type ButtonSize = 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg';

export interface ButtonProps extends ButtonHTMLAttributes<HTMLButtonElement> {
  variant?: ButtonVariant;
  size?: ButtonSize;
  loading?: boolean;
  fullWidth?: boolean;
  leftIcon?: React.ReactNode;
  rightIcon?: React.ReactNode;
}

const Button = forwardRef<HTMLButtonElement, ButtonProps>(
  (
    {
      variant = 'primary',
      size = 'md',
      loading = false,
      fullWidth = false,
      leftIcon,
      rightIcon,
      children,
      disabled,
      className = '',
      ...props
    },
    ref
  ) => {
    const { buttonProps, isPressed } = useButtonA11y({
      disabled: disabled || loading,
      ...props
    });

    const baseStyles = {
      display: 'inline-flex',
      alignItems: 'center',
      justifyContent: 'center',
      fontFamily: tokens.typography.fontFamily.sans,
      fontWeight: tokens.typography.fontWeight.semibold,
      border: '1px solid transparent',
      borderRadius: tokens.borderRadius.base,
      cursor: disabled || loading ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer',
      transition: 'all 150ms ease-in-out',
      outline: 'none',
      width: fullWidth ? '100%' : 'auto',
      position: 'relative',
      overflow: 'hidden'
    };

    const sizeStyles = {
      sm: {
        fontSize: tokens.typography.fontSize.sm,
        padding: `${tokens.spacing[1]} ${tokens.spacing[3]}`,
        gap: tokens.spacing[1]
      },
      md: {
        fontSize: tokens.typography.fontSize.base,
        padding: `${tokens.spacing[2]} ${tokens.spacing[4]}`,
        gap: tokens.spacing[2]
      },
      lg: {
        fontSize: tokens.typography.fontSize.lg,
        padding: `${tokens.spacing[3]} ${tokens.spacing[6]}`,
        gap: tokens.spacing[3]
      }
    };

    const variantStyles = {
      primary: {
        backgroundColor: tokens.colors.primary[600],
        color: 'white',
        '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
          backgroundColor: tokens.colors.primary[700]
        },
        '&:focus-visible': {
          boxShadow: `0 0 0 3px ${tokens.colors.primary[200]}`
        },
        '&:active:not(:disabled)': {
          backgroundColor: tokens.colors.primary[800]
        }
      },
      secondary: {
        backgroundColor: tokens.colors.neutral[100],
        color: tokens.colors.neutral[800],
        borderColor: tokens.colors.neutral[300],
        '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
          backgroundColor: tokens.colors.neutral[200]
        },
        '&:focus-visible': {
          boxShadow: `0 0 0 3px ${tokens.colors.neutral[300]}`
        },
        '&:active:not(:disabled)': {
          backgroundColor: tokens.colors.neutral[300]
        }
      },
      ghost: {
        backgroundColor: 'transparent',
        color: tokens.colors.neutral[700],
        '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
          backgroundColor: tokens.colors.neutral[100]
        },
        '&:focus-visible': {
          boxShadow: `0 0 0 3px ${tokens.colors.neutral[300]}`
        },
        '&:active:not(:disabled)': {
          backgroundColor: tokens.colors.neutral[200]
        }
      },
      danger: {
        backgroundColor: tokens.colors.error[600],
        color: 'white',
        '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
          backgroundColor: tokens.colors.error[700]
        },
        '&:focus-visible': {
          boxShadow: `0 0 0 3px ${tokens.colors.error[200]}`
        },
        '&:active:not(:disabled)': {
          backgroundColor: tokens.colors.error[800]
        }
      }
    };

    const disabledStyles = {
      opacity: 0.6,
      cursor: 'not-allowed'
    };

    const pressedStyles = isPressed
      ? {
          transform: 'scale(0.98)',
          transition: 'transform 100ms ease'
        }
      : {};

    const style = {
      ...baseStyles,
      ...sizeStyles[size],
      ...variantStyles[variant],
      ...(disabled || loading ? disabledStyles : {}),
      ...pressedStyles
    };

    return (
      <button
        ref={ref}
        style={style}
        className={`diyapp-button ${className}`}
        disabled={disabled || loading}
        aria-busy={loading}
        {...buttonProps}
        {...props}
      >
        {loading && (
          <span
            style={{
              position: 'absolute',
              left: 0,
              top: 0,
              right: 0,
              bottom: 0,
              backgroundColor: 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.8)',
              display: 'flex',
              alignItems: 'center',
              justifyContent: 'center'
            }}
            aria-hidden="true"
          >
            <span
              style={{
                width: '1em',
                height: '1em',
                border: '2px solid currentColor',
                borderTopColor: 'transparent',
                borderRadius: '50%',
                animation: 'spin 1s linear infinite'
              }}
            />
          </span>
        )}
        {leftIcon && (
          <span style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center' }}>
            {leftIcon}
          </span>

## 2. docker-compose.yml

```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  postgres:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: diyapp_v11
      POSTGRES_USER: diyapp_user
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: ${DB_PASSWORD:-secure_password_123}
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U diyapp_user"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"
    volumes:
      - redis_data:/data
    command: redis-server --appendonly yes
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "redis-cli", "ping"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  rabbitmq:
    image: rabbitmq:3.12-management-alpine
    environment:
      RABBITMQ_DEFAULT_USER: ${RABBITMQ_USER:-diyapp}
      RABBITMQ_DEFAULT_PASS: ${RABBITMQ_PASSWORD:-secure_password_123}
    ports:
      - "5672:5672"
      - "15672:15672"
    volumes:
      - rabbitmq_data:/var/lib/rabbitmq
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "rabbitmq-diagnostics", "ping"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  app:
    build: .
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    environment:
      NODE_ENV: production
      DB_HOST: postgres
      DB_PORT: 5432
      DB_NAME: diyapp_v11
      DB_USER: diyapp_user
      DB_PASSWORD: ${DB_PASSWORD:-secure_password_123}
      REDIS_HOST: redis
      REDIS_PORT: 6379
      RABBITMQ_HOST: rabbitmq
      RABBITMQ_PORT: 5672
      JWT_SECRET: ${JWT_SECRET:-your_super_secret_jwt_key_change_in_production}
    depends_on:
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
      rabbitmq:
        condition: service_healthy
    volumes:
      - ./logs:/app/logs

volumes:
  postgres_data:
  redis_data:
  rabbitmq_data:
```

## 4. src/config/index.js

```javascript
require('dotenv').config();

const config = {
  // Server
  env: process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development',
  port: parseInt(process.env.PORT, 10) || 3000,
  logLevel: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',

  // Database
  database: {
    host: process.env.DB_HOST || 'localhost',
    port: parseInt(process.env.DB_PORT, 10) || 5432,
    name: process.env.DB_NAME || 'diyapp_v11',
    user: process.env.DB_USER || 'diyapp_user',
    password: process.env.DB_PASSWORD || 'secure_password_123',
    pool: {
      max: 20,
      min: 5,
      acquire: 30000,
      idle: 10000
    }
  },

  // Redis
  redis: {
    host: process.env.REDIS_HOST || 'localhost',
    port: parseInt(process.env.REDIS_PORT, 10) || 6379,
    password: process.env.REDIS_PASSWORD || null,
    ttl: parseInt(process.env.REDIS_TTL, 10) || 3600
  },

  // RabbitMQ
  rabbitmq: {
    host: process.env.RABBITMQ_HOST || 'localhost',
    port: parseInt(process.env.RABBITMQ_PORT, 10) || 5672,
    user: process.env.RABBITMQ_USER || 'diyapp',
    password: process.env.RABBITMQ_PASSWORD || 'secure_password_123',
    queues: {
      email: 'email_queue',
      task: 'task_queue',
      notification: 'notification_queue'
    }
  },

  // JWT
  jwt: {
    secret: process.env.JWT_SECRET || 'your_super_secret_jwt_key_change_in_production',
    expiresIn: process.env.JWT_EXPIRES_IN || '24h',
    refreshExpiresIn: process.env.JWT_REFRESH_EXPIRES_IN || '7d'
  },

  // Rate Limiting
  rateLimit: {
    windowMs: parseInt(process.env.RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS, 10) || 900000,
    max: parseInt(process.env.RATE_LIMIT_MAX_REQUESTS, 10) || 100
  },

  // External Services
  external: {
    timeout: parseInt(process.env.EXTERNAL_API_TIMEOUT, 10) || 5000,
    retryAttempts: parseInt(process.env.EXTERNAL_API_RETRY_ATTEMPTS, 10) || 3
  },

  // Security
  security: {
    bcryptRounds: 12,
    tokenLength: 32
  }
};

// Validate required config
const requiredConfig = ['JWT_SECRET'];
requiredConfig.forEach(key => {
  if (!process.env[key] && config.env === 'production') {
    throw new Error(`Missing required environment variable: ${key}`);
  }
});

module.exports = config;
```

## 5. src/config/database.js

```javascript
const { Pool } = require('pg');
const config = require('./index');
const logger = require('../utils/logger');

class Database {
  constructor() {
    this.pool = new Pool(config.database);
    this.setupEventListeners();
  }

  setupEventListeners() {
    this.pool.on('connect', () => {
      logger.info('Database connection established');
    });

    this.pool.on('error', (err) => {
      logger.error('Unexpected database error', { error: err.message });
    });
  }

  async query(text, params) {
    const start = Date.now();
    const correlationId = global.correlationId || 'unknown';
    
    try {
      const result = await this.pool.query(text, params);
      const duration = Date.now() - start;
      
      logger.debug('Database query executed', {
        correlationId,
        query: text,
        duration,
        rowCount: result.rowCount
      });

      return result;
    } catch (error) {
      const duration = Date.now() - start;
      logger.error('Database query failed', {
        correlationId,
        query: text,
        duration,
        error: error.message,
        stack: config.env === 'development' ? error.stack : undefined
      });
      
      // Don't expose database errors to client
      throw new Error('Database operation failed');
    }
  }

  async transaction(callback) {
    const client = await this.pool.connect();
    
    try {
      await client.query('BEGIN');
      const result = await callback(client);
      await client.query('COMMIT');
      return result;
    } catch (error) {
      await client.query('ROLLBACK');
      throw error;
    } finally {
      client.release();
    }
  }

  async healthCheck() {
    try {
      await this.pool.query('SELECT 1');
      return { status: 'healthy', timestamp: new Date().toISOString() };
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Database health check failed', { error: error.message });
      return { status: 'unhealthy', error: error.message, timestamp: new Date().toISOString() };
    }
  }

  async close() {
    await this.pool.end();
    logger.info('Database connection pool closed');
  }
}

module.exports = new Database();
```

## 6. src/config/redis.js

```javascript
const { createClient } = require('redis');
const config = require('./index');
const logger = require('../utils/logger');

class RedisClient {
  constructor() {
    this.client = null;
    this.isConnected = false;
    this.circuitBreakerState = 'CLOSED';
    this.failureCount = 0;
    this.MAX_FAILURES = 5;
    this.RESET_TIMEOUT = 60000; // 1 minute
  }

  async connect() {
    if (this.isConnected && this.client) return;

    try {
      this.client = createClient({
        socket: {
          host: config.redis.host,
          port: config.redis.port,
          reconnectStrategy: (retries) => {
            if (retries > 10) {
              logger.error('Redis reconnection attempts exhausted');
              return new Error('Redis connection failed');
            }
            return Math.min(retries * 100, 3000);
          }
        },
        password: config.redis.password || undefined
      });

      this.setupEventListeners();
      await this.client.connect();
      this.isConnected = true;
      this.circuitBreakerState = 'CLOSED';
      this.failureCount = 0;
      
      logger.info('Redis connected successfully');
    } catch (error) {
      this.handleFailure(error);
      throw error;
    }
  }

  setupEventListeners() {
    this.client.on('error', (error) => {
      logger.error('Redis client error', { error: error.message });
      this.handleFailure(error);
    });

    this.client.on('connect', () => {
      logger.info('Redis client connecting');
    });

    this.client.on('ready', () => {
      logger.info('Redis client ready');
      this.isConnected = true;
    });

    this.client.on('end', () => {
      logger.warn('Redis client disconnected');
      this.isConnected = false;
    });

    this.client.on('reconnecting', () => {
      logger.info('Redis client reconnecting');
    });
  }

  handleFailure(error) {
    this.failureCount++;
    
    if (this.failureCount >= this.MAX_FAILURES && this.circuitBreakerState === 'CLOSED') {
      this.circuitBreakerState = 'OPEN';
      logger.warn('Redis circuit breaker opened', { failureCount: this.failureCount });
      
      // Auto-reset after timeout
      setTimeout(() => {
        this.circuitBreakerState = 'HALF_OPEN';
        logger.info('Redis circuit breaker half-open');
      }, this.RESET_TIMEOUT);
    }
  }

  handleSuccess() {
    if (this.circuitBreakerState === 'HALF_OPEN') {
      this.circuitBreakerState = 'CLOSED';
      this.failureCount = 0;
      logger.info('Redis circuit breaker closed');
    }
  }

  async executeWithCircuitBreaker(operation) {
    if (this.circuitBreakerState === 'OPEN') {
      throw new Error('Redis circuit breaker is open');
    }

    try {
      const result = await operation();
      this.handleSuccess();
      return result;
    } catch (error) {
      this.handleFailure(error);
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async get(key) {
    return this.executeWithCircuitBreaker(async () => {
      const start = Date.now();
      const value = await this.client.get(key);
      const duration = Date.now() - start;
      
      logger.debug('Redis GET operation', {
        key: this.maskSensitiveKey(key),
        duration,
        hit: value !== null
      });
      
      return value ? JSON.parse(value) : null;
    });
  }

  async set(key, value, ttl = config.redis.ttl) {
    return this.executeWithCircuitBreaker(async () => {
      const start = Date.now();
      const stringValue = JSON.stringify(value);
      const result = await this.client.set(key, stringValue, { EX: ttl });
      const duration = Date.now() - start;
      
      logger.debug('Redis SET operation', {
        key: this.maskSensitiveKey(key),
        duration,
        ttl
      });
      
      return result;
    });
  }

  async del(key) {
    return this.executeWithCircuitBreaker(async () => {
      const start = Date.now();
      const result = await this.client.del(key);
      const duration = Date.now() - start

### [Sessão Paralela: Data Engineer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Data Engineering Implementation

## 1. Esquema de Banco de Dados PostgreSQL (Escalável)

### `database/schemas/v11_core.sql`

```sql
-- =============================================
-- DIYAPP V11 Core - Database Schema
-- PostgreSQL 14+ with partitioning and scalability
-- =============================================

-- Enable required extensions
CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS "uuid-ossp";
CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS "pg_stat_statements";
CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS "timescaledb";

-- =============================================
-- CORE TABLES (High Write Frequency)
-- =============================================

-- Users table with partitioning by created_at
CREATE TABLE users (
    user_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    username VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    full_name VARCHAR(255),
    avatar_url TEXT,
    timezone VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'UTC',
    locale VARCHAR(10) DEFAULT 'en-US',
    
    -- Authentication
    password_hash VARCHAR(255),
    mfa_enabled BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    mfa_secret VARCHAR(100),
    last_login_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    
    -- Status
    status VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'active' CHECK (status IN ('active', 'inactive', 'suspended', 'pending')),
    email_verified BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    
    -- Metadata
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW() NOT NULL,
    updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW() NOT NULL,
    deleted_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    
    -- Indexes
    INDEX idx_users_email ON users(email),
    INDEX idx_users_status ON users(status),
    INDEX idx_users_created_at ON users(created_at)
) PARTITION BY RANGE (created_at);

-- Create monthly partitions for users
CREATE TABLE users_y2024m01 PARTITION OF users
    FOR VALUES FROM ('2024-01-01') TO ('2024-02-01');

-- Events table (time-series optimized with TimescaleDB)
CREATE TABLE events (
    event_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    user_id UUID REFERENCES users(user_id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
    session_id UUID NOT NULL,
    
    -- Event details
    event_type VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    event_name VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
    event_category VARCHAR(100),
    
    -- Event data
    properties JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
    metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
    
    -- Device/Platform info
    platform VARCHAR(50),
    os VARCHAR(50),
    browser VARCHAR(100),
    device_type VARCHAR(50),
    screen_resolution VARCHAR(20),
    
    -- Location
    country_code CHAR(2),
    region VARCHAR(100),
    city VARCHAR(100),
    
    -- Timing
    event_time TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW() NOT NULL,
    received_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW() NOT NULL,
    processed_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    
    -- Indexes
    INDEX idx_events_user_id ON events(user_id),
    INDEX idx_events_event_type ON events(event_type),
    INDEX idx_events_event_time ON events(event_time),
    INDEX idx_events_properties_gin ON events USING GIN (properties)
);

-- Convert to hypertable for time-series optimization
SELECT create_hypertable('events', 'event_time', 
    chunk_time_interval => INTERVAL '1 day',
    create_default_indexes => FALSE
);

-- =============================================
-- LLM INTERACTIONS (High Volume)
-- =============================================

CREATE TABLE llm_interactions (
    interaction_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    user_id UUID REFERENCES users(user_id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
    session_id UUID NOT NULL,
    
    -- LLM Provider Info
    provider VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL CHECK (provider IN ('openai', 'anthropic', 'google', 'azure', 'aws')),
    model VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    model_version VARCHAR(50),
    
    -- Token Usage
    prompt_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    completion_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    total_tokens INTEGER GENERATED ALWAYS AS (prompt_tokens + completion_tokens) STORED,
    
    -- Cost Tracking
    estimated_cost_usd DECIMAL(10,6),
    cost_currency VARCHAR(3) DEFAULT 'USD',
    
    -- Request/Response
    prompt TEXT NOT NULL,
    response TEXT,
    truncated_response BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    
    -- Performance
    latency_ms INTEGER,
    status_code INTEGER,
    error_message TEXT,
    
    -- Features/Context
    feature_name VARCHAR(100),
    context_id UUID,
    conversation_id UUID,
    
    -- Metadata
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW() NOT NULL,
    updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW() NOT NULL,
    
    -- Indexes
    INDEX idx_llm_user_id ON llm_interactions(user_id),
    INDEX idx_llm_provider_model ON llm_interactions(provider, model),
    INDEX idx_llm_created_at ON llm_interactions(created_at),
    INDEX idx_llm_feature ON llm_interactions(feature_name),
    INDEX idx_llm_cost ON llm_interactions(estimated_cost_usd)
) PARTITION BY RANGE (created_at);

-- =============================================
-- PRODUCT FEATURES
-- =============================================

CREATE TABLE features (
    feature_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    name VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    display_name VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
    description TEXT,
    
    -- Feature metadata
    category VARCHAR(50),
    tier VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'free' CHECK (tier IN ('free', 'pro', 'enterprise')),
    enabled BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    
    -- Usage limits
    daily_limit_per_user INTEGER,
    monthly_limit_per_user INTEGER,
    
    -- LLM Configuration
    default_llm_provider VARCHAR(50),
    default_llm_model VARCHAR(100),
    max_tokens_per_request INTEGER,
    
    -- Analytics
    total_uses BIGINT DEFAULT 0,
    last_used_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    
    -- Metadata
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW() NOT NULL,
    updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW() NOT NULL
);

CREATE TABLE feature_usage (
    usage_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    user_id UUID REFERENCES users(user_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    feature_id UUID REFERENCES features(feature_id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    session_id UUID NOT NULL,
    
    -- Usage details
    interaction_count INTEGER DEFAULT 1,
    total_tokens_used INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    total_cost_usd DECIMAL(10,6) DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Time tracking
    started_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW() NOT NULL,
    ended_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    duration_seconds INTEGER GENERATED ALWAYS AS (
        EXTRACT(EPOCH FROM (ended_at - started_at))
    ) STORED,
    
    -- Status
    status VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'completed' CHECK (status IN ('started', 'completed', 'failed', 'cancelled')),
    
    -- Indexes
    INDEX idx_feature_usage_user_feature ON feature_usage(user_id, feature_id),
    INDEX idx_feature_usage_started_at ON feature_usage(started_at),
    UNIQUE (user_id, feature_id, session_id)
);

-- =============================================
-- OPERATIONAL DATA (SRE/DevOps)
-- =============================================

CREATE TABLE deployments (
    deployment_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    service_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    version VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    environment VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL CHECK (environment IN ('development', 'staging', 'production')),
    
    -- Deployment details
    commit_hash VARCHAR(100),
    branch_name VARCHAR(100),
    deployer_email VARCHAR(255),
    
    -- Status
    status VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL CHECK (status IN ('started', 'success', 'failed', 'rolled_back')),
    rollback_reason TEXT,
    
    -- Performance
    deployment_duration_seconds INTEGER,
    downtime_seconds INTEGER,
    
    -- Timing
    started_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW() NOT NULL,
    completed_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    
    -- Indexes
    INDEX idx_deployments_service_env ON deployments(service_name, environment),
    INDEX idx_deployments_started_at ON deployments(started_at)
);

CREATE TABLE incidents (
    incident_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    title VARCHAR(500) NOT NULL,
    description TEXT,
    
    -- Severity
    severity VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL CHECK (severity IN ('critical', 'high', 'medium', 'low')),
    status VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'open' CHECK (status IN ('open', 'investigating', 'identified', 'monitoring', 'resolved', 'postmortem')),
    
    -- Service impact
    affected_services TEXT[],
    impact_score INTEGER CHECK (impact_score BETWEEN 1 AND 10),
    
    -- Resolution
    root_cause TEXT,
    resolution TEXT,
    action_items TEXT[],
    
    -- Timing
    detected_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW() NOT NULL,
    acknowledged_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    mitigated_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    resolved_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    
    -- Metrics
    mttd_seconds INTEGER,  -- Mean Time To Detect
    mtta_seconds INTEGER,  -- Mean Time To Acknowledge
    mttr_seconds INTEGER,  -- Mean Time To Resolve
    
    -- Indexes
    INDEX idx_incidents_severity_status ON incidents(severity, status),
    INDEX idx_incidents_detected_at ON incidents(detected_at)
);

-- =============================================
-- DATA WAREHOUSE TABLES (Analytics)
-- =============================================

CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS warehouse;

-- Daily User Activity Mart
CREATE TABLE warehouse.daily_user_activity (
    date DATE NOT NULL,
    user_id UUID NOT NULL,
    
    -- Activity metrics
    total_sessions INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    total_events INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    total_llm_interactions INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    total_tokens_used INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    total_cost_usd DECIMAL(10,6) DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Feature usage
    features_used TEXT[],
    unique_features_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Session duration
    first_session_start TIMESTAMPTZ,
    last_session_end TIMESTAMPTZ,
    total_session_duration_seconds INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Device/platform breakdown
    platforms_used TEXT[],
    
    -- Retention
    is_new_user BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    is_returning_user BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    
    -- Metadata
    processed_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
    
    PRIMARY KEY (date, user_id),
    INDEX idx_daily_activity_date ON warehouse.daily_user_activity(date),
    INDEX idx_daily_activity_user ON warehouse.daily_user_activity(user_id)
);

-- LLM Cost & Performance Mart
CREATE TABLE warehouse.llm_daily_metrics (
    date DATE NOT NULL,
    provider VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    model VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    feature_name VARCHAR(100),
    
    -- Volume metrics
    total_requests INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    successful_requests INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    failed_requests INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Token usage
    total_prompt_tokens BIGINT DEFAULT 0,
    total_completion_tokens BIGINT DEFAULT 0,
    avg_prompt_tokens_per_request DECIMAL(10,2),
    avg_completion_tokens_per_request DECIMAL(10,2),
    
    -- Cost metrics
    total_cost_usd DECIMAL(15,6) DEFAULT 0,
    avg_cost_per_request DECIMAL(10,6),
    cost_per_million_tokens DECIMAL(10,6),
    
    -- Performance
    avg_latency_ms DECIMAL(10,2),
    p95_latency_ms DECIMAL(10,2),
    p99_latency_ms DECIMAL(10,2),
    error_rate DECIMAL(5,4),
    
    -- Metadata
    processed_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
    
    PRIMARY KEY (date, provider, model, feature_name),
    INDEX idx_llm_metrics_date ON warehouse.llm_daily_metrics(date)
);

-- Feature Adoption Mart
CREATE TABLE warehouse.feature_adoption_daily (
    date DATE NOT NULL,
    feature_id UUID NOT NULL,
    feature_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    
    -- Adoption metrics
    total_users INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    new_users INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    returning_users INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Usage metrics
    total_sessions INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    total_interactions INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    avg_interactions_per_user DECIMAL(10,2),
    
    -- Token/cost metrics
    total_tokens_used BIGINT DEFAULT 0,
    total_cost_usd DECIMAL(15,6) DEFAULT 0,
    avg_cost_per_user DECIMAL(10,6),
    
    -- Retention
    day_1_retention_rate DECIMAL(5,4),
    day_7_retention_rate DECIMAL(5,4),
    day_30_retention_rate DECIMAL(5,4),
    
    -- Metadata
    processed_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
    
    PRIMARY KEY (date, feature_id),
    INDEX idx_feature_adoption_date ON warehouse.feature_adoption_daily(date),
    INDEX idx_feature_adoption_name ON warehouse.feature_adoption_daily(feature_name)
);

-- =============================================
-- AUDIT TABLES
-- =============================================

CREATE TABLE data_quality_checks (
    check_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    check_name VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
    check_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL CHECK (check_type IN ('completeness', 'uniqueness', 'validity', 'consistency', 'timeliness')),
    
    -- Target
    target_table VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
    target_column VARCHAR(200),
    
    -- Check configuration
    check_query TEXT NOT NULL,
    threshold DECIMAL(10,4),
    severity VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'warning' CHECK (severity IN ('critical', 'warning', 'info')),
    
    -- Results
    last_run_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    last_status VARCHAR(20) CHECK (last_status IN ('pass', 'fail', 'error')),
    last_value DECIMAL(20,6),
    last_message TEXT,
    
    -- Schedule
    schedule_cron VARCHAR(100),
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    
    -- Metadata
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW() NOT NULL,
    updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW() NOT NULL
);

CREATE TABLE pipeline_runs (
    run_id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    pipeline_name VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
    pipeline_version VARCHAR(50),
    
    -- Status
    status VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL CHECK (status IN ('started', 'running', 'success', 'failed', 'cancelled')),
    error_message TEXT,
    stack_trace TEXT,
    
    -- Timing
    started_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW() NOT NULL,
    ended_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    duration_seconds INTEGER GENERATED ALWAYS AS (
        EXTRACT(EPOCH FROM (ended_at - started_at))
    ) STORED,
    
    -- Metrics
    rows_processed BIGINT DEFAULT 0,
    rows_failed BIGINT DEFAULT 0,
    bytes_processed BIGINT DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- SLA tracking
    sla_seconds INTEGER,
    within_sla BOOLEAN,
    
    -- Indexes
    INDEX idx_pipeline_runs_name_status ON pipeline_runs(pipeline_name, status),
    INDEX idx_pipeline_runs_started_at ON pipeline_runs(started_at)
);

-- =============================================
-- FUNCTIONS & TRIGGERS
-- =============================================

-- Auto-update updated_at timestamp
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column()
RETURNS TRIGGER AS $$
BEGIN
    NEW.updated_at = NOW();
    RETURN NEW;
END;
$$ language 'plpgsql';

-- Apply triggers to all tables with updated_at
DO $$
DECLARE
    t RECORD;
BEGIN
    FOR t IN 
        SELECT table_name 
        FROM information_schema.columns 
        WHERE column_name = 'updated_at' 
        AND table_schema = 'public'
    LOOP
        EXECUTE format('
            DROP TRIGGER IF EXISTS update_%s_updated_at ON %s;
            CREATE TRIGGER update_%s_updated_at
            BEFORE UPDATE ON %s
            FOR EACH ROW
            EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();
        ', t.table_name, t.table_name, t.table_name, t.table_name);
    END LOOP;
END $$;

-- Function to calculate SLA compliance
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION calculate_sla_compliance(
    p_started_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    p_ended_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    p_expected_duration_seconds INTEGER
)
RETURNS BOOLEAN AS $$
BEGIN
    RETURN EXTRACT(EPOCH FROM (p_ended_at - p_started_at)) <= p_expected_duration_seconds;
END;
$$ LANGUAGE plpgsql IMMUTABLE;
```

# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Análise de Arquitetura e Padronização

## 1. Análise de Arquitetura do V10

### 1.1. Diagnóstico Técnico do V10
```javascript
// Arquivo: architecture-analysis/v10-assessment.md
# V10 Architecture Assessment Report

## Status Atual (V10)
- **Estrutura**: Monolito Node.js com acoplamento alto entre camadas
- **Banco de Dados**: MongoDB sem schema validation consistente
- **API**: REST sem versionamento estruturado
- **Segurança**: Autenticação JWT básica, falta de rate limiting
- **Testes**: Cobertura ~45%, falta de testes de integração
- **Deploy**: Manual, sem CI/CD pipeline estruturado

## Principais Problemas Identificados
1. **Acoplamento Alto**: Lógica de negócio misturada com controllers
2. **Falta de Padronização**: Estilos de código inconsistentes
3. **Débito Técnico**: 
   - N+1 queries em relatórios
   - Falta de cache estratégico
   - Logs não estruturados
4. **Segurança**: 
   - Input validation inconsistente
   - Falta de sanitização de XSS
   - Secrets em código (hardcoded)

## Métricas de Qualidade
- Complexidade ciclomática média: 12.4 (acima do ideal 10)
- Duplicação de código: 18.7%
- Dependências desatualizadas: 23%
```

    },

## 3. Configuração ESLint + Prettier

### 3.1. ESLint Configuration
```javascript
// Arquivo: .eslintrc.js
module.exports = {
  parser: '@typescript-eslint/parser',
  parserOptions: {
    ecmaVersion: 2022,
    sourceType: 'module',
    ecmaFeatures: {
      jsx: true
    }
  },
  env: {
    node: true,
    es2022: true,
    jest: true
  },
  extends: [
    'airbnb-base',
    'airbnb-typescript/base',
    'plugin:@typescript-eslint/recommended',
    'plugin:jest/recommended',
    'plugin:security/recommended',
    'plugin:sonarjs/recommended',
    'prettier'
  ],
  plugins: [
    '@typescript-eslint',
    'jest',
    'security',
    'sonarjs',
    'import',
    'unicorn'
  ],
  rules: {
    // Code Quality
    'complexity': ['error', 10],
    'max-depth': ['error', 4],
    'max-lines-per-function': ['warn', 50],
    'max-params': ['error', 3],
    
    // Security
    'security/detect-object-injection': 'error',
    'security/detect-non-literal-fs-filename': 'error',
    'security/detect-possible-timing-attacks': 'error',
    
    // TypeScript
    '@typescript-eslint/explicit-function-return-type': ['error', {
      allowExpressions: true,
      allowTypedFunctionExpressions: true
    }],
    '@typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any': 'error',
    '@typescript-eslint/no-unused-vars': ['error', {
      argsIgnorePattern: '^_',
      varsIgnorePattern: '^_'
    }],
    
    // Import/Export
    'import/order': ['error', {
      'groups': [
        'builtin',
        'external',
        'internal',
        'parent',
        'sibling',
        'index'
      ],
      'newlines-between': 'always'
    }],
    'import/no-cycle': 'error',
    'import/no-default-export': 'error',
    
    // Best Practices
    'no-console': ['error', { allow: ['warn', 'error'] }],
    'no-await-in-loop': 'error',
    'require-atomic-updates': 'error',
    
    // Unicorn Rules
    'unicorn/filename-case': ['error', {
      case: 'kebabCase'
    }],
    'unicorn/prevent-abbreviations': ['error', {
      replacements: {
        args: false,
        props: false,
        ref: false
      }
    }]
  },
  overrides: [
    {
      files: ['**/*.test.ts', '**/*.spec.ts'],
      rules: {
        'max-lines-per-function': 'off',
        '@typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any': 'off'
      }
    }
  ],
  settings: {
    'import/resolver': {
      typescript: {
        alwaysTryTypes: true
      }
    }
  }
};
```

### 3.3. Husky + Lint-Staged
```javascript
// Arquivo: .lintstagedrc.js
module.exports = {
  '*.{js,ts}': [
    'eslint --fix --max-warnings=0',
    'prettier --write'
  ],
  '*.{json,md,yml,yaml}': [
    'prettier --write'
  ],
  '*.{css,scss}': [
    'stylelint --fix'
  ]
};
```

```bash
#!/bin/bash
# Arquivo: .husky/pre-commit
#!/usr/bin/env sh
. "$(dirname -- "$0")/_/husky.sh"

npx lint-staged

# Run security audit for staged dependencies
if git diff --cached --name-only | grep -q 'package.json\|package-lock.json'; then
  echo "🔍 Running security audit for changed dependencies..."
  npm audit --audit-level=high
fi
```

## 4. SonarQube + Snyk Configuration

### 4.1. SonarQube Configuration
```properties
# Arquivo: sonar-project.properties
sonar.projectKey=diyapp-v11
sonar.projectName=DIYAPP V11
sonar.projectVersion=1.0.0

sonar.sources=src
sonar.tests=tests
sonar.test.inclusions=tests/**/*.test.ts,tests/**/*.spec.ts
sonar.exclusions=node_modules/**,dist/**,coverage/**,**/*.d.ts

sonar.javascript.lcov.reportPaths=coverage/lcov.info
sonar.typescript.lcov.reportPaths=coverage/lcov.info

sonar.qualitygate.wait=true
sonar.qualitygate.timeout=300

# TypeScript specific
sonar.typescript.tsconfigPath=tsconfig.json

# Test coverage
sonar.coverage.exclusions=**/*.d.ts,**/index.ts,**/config/**,**/types/**

# Duplication
sonar.cpd.exclusions=**/*.d.ts,**/migrations/**,**/fixtures/**

# Security
sonar.security.config=security-config.json
```

### 4.2. Snyk Configuration
```json
// Arquivo: .snyk
{
  "$schema": "https://snyk.io/schemas/snyk-policy-v1.0.0.schema.json",
  "version": "v1.0.0",
  "exclude": {
    "infrastructure": true
  },
  "patch": {},
  "ignore": {},
  "version": "v1.25.0",
  "audit": {
    "enabled": true,
    "frequency": "daily",
    "ignore": []
  },
  "docker": {
    "file": "Dockerfile",
    "image": "diyapp-v11",
    "args": {}
  }
}
```

### 4.3. GitHub Actions CI/CD
```yaml
# Arquivo: .github/workflows/ci.yml
name: CI Pipeline

on:
  push:
    branches: [ main, develop ]
  pull_request:
    branches: [ main ]

jobs:
  quality-gate:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3
      
      - name: Setup Node.js
        uses: actions/setup-node@v3
        with:
          node-version: '18'
          cache: 'npm'
      
      - name: Install dependencies
        run: npm ci
      
      - name: Lint
        run: npm run lint
      
      - name: Type check
        run: npm run type-check
      
      - name: Test with coverage
        run: npm run test:coverage
      
      - name: Security audit
        run: npm run audit
      
      - name: SonarQube Scan
        uses: SonarSource/sonarqube-scan-action@master
        env:
          SONAR_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.SONAR_TOKEN }}
          SONAR_HOST_URL: ${{ secrets.SONAR_HOST_URL }}
      
      - name: Snyk Security Scan
        uses: snyk/actions/node@master
        env:
          SNYK_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.SNYK_TOKEN }}
        with:
          args: --severity-threshold=high
      
      - name: Build
        run: npm run build
      
      - name: Upload coverage
        uses: codecov/codecov-action@v3
        with:
          token: ${{ secrets.CODECOV_TOKEN }}
  
  dependency-review:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3
      - uses: actions/dependency-review-action@v3
        with:
          fail-on-severity: high
  
  container-scan:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3
      - name: Build Docker image
        run: docker build -t diyapp-v11 .
      - name: Scan with Trivy
        uses: aquasecurity/trivy-action@master
        with:
          image-ref: 'diyapp-v11'
          format: 'sarif'
          output: 'trivy-results.sarif'
      - name: Upload Trivy scan results
        uses: github/codeql-action/upload-sarif@v2
        with:
          sarif_file: 'trivy-results.sarif'
```

## 5. Definition of Done (DoD) Técnico

```markdown
# Arquivo: DOD-TECHNICAL.md
# Definition of Done - Técnico

## ✅ PRÉ-REQUISITOS PARA TODO CARD

### 1. Código
- [ ] Segue os Engineering Standards (estilo, estrutura, convenções)
- [ ] Passa em todos os linters (ESLint, Prettier, Stylelint)
- [ ] TypeScript: sem `any`, tipos explícitos para funções públicas
- [ ] Complexidade ciclomática ≤ 10 por função
- [ ] Sem duplicação de código detectada pelo SonarQube
- [ ] Commits seguem Conventional Commits

### 2. Testes
- [ ] Cobertura mínima de 80% (linhas, branches, functions)
- [ ] Testes unitários para todas as funções públicas
- [ ] Testes de integração para APIs e serviços externos
- [ ] Testes E2E para fluxos críticos de usuário
- [ ] Edge cases cobertos conforme critérios de aceite
- [ ] Mocks apropriados para dependências externas

### 3. Segurança
- [ ] Input validation em todos os endpoints
- [ ] Output encoding para prevenir XSS
- [ ] SQL/NoSQL injection prevention
- [ ] Autenticação/autorização implementada conforme RBAC
- [ ] Secrets nunca hardcoded (usar variáveis de ambiente)
- [ ] Dependências atualizadas e sem vulnerabilidades críticas
- [ ] Rate limiting implementado onde necessário

### 4. Performance
- [ ] N+1 queries identificadas e otimizadas
- [ ] Cache implementado para dados frequentemente acessados
- [ ] Paginação implementada para listagens grandes
- [ ] Assets otimizados (minificação, compressão)
- [ ] Lazy loading para componentes/bibliotecas grandes

### 5. Documentação
- [ ] JSDoc/TSDoc para todas as funções públicas
- [ ] README atualizado se necessário
- [ ] API documentada (OpenAPI/Swagger)
- [ ] ADR criado para decisões arquiteturais
- [ ] Comentários apenas para "porquê", não "o quê"

### 6. Revisão de Código
- [ ] PR criado com template preenchido
- [ ] Tamanho do PR ≤ 400 linhas modificadas
- [ ] Descrição clara do problema e solução
- [ ] Link para card do Jira/Linear
- [ ] Reviewers atribuídos (Tech Lead obrigatório)
- [ ]

### [Sessão Paralela: UX Designer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Dashboard UI/UX

Vou criar um sistema de design premium completo com wireframes de alta fidelidade em HTML/CSS puro, implementando todos os componentes solicitados com foco em usabilidade e acessibilidade.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v11-dashboard/
├── index.html          # Dashboard principal
├── style.css          # Sistema de design completo
├── script.js          # Interatividade e funcionalidades
├── assets/
│   ├── icons/         # Ícones SVG
│   └── images/        # Imagens de placeholder
└── README.md          # Documentação do design system
```

```javascript
// services/core/LoggerService.js
const winston = require('winston');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');

class LoggerService {
    constructor() {
        this.correlationId = uuidv4();
        this.logger = winston.createLogger({
            level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
            format: winston.format.combine(
                winston.format.timestamp(),
                winston.format.json()
            ),
            defaultMeta: { service: 'diyapp-core' },
            transports: [
                new winston.transports.File({ 
                    filename: 'logs/error.log', 
                    level: 'error',
                    maxsize: 5242880, // 5MB
                    maxFiles: 5
                }),
                new winston.transports.File({ 
                    filename: 'logs/combined.log',
                    maxsize: 5242880,
                    maxFiles: 10
                })
            ]
        });

        if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production') {
            this.logger.add(new winston.transports.Console({
                format: winston.format.combine(
                    winston.format.colorize(),
                    winston.format.simple()
                )
            }));
        }
    }

    setCorrelationId(id) {
        this.correlationId = id || uuidv4();
        return this.correlationId;
    }

    maskSensitiveData(data) {
        if (!data) return data;
        
        const masked = { ...data };
        const sensitiveFields = ['password', 'token', 'apiKey', 'secret', 'creditCard', 'cpf', 'email'];
        
        sensitiveFields.forEach(field => {
            if (masked[field]) {
                masked[field] = '***MASKED***';
            }
        });
        
        return masked;
    }

    info(message, meta = {}) {
        this.logger.info(message, {
            correlation_id: this.correlationId,
            ...this.maskSensitiveData(meta)
        });
    }

    error(message, error = null, meta = {}) {
        const logMeta = {
            correlation_id: this.correlationId,
            ...this.maskSensitiveData(meta)
        };

        if (error) {
            logMeta.error_message = error.message;
            logMeta.error_stack = error.stack;
            logMeta.error_name = error.name;
        }

        this.logger.error(message, logMeta);
    }

    warn(message, meta = {}) {
        this.logger.warn(message, {
            correlation_id: this.correlationId,
            ...this.maskSensitiveData(meta)
        });
    }

    debug(message, meta = {}) {
        this.logger.debug(message, {
            correlation_id: this.correlationId,
            ...this.maskSensitiveData(meta)
        });
    }

    audit(action, userId, resource, meta = {}) {
        this.logger.info(`AUDIT: ${action}`, {
            correlation_id: this.correlationId,
            user_id: userId,
            resource,
            action,
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
            ...this.maskSensitiveData(meta)
        });
    }
}

module.exports = new LoggerService();
```

```javascript
// services/core/ApiClientService.js
const axios = require('axios');
const CircuitBreaker = require('opossum');
const logger = require('./LoggerService');

class ApiClientService {
    constructor() {
        this.circuitBreakers = new Map();
        this.defaultConfig = {
            timeout: parseInt(process.env.API_TIMEOUT_MS) || 10000,
            maxRetries: 3,
            retryDelay: 100,
            circuitBreakerOptions: {
                timeout: parseInt(process.env.CIRCUIT_BREAKER_TIMEOUT) || 30000,
                errorThresholdPercentage: 50,
                resetTimeout: 60000,
                rollingCountTimeout: 10000,
                rollingCountBuckets: 10
            }
        };
    }

    getCircuitBreaker(name, options = {}) {
        if (!this.circuitBreakers.has(name)) {
            const breakerOptions = {
                ...this.defaultConfig.circuitBreakerOptions,
                ...options
            };

            const breaker = new CircuitBreaker(
                async (url, config) => {
                    const response = await axios(url, config);
                    return response;
                },
                breakerOptions
            );

            breaker.on('open', () => {
                logger.warn(`Circuit breaker ${name} opened`, { breaker: name });
            });

            breaker.on('close', () => {
                logger.info(`Circuit breaker ${name} closed`, { breaker: name });
            });

            breaker.on('halfOpen', () => {
                logger.info(`Circuit breaker ${name} half-open`, { breaker: name });
            });

            breaker.fallback(() => {
                logger.warn(`Circuit breaker ${name} fallback activated`, { breaker: name });
                return Promise.reject(new Error(`Service ${name} unavailable - circuit breaker open`));
            });

            this.circuitBreakers.set(name, breaker);
        }

        return this.circuitBreakers.get(name);
    }

    async retryRequest(fn, maxRetries = 3, baseDelay = 100) {
        let lastError;
        
        for (let attempt = 0; attempt <= maxRetries; attempt++) {
            try {
                return await fn();
            } catch (error) {
                lastError = error;
                
                // Only retry on timeout or 5xx errors
                const shouldRetry = error.code === 'ECONNABORTED' || 
                                  (error.response && error.response.status >= 500);
                
                if (!shouldRetry || attempt === maxRetries) {
                    break;
                }
                
                const delay = baseDelay * Math.pow(2, attempt) + Math.random() * 100;
                await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, delay));
                
                logger.warn(`Retry attempt ${attempt + 1}/${maxRetries}`, {
                    error: error.message,
                    delay,
                    next_attempt: attempt + 2
                });
            }
        }
        
        throw lastError;
    }

    async request(method, url, data = null, config = {}, serviceName = 'external-api') {
        const startTime = Date.now();
        const requestId = uuidv4();
        
        const requestConfig = {
            method,
            url,
            timeout: config.timeout || this.defaultConfig.timeout,
            headers: {
                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                'X-Request-ID': requestId,
                'X-Correlation-ID': logger.correlationId,
                ...config.headers
            },
            ...config
        };

        if (data && method !== 'GET') {
            requestConfig.data = data;
        }

        try {
            logger.debug(`API Request: ${method} ${url}`, {
                request_id: requestId,
                service: serviceName,
                url,
                method
            });

            const breaker = this.getCircuitBreaker(serviceName);
            const response = await breaker.fire(url, requestConfig);
            
            const duration = Date.now() - startTime;
            
            logger.info(`API Response: ${method} ${url} - ${response.status}`, {
                request_id: requestId,
                service: serviceName,
                url,
                method,
                status: response.status,
                duration_ms: duration,
                response_size: JSON.stringify(response.data).length
            });

            // Log warning for slow responses
            if (duration > 1000) {
                logger.warn(`Slow API response`, {
                    request_id: requestId,
                    service: serviceName,
                    duration_ms: duration,
                    threshold_ms: 1000
                });
            }

            return {
                data: response.data,
                status: response.status,
                headers: response.headers,
                requestId
            };

        } catch (error) {
            const duration = Date.now() - startTime;
            
            logger.error(`API Error: ${method} ${url}`, error, {
                request_id: requestId,
                service: serviceName,
                url,
                method,
                duration_ms: duration,
                error_code: error.code,
                response_status: error.response?.status
            });

            throw this.normalizeError(error, requestId);
        }
    }

    normalizeError(error, requestId) {
        const normalized = new Error(error.message);
        normalized.name = 'ApiClientError';
        normalized.requestId = requestId;
        normalized.code = error.code;
        normalized.status = error.response?.status;
        normalized.data = error.response?.data;
        
        return normalized;
    }

    async get(url, config = {}, serviceName = 'external-api') {
        return this.request('GET', url, null, config, serviceName);
    }

    async post(url, data, config = {}, serviceName = 'external-api') {
        return this.request('POST', url, data, config, serviceName);
    }

    async put(url, data, config = {}, serviceName = 'external-api') {
        return this.request('PUT', url, data, config, serviceName);
    }

    async delete(url, config = {}, serviceName = 'external-api') {
        return this.request('DELETE', url, null, config, serviceName);
    }

    async patch(url, data, config = {}, serviceName = 'external-api') {
        return this.request('PATCH', url, data, config, serviceName);
    }
}

module.exports = new ApiClientService();
```

```javascript
// services/core/CacheService.js
const Redis = require('ioredis');
const logger = require('./LoggerService');

class CacheService {
    constructor() {
        this.client = null;
        this.memoryCache = new Map();
        this.useMemoryCache = process.env.REDIS_URL ? false : true;
        this.defaultTTL = parseInt(process.env.CACHE_TTL_MS) || 300000; // 5 minutes
        this.cacheHits = 0;
        this.cacheMisses = 0;
        
        this.initialize();
    }

    async initialize() {
        if (this.useMemoryCache) {
            logger.info('Using in-memory cache (Redis not configured)');
            return;
        }

        try {
            this.client = new Redis(process.env.REDIS_URL, {
                retryStrategy: (times) => {
                    const delay = Math.min(times * 50, 2000);
                    return delay;
                },
                maxRetriesPerRequest: 3,
                enableReadyCheck: true,
                connectTimeout: 10000
            });

            this.client.on('connect', () => {
                logger.info('Redis connected successfully');
            });

            this.client.on('error', (error) => {
                logger.error('Redis connection error', error);
                this.useMemoryCache = true;
            });

            this.client.on('ready', () => {
                logger.info('Redis ready for commands');
            });

            // Test connection
            await this.client.ping();
            
        } catch (error) {
            logger.error('Failed to initialize Redis, falling back to memory cache', error);
            this.useMemoryCache = true;
        }
    }

    async get(key) {
        try {
            let value;
            
            if (this.useMemoryCache) {
                const cached = this.memoryCache.get(key);
                if (cached && cached.expiry > Date.now()) {
                    value = cached.value;
                } else {
                    this.memoryCache.delete(key);
                }
            } else {
                value = await this.client.get(key);
                if (value) {
                    try {
                        value = JSON.parse(value);
                    } catch {
                        // Keep as string if not JSON
                    }
                }
            }

            if (value !== null && value !== undefined) {
                this.cacheHits++;
                logger.debug(`Cache hit for key: ${key}`, { key, cache_type: this.useMemoryCache ? 'memory' : 'redis' });
                return value;
            }

            this.cacheMisses++;
            logger.debug(`Cache miss for key: ${key}`, { key, cache_type: this.useMemoryCache ? 'memory' : 'redis' });
            return null;

        } catch (error) {
            logger.error(`Cache get error for key: ${key}`, error, { key });
            return null;
        }
    }

    async set(key, value, ttl = this.defaultTTL) {
        try {
            const cacheValue = typeof value === 'string' ? value : JSON.stringify(value);
            
            if (this.useMemoryCache) {
                this.memoryCache.set(key, {
                    value,
                    expiry: Date.now() + ttl
                });
                
                // Cleanup expired entries periodically
                if (this.memoryCache.size > 1000) {
                    this.cleanupMemoryCache();
                }
            } else {
                if (ttl > 0) {
                    await this.client.setex(key, Math.ceil(ttl / 1000), cacheValue);
                } else {
                    await this.client.set(key, cacheValue);
                }
            }

            logger.debug(`Cache set for key: ${key}`, { 
                key, 
                ttl_ms: ttl,
                cache_type: this.useMemoryCache ? 'memory' : 'redis'
            });

            return true;

        } catch (error) {
            logger.error(`Cache set error for key: ${key}`, error, { key });
            return false;
        }
    }

    async delete(key) {
        try {
            if (this.useMemoryCache) {
                this.memoryCache.delete(key);
            } else {
                await this.client.del(key);
            }

            logger.debug(`Cache delete for key: ${key}`, { key });
            return true;

        } catch (error) {
            logger.error(`Cache delete error for key: ${key}`, error, { key });
            return false;
        }
    }

    async getOrSet(key, fetchFn, ttl = this.defaultTTL) {
        const cached = await this.get(key);
        
        if (cached !== null) {
            return cached;
        }

        const value = await fetchFn();
        await this.set(key, value, ttl);
        
        return value;
    }

    async invalidatePattern(pattern) {
        try {
            if (this.useMemoryCache) {
                for (const key of this.memoryCache.keys()) {
                    if (key.includes(pattern)) {
                        this.memoryCache.delete(key);
                    }
                }
            } else {
                const keys = await this.client.keys(`*${pattern}*`);
                if (keys.length > 0) {
                    await this.client.del(...keys);
                }
            }

            logger.debug(`Cache invalidated for pattern: ${pattern}`, { pattern });
            return true;

        } catch (error) {
            logger.error(`Cache invalidate error for pattern: ${pattern}`, error, { pattern });
            return false;
        }
    }

    cleanupMemoryCache() {
        const now = Date.now();
        let cleaned = 0;
        
        for (const [key, value] of this.memoryCache.entries()) {
            if (value.expiry <= now) {
                this.memoryCache.delete(key);
                cleaned++;
            }
        }

        if (cleaned > 0) {
            logger.debug(`Memory cache cleaned: ${cleaned} expired entries removed`);
        }
    }

    getStats() {
        const hitRate = this.cacheHits + this.cacheMisses > 0 
            ? (this.cacheHits / (this.cacheHits + this.cacheMisses)) * 100 
            : 0;

        return {
            cache_type: this.useMemoryCache ? 'memory' : 'redis',
            memory_cache_size: this.useMemoryCache ? this.memoryCache.size : 0,
            cache_hits: this.cacheHits,
            cache_misses: this.cacheMisses,
            hit_rate: `${hitRate.toFixed(2)}%`,
            connected: !this.useMemoryCache && this.client?.status === 'ready'
        };
    }

    async flushAll() {
        try {
            if (this.useMemoryCache) {
                this.memoryCache.clear();
            } else {
                await this.client.flushall();
            }

            logger.info('Cache flushed');
            return true;

        } catch (error) {
            logger.error('Cache flush error', error);
            return false;
        }
    }
}

module.exports = new CacheService();
```

```javascript
// services/core/AuthService.js
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const bcrypt = require('bcrypt');
const crypto = require('crypto');
const logger = require('./LoggerService');
const cache = require('./CacheService');

class AuthService {
    constructor() {
        this.jwtSecret = process.env.JWT_SECRET || crypto.randomBytes(64).toString('hex');
        this.jwtExpiry = process.env.JWT_EXPIRY || '24h';
        this.refreshTokenExpiry = process.env.REFRESH_TOKEN_EXPIRY || '7d';
        this.saltRounds = 10;
        this.rateLimitWindow = 15 * 60 * 1000; // 15 minutes
        this.maxAttempts = 5;
    }

    async hashPassword(password) {
        try {
            const salt = await bcrypt.genSalt(this.saltRounds);
            const hash = await bcrypt.hash(password, salt);
            return hash;
        } catch (error) {
            logger.error('Password hashing failed', error);
            throw new Error('Password processing failed');
        }
    }

    async verifyPassword(password, hash) {
        try {
            return await bcrypt.compare(password, hash);
        } catch (error) {
            logger.error('Password verification failed', error);
            return false;
        }
    }

    generateTokens(userId, userRole = 'user') {
        const payload = {
            sub: userId,
            role: userRole,
            iat: Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000)
        };

        const accessToken = jwt.sign(payload, this.jwtSecret, {
            expiresIn: this.jwtExpiry
        });

        const refreshToken = crypto.randomBytes(40).toString('hex');
        const refreshTokenHash = crypto.createHash('sha256').update(refreshToken).digest('hex');

        // Store refresh token hash in cache
        const refreshKey = `refresh_token:${refreshTokenHash}`;
        cache.set(refreshKey, {
            userId,
            expiresAt: Date.now() + (7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000) // 7 days
        }, 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);

        return {
            accessToken,
            refreshToken,
            expiresIn: this.getExpiryInSeconds(this.jwtExpiry)
        };
    }

    verifyToken(token) {
        try {
            return jwt.verify(token, this.jwtSecret);
        } catch (error) {
            logger.error('Token verification failed', error, { token_type: 'JWT' });
            return null;
        }
    }



### [Sessão Paralela: Frontend]
```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="pt-BR">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>DIYAPP Evolution - Dashboard V11</title>
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/font-awesome/6.4.0/css/all.min.css">
    <script src="https://unpkg.com/vue@3/dist/vue.global.js"></script>
