### [Sessão Paralela: Data Engineer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Camada de Persistência

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v11-persistence/
├── src/
│   ├── database/
│   │   ├── config/
│   │   │   ├── development.js
│   │   │   ├── production.js
│   │   │   └── test.js
│   │   ├── migrations/
│   │   │   ├── 001_create_users_table.js
│   │   │   ├── 002_create_system_logs_table.js
│   │   │   ├── 003_create_cache_table.js
│   │   │   ├── 004_create_llm_requests_table.js
│   │   │   └── 005_create_data_pipelines_table.js
│   │   ├── seeds/
│   │   │   ├── development/
│   │   │   │   └── initial_data.js
│   │   │   └── production/
│   │   │       └── admin_user.js
│   │   ├── models/
│   │   │   ├── User.js
│   │   │   ├── SystemLog.js
│   │   │   ├── Cache.js
│   │   │   ├── LLMRequest.js
│   │   │   └── DataPipeline.js
│   │   ├── repositories/
│   │   │   ├── BaseRepository.js
│   │   │   ├── UserRepository.js
│   │   │   ├── SystemLogRepository.js
│   │   │   ├── CacheRepository.js
│   │   │   ├── LLMRequestRepository.js
│   │   │   └── DataPipelineRepository.js
│   │   └── connection.js
│   ├── services/
│   │   ├── DatabaseService.js
│   │   ├── MigrationService.js
│   │   └── BackupService.js
│   └── utils/
│       ├── logger.js
│       ├── validation.js
│       └── encryption.js
├── scripts/
│   ├── migrate.js
│   ├── rollback.js
│   ├── seed.js
│   └── backup.js
├── tests/
│   ├── database/
│   │   ├── connection.test.js
│   │   ├── migrations.test.js
│   │   └── models.test.js
│   └── integration/
│       └── persistence.test.js
├── public/
│   └── dashboard.html
├── knexfile.js
├── package.json
├── .env.example
├── .gitignore
├── README.md
└── index.html
```

## 1. Configuração do Ambiente

### package.json
```json
{
  "name": "diyapp-v11-persistence",
  "version": "1.0.0",
  "description": "Camada de persistência para DIYAPP Evolution V11",
  "main": "index.js",
  "scripts": {
    "start": "node index.js",
    "dev": "NODE_ENV=development nodemon index.js",
    "test": "NODE_ENV=test jest",
    "migrate": "node scripts/migrate.js",
    "migrate:latest": "npx knex migrate:latest",
    "migrate:rollback": "npx knex migrate:rollback",
    "seed": "npx knex seed:run",
    "backup": "node scripts/backup.js",
    "lint": "eslint src/**/*.js"
  },
  "dependencies": {
    "knex": "^2.5.1",
    "sqlite3": "^5.1.6",
    "pg": "^8.11.3",
    "dotenv": "^16.3.1",
    "bcryptjs": "^2.4.3",
    "jsonwebtoken": "^9.0.2",
    "uuid": "^9.0.1",
    "winston": "^3.11.0",
    "joi": "^17.11.0",
    "cors": "^2.8.5",
    "express": "^4.18.2",
    "helmet": "^7.1.0",
    "compression": "^1.7.4"
  },
  "devDependencies": {
    "nodemon": "^3.0.1",
    "jest": "^29.7.0",
    "supertest": "^6.3.3",
    "eslint": "^8.53.0",
    "@faker-js/faker": "^8.3.1"
  },
  "engines": {
    "node": ">=18.0.0"
  }
}
```

### .env.example
```env
# Database Configuration
NODE_ENV=development
DB_CLIENT=sqlite3
DB_CONNECTION_DEV=./data/dev.db
DB_CONNECTION_TEST=./data/test.db

# Production Database (PostgreSQL)
DB_HOST=localhost
DB_PORT=5432
DB_USER=postgres
DB_PASSWORD=your_password
DB_NAME=diyapp_prod
DB_SSL=false

# Security
JWT_SECRET=your_jwt_secret_key_here
ENCRYPTION_KEY=your_32_char_encryption_key

# Logging
LOG_LEVEL=info
LOG_TO_FILE=true
LOG_DIR=./logs

# Backup
BACKUP_ENABLED=true
BACKUP_SCHEDULE=0 2 * * * # Daily at 2 AM
BACKUP_RETENTION_DAYS=30
```

### knexfile.js
```javascript
require('dotenv').config();

const config = {
  development: {
    client: process.env.DB_CLIENT || 'sqlite3',
    connection: {
      filename: process.env.DB_CONNECTION_DEV || './data/dev.db'
    },
    migrations: {
      directory: './src/database/migrations',
      tableName: 'knex_migrations'
    },
    seeds: {
      directory: './src/database/seeds/development'
    },
    useNullAsDefault: true,
    pool: {
      min: 2,
      max: 10
    },
    debug: true
  },

  test: {
    client: 'sqlite3',
    connection: {
      filename: './data/test.db'
    },
    migrations: {
      directory: './src/database/migrations'
    },
    seeds: {
      directory: './src/database/seeds/development'
    },
    useNullAsDefault: true
  },

  production: {
    client: 'pg',
    connection: {
      host: process.env.DB_HOST,
      port: process.env.DB_PORT,
      user: process.env.DB_USER,
      password: process.env.DB_PASSWORD,
      database: process.env.DB_NAME,
      ssl: process.env.DB_SSL === 'true' ? { rejectUnauthorized: false } : false
    },
    migrations: {
      directory: './src/database/migrations'
    },
    seeds: {
      directory: './src/database/seeds/production'
    },
    pool: {
      min: 2,
      max: 20,
      acquireTimeoutMillis: 60000,
      createTimeoutMillis: 30000,
      idleTimeoutMillis: 600000,
      reapIntervalMillis: 1000,
      createRetryIntervalMillis: 2000
    }
  }
};

module.exports = config;
```

## 2. Configurações de Banco de Dados

### src/database/config/development.js
```javascript
module.exports = {
  client: 'sqlite3',
  connection: {
    filename: process.env.DB_CONNECTION_DEV || './data/dev.db'
  },
  useNullAsDefault: true,
  debug: process.env.DB_DEBUG === 'true',
  pool: {
    afterCreate: (conn, cb) => {
      conn.run('PRAGMA foreign_keys = ON', cb);
    }
  }
};
```

### src/database/config/production.js
```javascript
module.exports = {
  client: 'pg',
  connection: {
    host: process.env.DB_HOST,
    port: process.env.DB_PORT,
    user: process.env.DB_USER,
    password: process.env.DB_PASSWORD,
    database: process.env.DB_NAME,
    ssl: process.env.DB_SSL === 'true' ? { rejectUnauthorized: false } : false
  },
  pool: {
    min: 2,
    max: 20,
    acquireTimeoutMillis: 60000,
    createTimeoutMillis: 30000,
    idleTimeoutMillis: 600000,
    reapIntervalMillis: 1000,
    createRetryIntervalMillis: 2000
  },
  acquireConnectionTimeout: 60000
};
```

### src/database/config/test.js
```javascript

/**
 * Migration: Create users table
 * Data Engineer: Users são consumidores de dados - precisam de perfis de acesso bem definidos
 */
exports.up = function(knex) {
  return knex.schema.createTable('users', function(table) {
    // Identificação
    table.uuid('id').primary().defaultTo(knex.raw('gen_random_uuid()'));
    table.string('email').unique().notNullable();
    table.string('username').unique().notNullable();
    
    // Autenticação
    table.string('password_hash').notNullable();
    table.string('password_salt').notNullable();
    table.string('reset_token').unique();
    table.timestamp('reset_token_expires');
    
    // Perfil e permissões
    table.enum('role', ['admin', 'data_engineer', 'pm', 'ai_ops', 'llm_specialist', 'viewer']).defaultTo('viewer');
    table.jsonb('permissions').defaultTo('{}');
    table.boolean('is_active').defaultTo(true);
    table.boolean('email_verified').defaultTo(false);
    
    // Dados pessoais (compliance-ready)
    table.string('full_name');
    table.string('department');
    table.string('timezone').defaultTo('UTC');
    table.string('locale').defaultTo('en-US');
    
    // Preferências
    table.jsonb('preferences').defaultTo('{}');
    table.string('dashboard_layout').defaultTo('default');
    
    // Auditoria
    table.timestamp('last_login_at');
    table.string('last_login_ip');
    table.integer('login_count').defaultTo(0);
    
    // Retenção de dados (compliance)
    table.timestamp('data_retention_until');
    table.boolean('gdpr_compliant').defaultTo(false);
    
    // Timestamps
    table.timestamp('created_at').defaultTo(knex.fn.now());
    table.timestamp('updated_at').defaultTo(knex.fn.now());
    table.timestamp('deleted_at');
    
    // Indexes para performance
    table.index(['email', 'is_active']);
    table.index(['role', 'is_active']);
    table.index(['created_at', 'deleted_at']);
  });
};

exports.down = function(knex) {
  return knex.schema.dropTable('users');
};

### src/database/migrations/002_create_system_logs_table.js
```javascript
/**
 * Migration: Create system logs table
 * Data Engineer: Logs são dados brutos para monitoramento e troubleshooting
 */
exports.up = function(knex) {
  return knex.schema.createTable('system_logs', function(table) {
    // Identificação
    table.uuid('id').primary().defaultTo(knex.raw('gen_random_uuid()'));
    table.uuid('correlation_id').notNullable();
    
    // Contexto
    table.string('service').notNullable();
    table.string('module').notNullable();
    table.string('function').notNullable();
    
    // Dados do log
    table.enum('level', ['error', 'warn', 'info', 'debug', 'trace']).defaultTo('info');
    table.text('message').notNullable();
    table.jsonb('metadata').defaultTo('{}');
    table.jsonb('error_details');
    
    // Performance
    table.float('duration_ms');
    table.integer('memory_usage_mb');
    
    // Usuário/Request context
    table.uuid('user_id').references('id').inTable('users').onDelete('SET NULL');
    table.string('user_agent');
    table.string('ip_address');
    table.string('request_id');
    
    // Pipeline context (para Data Engineer)
    table.string('pipeline_id');
    table.string('pipeline_stage');
    table.string('data_source');
    
    // Timestamps com particionamento lógico
    table.timestamp('logged_at').defaultTo(knex.fn.now()).index();
    table.date('log_date').defaultTo(knex.raw('CURRENT_DATE')).index();
    
    // Indexes para queries comuns
    table.index(['service', 'level', 'logged_at']);
    table.index(['pipeline_id', 'pipeline_stage']);
    table.index(['correlation_id']);
    table.index(['user_id', 'logged_at']);
    
    // Partitionamento por data (para PostgreSQL)
    if (knex.client.config.client === 'pg') {
      table.raw('PARTITION BY RANGE (log_date)');
    }
  });
};

exports.down = function(knex) {
  return knex.schema.dropTable('system_logs');
};
```

### src/database/migrations/003_create_cache_table.js
```javascript
/**
 * Migration: Create cache table
 * Data Engineer: Cache precisa de TTL e invalidation tracking
 */
exports.up = function(knex) {
  return knex.schema.createTable('cache', function(table) {
    // Chave do cache
    table.string('key').primary();
    table.string('namespace').defaultTo('default').index();
    
    // Valor
    table.text('value').notNullable();
    table.string('content_type').defaultTo('application/json');
    table.integer('size_bytes');
    
    // Metadata
    table.string('tags').index();
    table.string('dependency_keys');
    
    // TTL e invalidação
    table.timestamp('expires_at').index();
    table.timestamp('invalidated_at');
    table.string('invalidation_reason');
    
    // Estatísticas de uso
    table.integer('hit_count').defaultTo(0);
    table.integer('miss_count').defaultTo(0);
    table.timestamp('last_accessed_at');
    table.timestamp('last_updated_at').defaultTo(knex.fn.now());
    
    // Origem
    table.string('source_system');
    table.string('cache_strategy').defaultTo('ttl');
    
    // Timestamps
    table.timestamp('created_at').defaultTo(knex.fn.now());
    
    // Indexes
    table.index(['namespace', 'expires_at']);
    table.index(['tags', 'expires_at']);
    table.index(['last_accessed_at']);
    
    // Para PostgreSQL, adicionar gin index para tags
    if (knex.client.config.client === 'pg') {
      table.index(['tags'], 'gin', { using: 'gin', expression: 'tags gin_trgm_ops' });
    }
  });
};

exports.down = function(knex) {
  return knex.schema.dropTable('cache');
};
```

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Arquitetura de Microsserviços

## 1. Documento de Arquitetura (ADR-001)

**ADR-001: Arquitetura de Microsserviços V11**

**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead, Especialista Infra, Especialista Segurança

**CONTEXTO:**
A V10 do DIYAPP evoluiu para uma arquitetura monolítica que está limitando:
1. Escalabilidade independente de componentes
2. Velocidade de deploy de novas funcionalidades
3. Isolamento de falhas entre módulos
4. Adoção de diferentes stacks tecnológicas por domínio
5. Manutenção paralela por múltiplas squads

**DECISÃO:**
Adotar arquitetura de microsserviços com os seguintes princípios:
1. **12-Factor App** para todos os serviços
2. **Domínio por serviço** (DDD boundaries)
3. **Comunicação**: gRPC para síncrono, Kafka para assíncrono
4. **API Gateway** como único ponto de entrada público
5. **Service Mesh** (Istio) para observabilidade e resiliência
6. **Banco de dados por serviço** (Database-per-service)
7. **Deploy independente** com CI/CD por serviço

**OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:**

**Opção A: Monólito modularizado**
- Prós: Simplicidade operacional, transações ACID fáceis
- Contras: Acoplamento alto, deploy único, escala vertical limitada

**Opção B: Microsserviços leves (REST + RabbitMQ)**
- Prós: Mais simples que gRPC, comunidade grande
- Contras: Overhead HTTP/JSON, sem streaming nativo, tipagem fraca

**Opção C: Microsserviços robustos (gRPC + Kafka)**
- Prós: Performance alta, contrato forte com Protobuf, streaming bidirecional
- Contras: Curva de aprendizado, complexidade operacional maior

**Opção escolhida: C** - Justificativa: DIYAPP V11 precisa de alta performance para processamento de IA em tempo real e contratos fortes para evitar breaking changes entre squads autônomas.

**CONSEQUÊNCIAS:**
**Positivas:**
- Escalabilidade granular por serviço
- Deploy independente por squad
- Stack tecnológica adequada por domínio
- Isolamento de falhas
- Evolução independente de APIs

**Negativas:**
- Complexidade distribuída aumenta
- Transações distribuídas necessárias
- Monitoramento mais complexo
- Latência de rede entre serviços
- Gerenciamento de dados consistente

**Riscos:**
1. **Latência de rede**: Mitigar com cache Redis e connection pooling
2. **Consistência eventual**: Implementar SAGA pattern e compensação
3. **Observabilidade**: Usar OpenTelemetry + Jaeger + Prometheus
4. **Segurança**: mTLS entre serviços, secret management com Vault

**REVISÃO:** 2024-04-15 (3 meses após implementação)

---

## 2. Template de Repositório de Microsserviço

```bash
# Estrutura do template
diyapp-v11-service-template/
├── .github/

## 3. CI/CD Pipeline Integrado

```yaml
# .github/workflows/ci.yml
name: CI Pipeline

on:
  push:
    branches: [ main, develop ]
  pull_request:
    branches: [ main ]

jobs:
  test:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    services:
      postgres:
        image: postgres:14
        env:
          POSTGRES_PASSWORD: postgres
        options: >-
          --health-cmd pg_isready
          --health-interval 10s
          --health-timeout 5s
          --health-retries 5
        ports:
          - 5432:5432
      kafka:
        image: confluentinc/cp-kafka:latest
        env:
          KAFKA_BROKER_ID: 1
          KAFKA_ZOOKEEPER_CONNECT: localhost:2181
        ports:
          - 9092:9092

    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v3
    
    - name: Set up Go
      uses: actions/setup-go@v4
      with:
        go-version: '1.21'
    
    - name: Run linters
      run: |
        go install github.com/golangci/golangci-lint/cmd/golangci-lint@latest
        golangci-lint run --timeout 5m
    
    - name: Run unit tests
      run: |
        go test ./... -v -coverprofile=coverage.out -covermode=atomic
        go tool cover -func=coverage.out
    
    - name: Run integration tests
      run: |
        go test ./tests/integration -v -tags=integration
    
    - name: Security scan
      uses: aquasecurity/trivy-action@master
      with:
        scan-type: 'fs'
        scan-ref: '.'
        format: 'sarif'
        output: 'trivy-results.sarif'
    
    - name: Upload coverage to Codecov
      uses: codecov/codecov-action@v3
      with:
        file: ./coverage.out

  build:
    needs: test
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    if: github.event_name == 'push' || github.event.pull_request.merged == true
    
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v3
    
    - name: Build Docker image
      run: |
        docker build -t ${{ secrets.REGISTRY }}/${{ github.event.repository.name }}:${{ github.sha }} .
    
    - name: Scan Docker image
      uses: aquasecurity/trivy-action@master
      with:
        image-ref: '${{ secrets.REGISTRY }}/${{ github.event.repository.name }}:${{ github.sha }}'
        format: 'sarif'
        output: 'trivy-image-results.sarif'
    
    - name: Push to Registry
      if: success()
      run: |
        echo "${{ secrets.REGISTRY_PASSWORD }}" | docker login ${{ secrets.REGISTRY }} -u ${{ secrets.REGISTRY_USERNAME }} --password-stdin
        docker push ${{ secrets.REGISTRY }}/${{ github.event.repository.name }}:${{ github.sha }}
```

```yaml
# .github/workflows/cd.yml
name: CD Pipeline

on:
  workflow_run:
    workflows: ["CI Pipeline"]
    branches: [main]
    types:
      - completed

jobs:
  deploy-staging:
    if: ${{ github.event.workflow_run.conclusion == 'success' }}
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    environment: staging
    
    steps:
    - name: Deploy to Staging
      uses: appleboy/ssh-action@master
      with:
        host: ${{ secrets.STAGING_HOST }}
        username: ${{ secrets.STAGING_USER }}
        key: ${{ secrets.STAGING_SSH_KEY }}
        script: |
          cd /opt/diyapp/staging
          ./deploy.sh ${{ github.sha }}
    
    - name: Run smoke tests
      run: |
        curl -f ${{ secrets.STAGING_URL }}/health || exit 1
        # Adicionar mais verificações de saúde
    
    - name: Notify Slack
      uses: 8398a7/action-slack@v3
      with:
        status: ${{ job.status }}
        fields: repo,message,commit,author,action,eventName,ref,workflow,job,took
      env:
        SLACK_WEBHOOK_URL: ${{ secrets.SLACK_WEBHOOK }}

  deploy-production:
    needs: deploy-staging
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    environment: production
    
    steps:
    - name: Approve Production Deploy
      uses: trstringer/manual-approval@v1
      with:
        secret: ${{ github.TOKEN }}
        approvers: ${{ secrets.PRODUCTION_APPROVERS }}
        minimum-approvals: 2
    
    - name: Blue-Green Deployment
      uses: appleboy/ssh-action@master
      with:
        host: ${{ secrets.PRODUCTION_HOST }}
        username: ${{ secrets.PRODUCTION_USER }}
        key: ${{ secrets.PRODUCTION_SSH_KEY }}
        script: |
          cd /opt/diyapp/production
          ./blue-green-deploy.sh ${{ github.sha }}
    
    - name: Run canary analysis
      run: |
        # Verificar métricas do Istio
        # Rollback automático se error rate > 1%
    
    - name: Update deployment tracker
      run: |
        curl -X POST https://deploy-tracker.diyapp.internal/deployments \
          -H "Authorization: Bearer ${{ secrets.DEPLOY_TRACKER_TOKEN }}" \
          -d '{"service": "${{ github.event.repository.name }}", "version": "${{ github.sha }}", "environment": "production"}'
```

## 4. Especificação de Comunicação

```proto
// src/proto/service.proto
syntax = "proto3";

package diyapp.v11;

import "google/protobuf/timestamp.proto";
import "google/api/annotations.proto";

option go_package = "github.com/diyapp/v11/proto";

// Serviço de Autenticação
service AuthService {
  rpc Login(LoginRequest) returns (LoginResponse) {
    option (google.api.http) = {
      post: "/v1/auth/login"
      body: "*"
    };
  }
  
  rpc ValidateToken(TokenRequest) returns (TokenResponse);
  
  rpc RefreshToken(RefreshRequest) returns (RefreshResponse);
}

message LoginRequest {
  string email = 1;
  string password = 2;
  string client_id = 3;
}

message LoginResponse {
  string access_token = 1;
  string refresh_token = 2;
  int64 expires_in = 3;
  string token_type = 4;
}

// Serviço de Processamento de IA
service AIService {
  rpc ProcessTask(ProcessRequest) returns (stream ProcessResponse);
  rpc BatchProcess(BatchRequest) returns (BatchResponse);
  rpc GetModelStatus(StatusRequest) returns (StatusResponse);
}

message ProcessRequest {
  string task_id = 1;
  string model = 2;
  bytes input_data = 3;
  map<string, string> parameters = 4;
}

message ProcessResponse {
  enum Status {
    PROCESSING = 0;
    COMPLETED = 1;
    FAILED = 2;
  }
  
  Status status = 1;
  bytes result = 2;
  float progress = 3;
  string error_message = 4;
}

// Eventos Kafka
message TaskEvent {
  string event_id = 1;
  string event_type = 2; // TASK_CREATED, TASK_PROCESSED, TASK_FAILED
  string task_id = 3;
  string service = 4;
  google.protobuf.Timestamp timestamp = 5;
  map<string, string> metadata = 6;
}
```

---

## 5. Configuração do Service Mesh (Istio)

```yaml
# deployments/k8s/istio/virtual-service.yaml
apiVersion: networking.istio.io/v1beta1
kind: VirtualService
metadata:
  name: diyapp-service
spec:
  hosts:
  - diyapp-service
  http:
  - route:
    - destination:
        host: diyapp-service
        subset: v1
      weight: 90
    - destination:
        host: diyapp-service
        subset: v2
      weight: 10
    retries:
      attempts: 3
      perTryTimeout: 2s
      retryOn: gateway-error,connect-failure,refused-stream
    timeout: 10s
---
apiVersion: networking.istio.io/v1beta1
kind: DestinationRule
metadata:
  name: diyapp-service
spec:
  host: diyapp-service
  subsets:
  - name: v1
    labels:
      version: v1.0.0
  - name: v2
    labels:
      version: v1.1.0
  trafficPolicy:
    connectionPool:
      tcp:
        maxConnections: 100
        connectTimeout: 30ms
      http:
        http1MaxPendingRequests: 10
        maxRequestsPerConnection: 10
    outlierDetection:
      consecutive5xxErrors: 5
      interval: 10s
      baseEjectionTime: 30s
      maxEjectionPercent: 50
```

# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Design System & Premium Prototypes

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-design-system/
├── src/
│   ├── design-tokens/
│   │   ├── colors.js
│   │   ├── typography.js

  sm: '0 1px 3px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1), 0 1px 2px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.06)',
  md: '0 4px 6px -1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1), 0 2px 4px -1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.06)',
  lg: '0 10px 15px -3px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1), 0 4px 6px -2px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.05)',
  xl: '0 20px 25px -5px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1), 0 10px 10px -5px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04)',
  '2xl': '0 25px 50px -12px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.25)',
  
  // Premium Glow
  premium: {
    sm: '0 0 10px rgba(14, 165, 233, 0.3)',
    md: '0 0 20px rgba(14, 165, 233, 0.3)',
    lg: '0 0 30px rgba(14, 165, 233, 0.4)',
  },
  
  // Inner Shadows
  inner: 'inset 0 2px 4px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.06)',
  
  // Focus Rings
  focus: {
    primary: '0 0 0 3px rgba(14, 165, 233, 0.5)',
    error: '0 0 0 3px rgba(239, 68, 68, 0.5)',
  },
};

  colors,
  typography,
  spacing,
  shadows,

  borderRadius: {
    none: '0',
    sm: '0.25rem',  // 4px
    md: '0.375rem', // 6px
    lg: '0.5rem',   // 8px
    xl: '0.75rem',  // 12px
    '2xl': '1rem',  // 16px
    full: '9999px',
  },
  
  // Transitions
  transition: {
    duration: {
      fast: '150ms',
      normal: '300ms',
      slow: '500ms',
    },
    easing: {
      easeInOut: 'cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1)',
      easeOut: 'cubic-bezier(0, 0, 0.2, 1)',
      easeIn: 'cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 1, 1)',
      spring: 'cubic-bezier(0.68, -0.55, 0.265, 1.55)',
    },
  },
  
  // Z-Index Scale
  zIndex: {
    hide: -1,
    base: 0,
    docked: 10,
    dropdown: 1000,
    sticky: 1100,
    banner: 1200,
    overlay: 1300,
    modal: 1400,
    popover: 1500,
    skipLink: 1600,

## 2. Component Library - Button Component

### `src/components/Button/Button.jsx`
```javascript
import React from 'react';
import { motion } from 'framer-motion';
import { designTokens } from '../../design-tokens';

const Button = React.forwardRef(({
  children,
  variant = 'primary',
  size = 'md',
  isLoading = false,
  disabled = false,
  fullWidth = false,
  leftIcon,
  rightIcon,
  onClick,
  className = '',
  ...props
}, ref) => {
  const tokens = designTokens;
  
  // Variant Styles
  const variantStyles = {
    primary: {
      bg: tokens.colors.primary[500],
      hoverBg: tokens.colors.primary[600],
      activeBg: tokens.colors.primary[700],
      text: tokens.colors.a11y.textOnPrimary,
      border: 'transparent',
      shadow: tokens.shadows.md,
    },
    secondary: {
      bg: tokens.colors.secondary[500],
      hoverBg: tokens.colors.secondary[600],
      activeBg: tokens.colors.secondary[700],
      text: tokens.colors.a11y.textOnSecondary,
      border: 'transparent',
      shadow: tokens.shadows.md,
    },
    outline: {
      bg: 'transparent',
      hoverBg: tokens.colors.neutral[100],
      activeBg: tokens.colors.neutral[200],
      text: tokens.colors.neutral[700],
      border: tokens.colors.neutral[300],
      shadow: 'none',
    },
    ghost: {
      bg: 'transparent',
      hoverBg: tokens.colors.neutral[100],
      activeBg: tokens.colors.neutral[200],
      text: tokens.colors.neutral[700],
      border: 'transparent',
      shadow: 'none',
    },
    premium: {
      bg: tokens.colors.premium.gradient,
      hoverBg: tokens.colors.premium.gradient,
      activeBg: tokens.colors.premium.gradient,
      text: tokens.colors.a11y.textOnPrimary,
      border: 'transparent',
      shadow: `${tokens.shadows.md}, ${tokens.shadows.premium.sm}`,
    },
  };
  
  // Size Styles
  const sizeStyles = {
    xs: {
      padding: `${tokens.spacing[1]} ${tokens.spacing[2]}`,
      fontSize: tokens.typography.fontSize.xs,
      height: '1.75rem',
    },
    sm: {
      padding: `${tokens.spacing[2]} ${tokens.spacing[3]}`,
      fontSize: tokens.typography.fontSize.sm,
      height: '2rem',
    },
    md: {
      padding: `${tokens.spacing[2]} ${tokens.spacing[4]}`,
      fontSize: tokens.typography.fontSize.base,
      height: '2.5rem',
    },
    lg: {
      padding: `${tokens.spacing[3]} ${tokens.spacing[6]}`,
      fontSize: tokens.typography.fontSize.lg,
      height: '3rem',
    },
  };
  
  const style = variantStyles[variant];
  const sizeStyle = sizeStyles[size];
  
  return (
    <motion.button
      ref={ref}
      className={`button button--${variant} button--${size} ${fullWidth ? 'button--full-width' : ''} ${className}`}
      style={{
        display: 'inline-flex',
        alignItems: 'center',
        justifyContent: 'center',
        gap: tokens.spacing[2],
        backgroundColor: style.bg,
        color: style.text,
        border: `1px solid ${style.border}`,
        borderRadius: tokens.borderRadius.md,
        boxShadow: style.shadow,
        padding: sizeStyle.padding,
        fontSize: sizeStyle.fontSize,
        height: sizeStyle.height,
        minWidth: sizeStyle.height,
        fontWeight: tokens.typography.fontWeight.medium,
        lineHeight: tokens.typography.lineHeight.normal,
        cursor: disabled || isLoading ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer',
        opacity: disabled ? 0.6 : 1,
        width: fullWidth ? '100%' : 'auto',
        position: 'relative',
        overflow: 'hidden',
        transition: `all ${tokens.transition.duration.normal} ${tokens.transition.easing.easeInOut}`,
        outline: 'none',
      }}
      whileHover={!disabled && !isLoading ? {
        scale: 1.02,
        boxShadow: variant === 'premium' 
          ? `${tokens.shadows.lg}, ${tokens.shadows.premium.md}`
          : tokens.shadows.lg,
        backgroundColor: style.hoverBg,
      } : {}}
      whileTap={!disabled && !isLoading ? {
        scale: 0.98,
        boxShadow: tokens.shadows.sm,
        backgroundColor: style.activeBg,
      } : {}}
      onClick={!disabled && !isLoading ? onClick : undefined}
      disabled={disabled || isLoading}
      aria-busy={isLoading}
      {...props}
    >
      {/* Loading Overlay */}
      {isLoading && (
        <motion.div
          style={{
            position: 'absolute',
            top: 0,
            left: 0,
            right: 0,
            bottom: 0,
            backgroundColor: 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.3)',
            display: 'flex',
            alignItems: 'center',
            justifyContent: 'center',
          }}
          initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
          animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
          transition={{ duration: 0.2 }}
        >
          <motion.div
            style={{
              width: '1rem',
              height: '1rem',
              border: `2px solid ${style.text}`,
              borderTopColor: 'transparent',
              borderRadius: '50%',
            }}
            animate={{ rotate: 360 }}
            transition={{
              duration: 1,
              repeat: Infinity,
              ease: 'linear',
            }}
          />
        </motion.div>
      )}
      
      {/* Left Icon */}
      {leftIcon && !isLoading && (
        <motion.span
          initial={{ scale: 0.8, opacity: 0 }}
          animate={{ scale: 1, opacity: 1 }}
          transition={{ duration: 0.2 }}
        >
          {leftIcon}
        </motion.span>
      )}
      
      {/* Button Text */}
      <motion.span
        animate={{
          opacity: isLoading ? 0.7 : 1,
        }}
      >
        {children}
      </motion.span>
      
      {/* Right Icon */}
      {rightIcon && !isLoading && (
        <motion.span
          initial={{ scale: 0.8, opacity: 0 }}
          animate={{ scale: 1, opacity: 1 }}
          transition={{ duration: 0.2 }}
        >
          {rightIcon}
        </motion.span>
      )}
      
      {/* Premium Glow Effect */}
      {variant === 'premium' && !disabled && (
        <motion.div
          style={{
            position: 'absolute',
            top: 0,
            left: 0,
            right: 0,
            bottom: 0,
            borderRadius: tokens.borderRadius.md,
            boxShadow: tokens.shadows.premium.lg,


### [Sessão Paralela: Data Engineer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Data Lake para Telemetria

## 1. Arquitetura do Data Lake - Diagrama Star Schema

```
DIYAPP Data Lake - Star Schema
================================

FATO_TELEMETRIA (Fact Table)
-----------------------------
- telemetria_id (PK, UUID)
- session_id (FK → DIM_SESSAO)
- user_id (FK → DIM_USUARIO)
- feature_id (FK → DIM_FEATURE)
- timestamp_id (FK → DIM_TEMPO)
- location_id (FK → DIM_LOCALIZACAO)
- device_id (FK → DIM_DISPOSITIVO)
- event_type (click, error, performance, custom)
- event_value (JSON - dados específicos do evento)
- duration_ms (para eventos de performance)
- error_code (para eventos de erro)
- http_status (para requisições HTTP)
- created_at (timestamp do evento)

DIM_USUARIO (Dimension Table)
-----------------------------
- user_id (PK)
- user_tier (free, pro, enterprise)
- account_age_days
- registration_date
- last_active_date
- country
- language
- is_active (boolean)
- subscription_status

DIM_SESSAO (Dimension Table)
---------------------------
- session_id (PK)
- session_start
- session_end
- session_duration_seconds
- pages_visited
- events_count
- is_completed (boolean)
- exit_reason (timeout, user_exit, error)

DIM_FEATURE (Dimension Table)
-----------------------------
- feature_id (PK)
- feature_name
- feature_category (ui, api, background, integration)
- feature_version
- module_name
- is_experimental (boolean)
- release_date

DIM_TEMPO (Dimension Table)
--------------------------
- timestamp_id (PK)
- event_timestamp
- year
- quarter
- month
- week
- day
- hour
- minute
- day_of_week
- is_weekend (boolean)
- hour_of_day

DIM_LOCALIZACAO (Dimension Table)
--------------------------------
- location_id (PK)
- country
- region
- city
- timezone
- latitude
- longitude
- network_provider
- connection_type (wifi, mobile, ethernet)

DIM_DISPOSITIVO (Dimension Table)
--------------------------------
- device_id (PK)
- device_type (desktop, mobile, tablet)
- os_name
- os_version
- browser_name
- browser_version
- screen_resolution
- device_manufacturer
- device_model
- memory_mb
- cpu_cores

DIM_ERRO (Dimension Table - SCD Type 2)
--------------------------------------
- error_id (PK)
- error_code
- error_message
- error_category (client, server, network, validation)
- severity (low, medium, high, critical)
- component_name
- start_date (SCD Type 2)
- end_date (SCD Type 2)
- is_current (boolean)
```

## 3. Pipeline Apache Beam em Tempo Real (Python)

```python
# src/pipelines/realtime/beam_pipeline.py
"""
Pipeline Apache Beam para processamento de telemetria em tempo real
Processa eventos de click, performance e erros da DIYAPP
"""

import apache_beam as beam
from apache_beam.options.pipeline_options import PipelineOptions
from apache_beam.io.gcp.pubsub import ReadFromPubSub
from apache_beam.io.gcp.bigquery import WriteToBigQuery
from apache_beam.io.gcp.bigquery_tools import parse_table_schema_from_json
import json
import logging
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Dict, Any, List
import hashlib

# Configuração de logging
logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class TelemetryEvent:
    """Classe para representar eventos de telemetria"""
    
    def __init__(self, raw_event: Dict[str, Any]):
        self.raw_event = raw_event
        self.event_type = raw_event.get('event_type', 'unknown')
        self.timestamp = raw_event.get('timestamp', datetime.utcnow().isoformat())
        self.session_id = raw_event.get('session_id')
        self.user_id = raw_event.get('user_id')
        self.validate()
    
    def validate(self) -> bool:
        """Validação básica do evento"""
        required_fields = ['event_type', 'session_id', 'user_id']
        for field in required_fields:
            if not getattr(self, field):
                raise ValueError(f"Campo obrigatório faltando: {field}")
        return True
    
    def generate_id(self) -> str:
        """Gera ID único para o evento"""
        content = f"{self.session_id}_{self.user_id}_{self.timestamp}_{self.event_type}"
        return hashlib.md5(content.encode()).hexdigest()

class ParseTelemetryEvent(beam.DoFn):
    """Transformação para parsear eventos de telemetria"""
    
    def process(self, element: bytes, *args, **kwargs):
        try:
            raw_event = json.loads(element.decode('utf-8'))
            event = TelemetryEvent(raw_event)
            
            # Enriquecer evento com dados adicionais
            enriched_event = self._enrich_event(event)
            
            # Validar qualidade dos dados
            if self._validate_quality(enriched_event):
                yield enriched_event
            else:
                logger.warning(f"Evento falhou validação de qualidade: {event.event_type}")
                
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Erro ao processar evento: {e}")
            # Enviar para dead letter queue
            error_event = {
                'raw_event': element.decode('utf-8'),
                'error': str(e),
                'timestamp': datetime.utcnow().isoformat()
            }
            yield beam.pvalue.TaggedOutput('errors', error_event)
    
    def _enrich_event(self, event: TelemetryEvent) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Enriquece evento com dados adicionais"""
        enriched = {
            'telemetria_id': event.generate_id(),
            'session_id': event.session_id,
            'user_id': event.user_id,
            'event_type': event.event_type,
            'event_timestamp': event.timestamp,
            'processed_at': datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
            'event_value': json.dumps(event.raw_event.get('event_value', {})),
            'duration_ms': event.raw_event.get('duration_ms'),
            'error_code': event.raw_event.get('error_code'),
            'http_status': event.raw_event.get('http_status'),
            'feature_name': event.raw_event.get('feature_name'),
            'device_info': event.raw_event.get('device_info', {}),
            'location_info': event.raw_event.get('location_info', {})
        }
        
        # Extrair dimensões do evento
        enriched.update(self._extract_dimensions(event.raw_event))
        
        return enriched
    
    def _extract_dimensions(self, raw_event: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Extrai dimensões do evento para o star schema"""
        dimensions = {}
        
        # Extrair dados de tempo
        event_time = datetime.fromisoformat(raw_event.get('timestamp', datetime.utcnow().isoformat()))
        dimensions.update({
            'year': event_time.year,
            'month': event_time.month,
            'day': event_time.day,
            'hour': event_time.hour,
            'minute': event_time.minute,
            'day_of_week': event_time.weekday(),
            'is_weekend': event_time.weekday() >= 5
        })
        
        # Extrair dados de dispositivo
        device_info = raw_event.get('device_info', {})
        dimensions.update({
            'device_type': device_info.get('type'),
            'os_name': device_info.get('os'),
            'browser_name': device_info.get('browser'),
            'screen_resolution': device_info.get('resolution')
        })
        
        # Extrair dados de localização
        location_info = raw_event.get('location_info', {})
        dimensions.update({
            'country': location_info.get('country'),
            'city': location_info.get('city'),
            'timezone': location_info.get('timezone')
        })
        
        return dimensions
    
    def _validate_quality(self, event: Dict[str, Any]) -> bool:
        """Valida qualidade dos dados do evento"""
        quality_rules = [
            ('session_id', lambda x: x is not None and len(x) > 0),
            ('user_id', lambda x: x is not None and len(x) > 0),
            ('event_timestamp', lambda x: x is not None),
            ('event_type', lambda x: x in ['click', 'error', 'performance', 'custom', 'pageview'])
        ]
        
        for field, rule in quality_rules:
            if not rule(event.get(field)):
                logger.warning(f"Regra de qualidade falhou para campo {field}: {event.get(field)}")
                return False
        
        return True

class CalculateSessionMetrics(beam.DoFn):
    """Calcula métricas de sessão em tempo real"""
    
    def __init__(self, session_timeout_seconds=1800):
        self.session_timeout = session_timeout_seconds
    
    def process(self, element: Dict[str, Any], *args, **kwargs):
        # Implementar lógica de sessão
        # Agrupar eventos por session_id e calcular:
        # - Duração da sessão
        # - Número de eventos
        # - Páginas visitadas
        # - Status de conclusão
        
        session_metrics = {
            'session_id': element['session_id'],
            'user_id': element['user_id'],
            'session_start': element['event_timestamp'],
            'session_end': element['event_timestamp'],  # Será atualizado
            'events_count': 1,
            'pages_visited': 1 if element['event_type'] == 'pageview' else 0,
            'last_event_time': element['event_timestamp']
        }
        
        yield session_metrics

class WindowedAggregations(beam.PTransform):
    """Agregações em janelas de tempo"""
    
    def __init__(self, window_duration_seconds=300):
        self.window_duration = window_duration_seconds
    
    def expand(self, pcoll):
        return (
            pcoll
            | 'WindowIntoFixed' >> beam.WindowInto(
                beam.window.FixedWindows(self.window_duration)
            )
            | 'ExtractEventType' >> beam.Map(lambda x: (x['event_type'], 1))
            | 'CountByEventType' >> beam.CombinePerKey(sum)
            | 'FormatAggregation' >> beam.Map(
                lambda x: {
                    'window_start': datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
                    'event_type': x[0],
                    'count': x[1],
                    'window_duration_seconds': self.window_duration
                }
            )
        )

def run_pipeline(project_id: str, input_topic: str, output_table: str):
    """Executa o pipeline Apache Beam"""
    
    # Schema BigQuery para fato_telemetria
    fact_schema = {
        'fields': [
            {'name': 'telemetria_id', 'type': 'STRING', 'mode': 'REQUIRED'},
            {'name': 'session_id', 'type': 'STRING', 'mode': 'REQUIRED'},
            {'name': 'user_id', 'type': 'STRING', 'mode': 'REQUIRED'},
            {'name': 'event_type', 'type': 'STRING', 'mode': 'REQUIRED'},
            {'name': 'event_timestamp', 'type': 'TIMESTAMP', 'mode': 'REQUIRED'},
            {'name': 'processed_at', 'type': 'TIMESTAMP', 'mode': 'REQUIRED'},
            {'name': 'event_value', 'type': 'STRING', 'mode': 'NULLABLE'},
            {'name': 'duration_ms', 'type': 'INTEGER', 'mode': 'NULLABLE'},
            {'name': 'error_code', 'type': 'STRING', 'mode': 'NULLABLE'},
            {'name': 'http_status', 'type': 'INTEGER', 'mode': 'NULLABLE'},
            {'name': 'feature_name', 'type': 'STRING', 'mode': 'NULLABLE'},
            {'name': 'year', 'type': 'INTEGER', 'mode': 'NULLABLE'},
            {'name': 'month', 'type': 'INTEGER', 'mode': 'NULLABLE'},
            {'name': 'day', 'type': 'INTEGER', 'mode': 'NULLABLE'},
            {'name': 'hour', 'type': 'INTEGER', 'mode': 'NULLABLE'},
            {'name': 'minute', 'type': 'INTEGER', 'mode': 'NULLABLE'},
            {'name': 'day_of_week', 'type': 'INTEGER', 'mode': 'NULLABLE'},
            {'name': 'is_weekend', 'type': 'BOOLEAN', 'mode': 'NULLABLE'},
            {'name': 'device_type', 'type': 'STRING', 'mode': 'NULLABLE'},
            {'name': 'os_name', 'type': 'STRING', 'mode': 'NULLABLE'},
            {'name': 'browser_name', 'type': 'STRING', 'mode': 'NULLABLE'},
            {'name': 'screen_resolution', 'type': 'STRING', 'mode': 'NULLABLE'},
            {'name': 'country', 'type': 'STRING', 'mode': 'NULLABLE'},
            {'name': 'city', 'type': 'STRING', 'mode': 'NULLABLE'},
            {'name': 'timezone', 'type': 'STRING', 'mode': 'NULLABLE'}
        ]
    }
    
    # Schema para métricas de sessão
    session_schema = {
        'fields': [
            {'name': 'session_id', 'type': 'STRING', 'mode': 'REQUIRED'},
            {'name': 'user_id', 'type': 'STRING', 'mode': 'REQUIRED'},
            {'name': 'session_start', 'type': 'TIMESTAMP', 'mode': 'REQUIRED'},
            {'name': 'session_end', 'type': 'TIMESTAMP', 'mode': 'REQUIRED'},
            {'name': 'session_duration_seconds', 'type': 'INTEGER', 'mode': 'NULLABLE'},
            {'name': 'events_count', 'type': 'INTEGER', 'mode': 'NULLABLE'},
            {'name': 'pages_visited', 'type': 'INTEGER', 'mode': 'NULLABLE'},
            {'name': 'is_completed', 'type': 'BOOLEAN', 'mode': 'NULLABLE'},
            {'name': 'exit_reason', 'type': 'STRING', 'mode': 'NULLABLE'}
        ]
    }
    
    # Opções do pipeline
    pipeline_options = PipelineOptions(
        streaming=True,
        save_main_session=True,
        project=project_id,
        region='us-central1',
        temp_location=f'gs://{project_id}-temp/temp',
        staging_location=f'gs://{project_id}-temp/staging'
    )
    
    with beam.Pipeline(options=pipeline_options) as pipeline:
        # Ler eventos do Pub/Sub
        events = (
            pipeline
            | 'ReadFromPubSub' >> ReadFromPubSub(topic=input_topic)
            | 'ParseEvents' >> beam.ParDo(ParseTelemetryEvent()).with_outputs('errors', main='main')
        )
        
        # Processar eventos principais
        main_events = events.main
        
        # Escrever eventos no BigQuery (fato_telemetria)
        _ = (
            main_events
            | 'WriteToBigQuery' >> WriteToBigQuery

### [Sessão Paralela: Backend]

## 3. Configuração Redis Cluster (src/config/redis-cluster.js)

```javascript
const Redis = require('ioredis');
const config = require('./index');
const logger = require('../utils/logger');

class RedisClusterManager {
  constructor() {
    this.cluster = null;
    this.circuitBreakerState = 'CLOSED';
    this.failureCount = 0;
    this.MAX_FAILURES = 3;
    this.RESET_TIMEOUT = 30000; // 30 seconds
  }

  async connect() {
    try {
      const options = {
        scaleReads: 'slave',
        retryDelayOnFailover: 100,
        retryDelayOnClusterDown: 100,
        retryDelayOnTryAgain: 100,
        maxRetriesPerRequest: 3,
        enableReadyCheck: true,
        enableOfflineQueue: true,
        redisOptions: {
          password: config.REDIS_PASSWORD,
          tls: config.REDIS_TLS ? {} : undefined,
          connectTimeout: 5000,
          maxRetriesPerRequest: 1,
          retryStrategy: (times) => {
            if (times > 3) {
              this.handleFailure();
              return null; // Stop retrying
            }
            return Math.min(times * 100, 3000);
          }
        }
      };

      this.cluster = new Redis.Cluster(config.REDIS_CLUSTER_NODES, options);

      // Event listeners for monitoring
      this.cluster.on('connect', () => {
        logger.info('Redis Cluster connected');
        this.circuitBreakerState = 'CLOSED';
        this.failureCount = 0;
      });

      this.cluster.on('error', (err) => {
        logger.error('Redis Cluster error:', { error: err.message });
        this.handleFailure();
      });

      this.cluster.on('close', () => {
        logger.warn('Redis Cluster connection closed');
        this.handleFailure();
      });

      // Test connection
      await this.cluster.ping();
      logger.info('Redis Cluster connection test successful');
      
      return this.cluster;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Failed to connect to Redis Cluster:', { error: error.message });
      this.handleFailure();
      throw error;
    }
  }

  handleFailure() {
    this.failureCount++;
    if (this.failureCount >= this.MAX_FAILURES && this.circuitBreakerState === 'CLOSED') {
      this.circuitBreakerState = 'OPEN';
      logger.warn('Redis Cluster circuit breaker OPENED');
      
      // Auto-reset after timeout
      setTimeout(() => {
        this.circuitBreakerState = 'HALF_OPEN';
        logger.info('Redis Cluster circuit breaker HALF_OPEN');
      }, this.RESET_TIMEOUT);
    }
  }

  async execute(command, ...args) {
    if (this.circuitBreakerState === 'OPEN') {
      throw new Error('Redis Cluster circuit breaker is OPEN');
    }

    try {
      const result = await this.cluster[command](...args);
      
      if (this.circuitBreakerState === 'HALF_OPEN') {
        this.circuitBreakerState = 'CLOSED';
        this.failureCount = 0;
        logger.info('Redis Cluster circuit breaker CLOSED');
      }
      
      return result;
    } catch (error) {
      this.handleFailure();
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async get(key) {
    return this.execute('get', key);
  }

  async set(key, value, ttl = null) {
    if (ttl) {
      return this.execute('setex', key, ttl, value);
    }
    return this.execute('set', key, value);
  }

  async del(key) {
    return this.execute('del', key);
  }

  async hset(hash, field, value) {
    return this.execute('hset', hash, field, value);
  }

  async hget(hash, field) {
    return this.execute('hget', hash, field);
  }

  async hgetall(hash) {
    return this.execute('hgetall', hash);
  }

  async expire(key, seconds) {
    return this.execute('expire', key, seconds);
  }

  async exists(key) {
    return this.execute('exists', key);
  }

  async disconnect() {
    if (this.cluster) {
      await this.cluster.quit();
      logger.info('Redis Cluster disconnected');
    }
  }

  getStatus() {
    return {
      circuitBreaker: this.circuitBreakerState,
      failureCount: this.failureCount,
      connected: this.cluster && this.cluster.status === 'ready'
    };
  }
}

// Singleton instance
const redisCluster = new RedisClusterManager();

module.exports = redisCluster;
```

## 4. Serviço de Autenticação (src/services/auth/auth.service.js)

```javascript
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const bcrypt = require('bcrypt');
const { Issuer } = require('openid-client');
const config = require('../../config');
const logger = require('../../utils/logger');
const redisCluster = require('../../config/redis-cluster');
const CircuitBreaker = require('circuit-breaker-js');

class AuthService {
  constructor() {
    this.oidcClient = null;
    this.db = require('../../db'); // PostgreSQL connection
    
    // Circuit breaker for OAuth2 provider
    this.oauthCircuitBreaker = new CircuitBreaker({
      timeoutDuration: 10000,
      volumeThreshold: 10,
      errorThreshold: 50
    });
    
    this.initializeOIDC();
  }

  async initializeOIDC() {
    try {
      const issuer = await Issuer.discover(config.OAUTH2_AUTH_URL.replace('/auth', ''));
      this.oidcClient = new issuer.Client({
        client_id: config.OAUTH2_CLIENT_ID,
        client_secret: config.OAUTH2_CLIENT_SECRET,
        redirect_uris: [config.OAUTH2_REDIRECT_URI],
        response_types: ['code']
      });
      logger.info('OIDC client initialized');
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Failed to initialize OIDC client:', { error: error.message });
    }
  }

  async registerUser(email, password, name) {
    // Input validation
    if (!email || !password || !name) {
      throw new Error('Missing required fields');
    }

    if (password.length < 8) {
      throw new Error('Password must be at least 8 characters');
    }

    // Check if user exists
    const existingUser = await this.db('users').where({ email }).first();
    if (existingUser) {
      throw new Error('User already exists');
    }

    // Hash password with bcrypt
    const saltRounds = 10;
    const passwordHash = await bcrypt.hash(password, saltRounds);

    // Create user in transaction
    const trx = await this.db.transaction();
    try {
      const [userId] = await trx('users').insert({
        email,
        password_hash: passwordHash,
        name,
        created_at: new Date(),
        updated_at: new Date()
      }).returning('id');

      // Create default user profile
      await trx('user_profiles').insert({
        user_id: userId,
        email_verified: false,
        login_count: 0,
        last_login: null
      });

      await trx.commit();

      // Generate JWT token
      const token = this.generateToken(userId, email);

      // Store session in Redis with TTL
      await redisCluster.set(`session:${userId}`, JSON.stringify({
        userId,
        email,
        lastActivity: new Date().toISOString()
      }), 86400); // 24 hours

      logger.info('User registered successfully', { userId, email: this.maskEmail(email) });

      return {
        userId,
        email,
        name,
        token,
        expiresIn: 86400
      };
    } catch (error) {
      await trx.rollback();
      logger.error('User registration failed:', { 
        error: error.message,
        email: this.maskEmail(email)
      });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async loginUser(email, password) {
    // Rate limiting check
    const attemptsKey = `login_attempts:${email}`;
    const attempts = await redisCluster.get(attemptsKey) || 0;
    
    if (parseInt(attempts) >= 5) {
      throw new Error('Too many login attempts. Please try again later.');
    }

    try {
      // Find user
      const user = await this.db('users')
        .select('id', 'email', 'password_hash', 'name')
        .where({ email })
        .first();

      if (!user) {
        await this.incrementLoginAttempts(email);
        throw new Error('Invalid credentials');
      }

      // Verify password
      const isValid = await bcrypt.compare(password, user.password_hash);
      if (!isValid) {
        await this.incrementLoginAttempts(email);
        throw new Error('Invalid credentials');
      }

      // Reset login attempts on successful login
      await redisCluster.del(attemptsKey);

      // Update user profile
      await this.db('user_profiles')
        .where({ user_id: user

### [Sessão Paralela: Frontend]

## 1. package.json
```json
{
  "name": "diyapp-evolution-v11",

  "private": true,

## 2. next.config.js
```javascript
/** @type {import('next').NextConfig} */
const nextConfig = {
  reactStrictMode: true,
  swcMinify: true,
  experimental: {
    optimizeCss: true,
  },
  compiler: {
    removeConsole: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production',
  },
  images: {
    formats: ['image/avif', 'image/webp'],
    deviceSizes: [640, 750, 828, 1080, 1200, 1920, 2048, 3840],
    imageSizes: [16, 32, 48, 64, 96, 128, 256, 384],
    remotePatterns: [
      {
        protocol: 'https',
        hostname: '**',
      },
    ],
  },
  async headers() {
    return [
      {
        source: '/(.*)',
        headers: [
          {
            key: 'X-Content-Type-Options',
            value: 'nosniff',
          },
          {
            key: 'X-Frame-Options',
            value: 'DENY',
          },
          {
            key: 'X-XSS-Protection',
            value: '1; mode=block',
          },
        ],
      },
    ];
  },
};

const withBundleAnalyzer = require('@next/bundle-analyzer')({
  enabled: process.env.ANALYZE === 'true',
});

module.exports = withBundleAnalyzer(nextConfig);
```

## 4. src/app/layout.tsx
```tsx
import type { Metadata } from 'next'
import { Inter } from 'next/font/google'
import './globals.css'
import { TelemetryProvider } from '@/lib/telemetry'
import { PerformanceMonitor } from '@/components/ui/PerformanceMonitor'
import { Navigation } from '@/components/layout/Navigation'

const inter = Inter({ subsets: ['latin'] })

export const metadata: Metadata = {
  title: 'DIYAPP Evolution V11 - Dashboard',
  description: 'Autonomous squad management platform with AI integration',
  viewport: 'width=device-width, initial-scale=1, maximum-scale=5',
  robots: 'index, follow',
}

export default function RootLayout({
  children,
}: {
  children: React.ReactNode
}) {
  return (
    <html lang="en" className={inter.className}>
      <head>
        <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com" />
        <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.gstatic.com" crossOrigin="anonymous" />
        <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Inter:wght@300;400;500;600;700&family=JetBrains+Mono:wght@400;500&display=swap" rel="stylesheet" />
      </head>
      <body className="min-h-screen bg-neutral-50 text-neutral-900">
        <TelemetryProvider>
          <div className="flex min-h-screen">
            <Navigation />
            <main className="flex-1 p-6 md:p-8">
              <PerformanceMonitor />
              {children}
            </main>
          </div>
        </TelemetryProvider>
      </body>
    </html>
  )
}

## 5. src/app/page.tsx (Dashboard principal)
```tsx
import { Suspense } from 'react'
import dynamic from 'next/dynamic'
import { Card } from '@/components/ui/Card'
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/Button'
import { Activity, Users, Zap, TrendingUp } from 'lucide-react'
import { LoadingSpinner } from '@/components/ui/Loading/Spinner'

// Lazy load heavy components
const MetricsChart = dynamic(() => import('@/components/ui/MetricsChart'), {
  loading: () => <LoadingSpinner />,
  ssr: false,
})

const SquadStatus = dynamic(() => import('@/components/ui/SquadStatus'), {
  loading: () => <LoadingSpinner />,
})

const RecentActivity = dynamic(() => import('@/components/ui/RecentActivity'), {
  loading: () => <LoadingSpinner />,
})

const PerformanceWidget = dynamic(() => import('@/components/ui/PerformanceWidget'), {
  loading: () => <LoadingSpinner />,
})

export default function DashboardPage() {
  const stats = [
    {
      title: 'Active Squads',
      value: '12',
      change: '+2',
      icon: Users,
      color: 'primary',
    },
    {
      title: 'Avg Response Time',
      value: '142ms',
      change: '-18ms',
      icon: Zap,
      color: 'success',
    },
    {
      title: 'Tasks Completed',
      value: '1,847',
      change: '+12%',
      icon: TrendingUp,
      color: 'warning',
    },
    {
      title: 'System Uptime',
      value: '99.97%',
      change: '+0.03%',
      icon: Activity,
      color: 'primary',
    },
  ]

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="flex flex-col md:flex-row md:items-center justify-between gap-4">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold text-neutral-900">DIYAPP Evolution V11</h1>
          <p className="text-neutral-600 mt-2">Autonomous squad performance dashboard</p>
        </div>
        <div className="flex gap-3">
          <Button variant="outline" size="lg">
            Generate Report
          </Button>
          <Button variant="primary" size="lg">
            New Squad
          </Button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Stats Grid */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-4 gap-4">
        {stats.map((stat) => (
          <Card key={stat.title} className="p-6">
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
              <div>
                <p className="text-sm font-medium text-neutral-600">{stat.title}</p>
                <div className="flex items-baseline mt-2">
                  <span className="text-2xl font-bold text-neutral-900">{stat.value}</span>
                  <span className={`ml-2 text-sm font-medium ${
                    stat.change.startsWith('+') ? 'text-success-500' : 'text-error-500'
                  }`}>
                    {stat.change}
                  </span>
                </div>
              </div>
              <div className={`p-3 rounded-lg bg-${stat.color}-50`}>
                <stat.icon className={`h-6 w-6 text-${stat.color}-500`} />
              </div>
            </div>
          </Card>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* Main Content Grid */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-6">
        {/* Left Column */}
        <div className="lg:col-span-2 space-y-6">
          <Suspense fallback={<LoadingSpinner />}>
            <Card className="p-6">
              <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold mb-4">Performance Metrics</h2>
              <div className="h-80">
                <MetricsChart />
              </div>
            </Card>
          </Suspense>

          <Suspense fallback={<LoadingSpinner />}>
            <Card className="p-6">
              <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold mb-4">Recent Activity</h2>
              <RecentActivity />
            </Card>
          </Suspense>
        </div>

        {/* Right Column */}
        <div className="space-y-6">
          <Suspense fallback={<LoadingSpinner />}>
            <Card className="p-6">
              <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold mb-4">Squad Status</h2>
              <SquadStatus />
            </Card>
          </Suspense>

          <Suspense fallback={<LoadingSpinner />}>
            <PerformanceWidget />
          </Suspense>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}
```

## 6. src/components/ui/Button/index.tsx
```tsx
import React from 'react'
import { cva, type VariantProps } from 'class-variance-authority'
import { clsx } from 'clsx'
import { twMerge } from 'tailwind-merge'

const buttonVariants = cva(
  'inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-lg font-medium transition-colors focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-primary-500 focus-visible:ring-offset-2 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50',
  {
    variants: {
      variant: {
        primary: 'bg-primary-600 text-white hover:bg-primary-700 active:bg-primary-800',
        secondary: 'bg-neutral-100 text-neutral-900 hover:bg-neutral-200 active:bg-neutral-300',
        outline: 'border border-neutral-300 bg-transparent hover:bg-neutral-50 active:bg-neutral-100',
        ghost: 'bg-transparent hover:bg-neutral-100 active:bg-neutral-200',
        danger: 'bg-error-500 text-white hover:bg-error-600 active:bg-error-700',
      },
      size: {
        sm: 'h-8 px-3 text-sm',
        md: 'h-10 px-4 text-base',
        lg: 'h-12 px-6 text-lg',
      },
    },
    defaultVariants: {
      variant: 'primary',
      size: 'md',
    },
  }
)

export interface ButtonProps
  extends React.ButtonHTMLAttributes<HTMLButtonElement>,
    VariantProps<typeof buttonVariants> {
  loading?: boolean
  icon?: React.ReactNode
}

const Button = React.forwardRef<HTMLButtonElement, ButtonProps>(
  ({ className, variant, size, loading, icon, children, disabled, ...props }, ref) => {
    return (
      <button
        className={twMerge(clsx(buttonVariants({ variant, size, className })))}
        ref={ref}
        disabled={disabled || loading}
        aria-busy={loading}
        {...props}
      >
        {loading && (
          <svg
            className="animate-spin -ml-1 mr-2 h-4 w-4"
            xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"
            fill="none"
            viewBox="0 0 24 24"
            aria-hidden="true"
          >
            <circle
              className="opacity-25"
              cx="12"
              cy="12"
              r="10"
              stroke="currentColor"
              strokeWidth="4"
            />
            <path
              className="opacity-75"
              fill="currentColor"
              d="M4 12a8 8 0 018-8V0C5.373 0 0 5.373 0 12h4zm2 5.291A7.962 7.962 0 014 12H0c0 3.042 1.135 5.824 3 7.938l3-2.647z"
            />
          </svg>
        )}
        {icon && !loading && <span className="mr-2">{icon}</span>}
        {children}
      </button>
    )
  }
)

Button.displayName = 'Button'

export { Button, buttonVariants }
```

## 7. src/components/ui/Card/index.tsx
```tsx
import React from 'react'
import { clsx } from 'clsx

### [Sessão Paralela: SRE]
```hcl
# ============================================
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core
# Infrastructure as Code - Multi-Cloud Setup
# SRE Senior: Multi-Cloud Kubernetes with Istio & Monitoring
# ============================================

# ============================================
# 1. PROVIDERS CONFIGURATION (AWS & GCP)
# ============================================

# AWS Provider Configuration
provider "aws" {
  region = var.aws_region
  
  default_tags {
    tags = {
      Project     = "diyapp-v11"
      Environment = var.environment
      ManagedBy   = "terraform"
      Squad       = "autonomous-senior-squad"
    }
  }
}

# GCP Provider Configuration
provider "google" {
  project = var.gcp_project_id
  region  = var.gcp_region
}

# ============================================
# 2. VARIABLES DEFINITION
# ============================================

variable "environment" {
  description = "Environment (staging/production)"
  type        = string
  default     = "staging"
  
  validation {
    condition     = contains(["staging", "production"], var.environment)
    error_message = "Environment must be 'staging' or 'production'."
  }
}

variable "aws_region" {
  description = "AWS region"
  type        = string
  default     = "us-east-1"
}

variable "gcp_project_id" {
  description = "GCP Project ID"
  type        = string
}

variable "gcp_region" {
  description = "GCP region"
  type        = string
  default     = "us-central1"
}

variable "cluster_name" {
  description = "Kubernetes cluster name"
  type        = string
  default     = "diyapp-v11-cluster"
}

variable "node_count" {
  description = "Number of worker nodes"
  type        = number
  default     = 3
}

variable "machine_type" {
  description = "Machine type for nodes"
  type        = string
  default     = "e2-standard-4"
}

variable "prometheus_retention_days" {
  description = "Prometheus metrics retention days"
  type        = number
  default     = 15
}

# ============================================
# 3. AWS EKS CLUSTER (PRIMARY)
# ============================================

# VPC for EKS
module "aws_vpc" {
  source = "terraform-aws-modules/vpc/aws"
  
  name = "${var.cluster_name}-vpc"
  cidr = "10.0.0.0/16"
  
  azs             = ["${var.aws_region}a", "${var.aws_region}b", "${var.aws_region}c"]
  private_subnets = ["10.0.1.0/24", "10.0.2.0/24", "10.0.3.0/24"]
  public_subnets  = ["10.0.101.0/24", "10.0.102.0/24", "10.0.103.0/24"]
  
  enable_nat_gateway   = true
  single_nat_gateway   = true
  enable_dns_hostnames = true
  
  tags = {
    "kubernetes.io/cluster/${var.cluster_name}" = "shared"
  }
}

# EKS Cluster
module "aws_eks" {
  source = "terraform-aws-modules/eks/aws"
  
  cluster_name    = "${var.cluster_name}-aws"
  cluster_version = "1.28"
  
  vpc_id     = module.aws_vpc.vpc_id
  subnet_ids = module.aws_vpc.private_subnets
  
  eks_managed_node_groups = {
    diyapp_nodes = {
      min_size     = var.node_count
      max_size     = var.node_count * 2
      desired_size = var.node_count
      
      instance_types = ["t3.medium"]
      capacity_type  = "ON_DEMAND"
      
      labels = {
        Environment = var.environment
        Role        = "diyapp-worker"
      }
      
      tags = {
        "k8s.io/cluster-autoscaler/enabled"               = "true"
        "k8s.io/cluster-autoscaler/${var.cluster_name}" = "owned"
      }
    }
  }
  
  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
  }
}

# ============================================
# 4. GCP GKE CLUSTER (SECONDARY/FALLBACK)
# ============================================

# GKE Cluster
resource "google_container_cluster" "gke_primary" {
  name     = "${var.cluster_name}-gcp"
  location = var.gcp_region
  
  # We'll use autopilot for simplicity and cost optimization
  enable_autopilot = true
  
  network    = "default"
  subnetwork = "default"
  
  ip_allocation_policy {
    # Let GCP manage IP allocation
  }
  
  private_cluster_config {
    enable_private_nodes    = true
    enable_private_endpoint = false
    master_ipv4_cidr_block  = "172.16.0.0/28"
  }
  
  release_channel {
    channel = "REGULAR"
  }
  
  workload_identity_config {
    workload_pool = "${var.gcp_project_id}.svc.id.goog"
  }
  
  addons_config {
    horizontal_pod_autoscaling {
      disabled = false
    }
    
    http_load_balancing {
      disabled = false
    }
  }
  
  lifecycle {
    ignore_changes = [
      node_pool,
    ]
  }
}

# ============================================
# 5. ISTIO SERVICE MESH
# ============================================

# Istio Operator for AWS EKS
resource "kubernetes_namespace" "istio_system" {
  metadata {
    name = "istio-system"
    labels = {
      istio-injection = "disabled"
    }
  }
  
  depends_on = [module.aws_eks]
}

resource "helm_release" "istio_base" {
  name       = "istio-base"
  repository = "https://istio-release.storage.googleapis.com/charts"
  chart      = "base"
  namespace  = kubernetes_namespace.istio_system.metadata[0].name
  version    = "1.19.0"
  
  set {
    name  = "global.istioNamespace"
    value = "istio-system"
  }
}

resource "helm_release" "istiod" {
  name       = "istiod"
  repository = "https://istio-release.storage.googleapis.com/charts"
  chart      = "istiod"
  namespace  = kubernetes_namespace.istio_system.metadata[0].name
  version    = "1.19.0"
  
  set {
    name  = "meshConfig.accessLogFile"
    value = "/dev/stdout"
  }
  
  set {
    name  = "meshConfig.enableTracing"
    value = "true"
  }
  
  depends_on = [helm_release.istio_base]
}

resource "helm_release" "istio_ingress" {
  name       = "istio-ingress"
  repository = "https://istio-release.storage.googleapis.com/charts"
  chart      = "gateway"
  namespace  = kubernetes_namespace.istio_system.metadata[0].name
  version    = "1.19.0"
  
  set {
    name  = "service.type"
    value = "LoadBalancer"
  }
  
  depends_on = [helm_release.istiod]
}

# ============================================
# 6. MONITORING STACK (PROMETHEUS + GRAFANA)
# ============================================

# Prometheus Stack
resource "kubernetes_namespace" "monitoring" {
  metadata {
    name = "monitoring"
  }
}

resource "helm_release" "kube_prometheus_stack" {
  name       = "kube-prometheus-stack"
  repository = "https://prometheus-community.github.io/helm-charts"
  chart      = "kube-prometheus-stack"
  namespace  = kubernetes_namespace.monitoring.metadata[0].name
  version    = "48.1.1"
  
  values = [templatefile("${path.module}/templates/prometheus-values.yaml", {
    retention_days = var.prometheus_retention_days
    environment    = var.environment
  })]
  
  set {
    name  = "grafana.adminPassword"
    value = "diyapp-admin-${var.environment}"
  }
  
  set {
    name  = "prometheus.prometheusSpec.serviceMonitorSelectorNilUsesHelmValues"
    value = "false"
  }
  
  set {
    name  = "prometheus.prometheusSpec.podMonitorSelectorNilUsesHelmValues"
    value = "false"
  }
}

# ============================================
# 7. SLO MONITORING & ALERTING
# ============================================

# SLO Configuration for DIYAPP
resource "kubernetes_config_map" "slo_rules" {
  metadata {
    name      = "slo-rules"
    namespace = kubernetes_namespace.monitoring.metadata[0].name
  }
  
  data = {
    "slo-rules.yaml" = <<-EOT
    groups:
      - name: diyapp-slos
        rules:
          # Availability SLO: 99.9%
          - record: slo:diyapp_availability:ratio
            expr: |
              sum(rate(http_requests_total{status!~"5..",job="diyapp-api"}[5m]))
              /
              sum(rate(http_requests_total{job="diyapp-api"}[5m]))
          
          # Latency SLO: P95 < 300ms
          - record: slo:diyapp_latency_p95:histogram_quantile
            expr: |
              histogram_quantile(0.95,
                sum(rate(http_request_duration_seconds_bucket{job="diyapp-api"}[5m]))
                by (le)
              )
          
          # Error Rate SLO: < 0.1%
          - record: slo:diyapp_error_rate:ratio
            expr: |
              sum(rate(http_requests_total{status=~"5..",job="diyapp-api"}[5m]))
              /
              sum(rate(http_requests_total{job="diyapp-api"}[5m]))
          
          # LLM Latency SLO: P95 < 8s
          - record: slo:diyapp_llm_latency_p95:histogram_quantile
            expr: |
              histogram_quantile(0.95,
                sum(rate(llm_request_duration_seconds_bucket{job="diyapp-llm"}[5m]))
                by (le)
              )
    EOT
  }
  
  depends_on = [helm_release.kube_prometheus_stack]
}

# Alert Rules based on Error Budget
resource "kubernetes_config_map" "alert_rules" {
  metadata {
    name      = "alert-rules"
    namespace = kubernetes_namespace.monitoring.metadata[0].name
  }
  
  data = {
    "alert-rules.yaml" = <<-EOT
    groups:
      - name: diyapp-error-budget
        rules:
          # Error Budget Burn Rate alerts
          - alert: ErrorBudgetBurnRateCritical
            expr: |
              (
                (1 - slo:diyapp_availability:ratio)
                / (1 - 0.999)
              ) > 14
            for: 5m
            labels:
              severity: critical
              squad: sre
            annotations:
              summary: "Critical error budget burn rate for DIYAPP"
              description: "Error budget is burning 14x faster than allowed. Current availability: {{ $value | humanizePercentage }}"
          
          - alert: ErrorBudgetBurnRateWarning
            expr: |
              (
                (1 - slo:diyapp_availability:ratio)
                / (1 - 0.999)
              ) > 7
            for: 15m
            labels:
              severity: warning
              squad: sre
            annotations:
              summary: "Warning error budget burn rate for DIYAPP"
              description: "Error budget is burning 7x faster than allowed. Current availability: {{ $value | humanizePercentage }}"
          
          # Latency SLO Alert
          - alert: APILatencySLOViolation
            expr: |
              slo:diyapp_latency_p95:histogram_quantile > 0.3
            for: 10m
            labels:
              severity: warning
              squad: sre
            annotations:
              summary: "API Latency SLO violation"
              description: "P95 latency is {{ $value }}s (SLO: <0.3s)"
          
          # LLM Latency Alert
          - alert: LLMLatencySLOViolation
            expr: |
              slo:diyapp_llm_latency_p95:histogram_quantile > 8
            for: 5m
            labels:
              severity: warning
              squad: sre
            annotations:
              summary: "LLM Latency SLO violation"
              description: "LLM P95 latency is {{ $value }}s (SLO: <8s)"
          
          # Error Rate Alert
          - alert: ErrorRateSLOViolation
            expr: |
              slo:diyapp_error_rate:ratio > 0.001
            for: 5m
            labels:
              severity: warning
              squad: sre
            annotations:
              summary: "Error Rate SLO violation"
              description: "Error rate is {{ $value | humanizePercentage }} (SLO: <0.1%)"
    EOT
  }
  
  depends_on = [helm_release.kube_prometheus_stack]
}
